{ĀpŚS, 1, 1}
athāto darśapūrṇamāsau vyākhyāsyāmaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 1, 1 1.1]
prātar agnihotraṃ hutvānyam āhavanīyaṃ praṇīyāgnīn anvādadhāti | [ĀpŚS, 1, 1 2.1]
na gataśriyo 'nyam agniṃ praṇayati | [ĀpŚS, 1, 1 3.1]
devā gātuvido gātuṃ yajñāya vindata | [ĀpŚS, 1, 1 4.1]
manasaspatinā devena vātād yajñaḥ prayujyatām iti japitvā mamāgne varco vihaveṣv astv ity āhavanīyam upasaminddhe | [ĀpŚS, 1, 1 4.2]
uttarayā gārhapatyam uttarayānvāhāryapacanam | [ĀpŚS, 1, 1 4.3]
tisṛbhistisṛbhir vā | [ĀpŚS, 1, 1 5.1]
uttamāṃ tu japed āhavanīye vādadhyāt | [ĀpŚS, 1, 1 6.1]
vyāhṛtībhir anvādhānam eke samāmananti | [ĀpŚS, 1, 1 7.1]
saṃnayataḥ palāśaśākhāṃ śamīśākhāṃ vāharati bahuparṇāṃ bahuśākhām apratiśuṣkāgrām asuṣirām | [ĀpŚS, 1, 1 8.1]
yaṃ kāmayetāpaśuḥ syād ity aparṇāṃ tasmai śuṣkāgrām āhared apaśur eva bhavati | [ĀpŚS, 1, 1 9.1]
yaṃ kāmayeta paśumān syād iti bahuparṇāṃ tasmai bahuśākhām āharet paśumantam evainaṃ karotīti vijñāyate | [ĀpŚS, 1, 1 9.2]
sā yā prācy udīcī prāgudīcī vā bhavatīṣe tvorje tveti tām ācchinatti | [ĀpŚS, 1, 1 10.1]
api veṣe tvety ācchinatty ūrje tveti saṃnamayaty anumārṣṭi vā | [ĀpŚS, 1, 1 11.1]
{ĀpŚS, 1, 2}
imāṃ prācīm udīcīm iṣam ūrjam abhisaṃskṛtāṃ bahuparṇām aśuṣkāgrāṃ harāmi paśupām aham ity āharati | [ĀpŚS, 1, 2 1.1]
vāyava sthopāyava stheti tayā ṣaḍavarārdhyān vatsān apākaroti | [ĀpŚS, 1, 2 2.1]
darbhair darbhapuñjīlair vā | [ĀpŚS, 1, 2 3.1]
devo vaḥ savitā prārpayatv iti śākhayā gocarāya gāḥ prasthāpayati | [ĀpŚS, 1, 2 4.1]
prasthitānām ekāṃ śākhayopaspṛśati darbhair darbhapuñjīlair vā | [ĀpŚS, 1, 2 5.1]
āpyāyadhvam aghniyā indrāya devabhāgam ity eke samāmananti | [ĀpŚS, 1, 2 6.1]
mahendrāyety eke | [ĀpŚS, 1, 2 6.2]
indraṃ nigameṣūpalakṣayed indrayājino mahendraṃ mahendrayājinaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 1, 2 7.1]
śuddhā apaḥ suprapāṇe pibantīḥ śatam indrāya śarado duhānāḥ | [ĀpŚS, 1, 2 8.1]
rudrasya hetiḥ pari vo vṛṇaktv iti prasthitā anumantrayate | [ĀpŚS, 1, 2 8.2]
dhruvā asmin gopatau syāta bahvīr iti yajamānasya gṛhān abhiparyāvartate | [ĀpŚS, 1, 2 9.1]
yajamānasya paśūn pāhīty agniṣṭhe 'nasy agnyagāre vā purastātpratīcīṃ śākhām upagūhati paścātprācīṃ vā | [ĀpŚS, 1, 2 10.1]
yo vā adhvaryor gṛhān veda gṛhavān bhavati | [ĀpŚS, 1, 2 11.1]
ā caturthāt karmaṇo 'bhisamīkṣetedaṃ kariṣyāmīdaṃ kariṣyāmīty ete vā adhvaryor gṛhāḥ | [ĀpŚS, 1, 2 11.2]
ya evaṃ veda gṛhavān bhavatīti vijñāyate | [ĀpŚS, 1, 2 11.3]
{ĀpŚS, 1, 3}
uttareṇa gārhapatyam asido 'śvaparśur anaḍutparśur vā nihitā | [ĀpŚS, 1, 3 1.1]
devasya tvā savituḥ prasava ity asidam aśvaparśuṃ vādatte tūṣṇīm anaḍutparśum | [ĀpŚS, 1, 3 2.1]
yajñasya ghoṣad asīti gārhapatyam abhimantrya pratyuṣṭaṃ rakṣaḥ pratyuṣṭā arātaya ity āhavanīye gārhapatye vāsidaṃ pratitapati | [ĀpŚS, 1, 3 3.1]
na parśum | [ĀpŚS, 1, 3 4.1]
preyam agād ity uktvorv antarikṣam anvihīti prācīm udīcīṃ vā diśam abhipravrajya yataḥ kutaścid darbhamayaṃ barhir āharati | [ĀpŚS, 1, 3 5.1]
devānāṃ pariṣūtam asīti darbhān pariṣauti | [ĀpŚS, 1, 3 6.1]
viṣṇo stūpo 'sīty abhipretānām ekaṃ stambam utsṛjati | [ĀpŚS, 1, 3 7.1]
ekaṃ vā stambaṃ pariṣūya taṃ sarvaṃ dāti | [ĀpŚS, 1, 3 8.1]
atisṛṣṭo gavāṃ bhāga iti vaikāṃ dve tisro vā nāḍīr utsṛjati | [ĀpŚS, 1, 3 9.1]
idaṃ devānām iti pariṣūtān abhimṛśati | [ĀpŚS, 1, 3 10.1]
idaṃ paśūnām ity atisṛṣṭān | [ĀpŚS, 1, 3 10.2]
devasya tvā savituḥ prasave 'śvinor bāhubhyāṃ pūṣṇo hastābhyāṃ barhir devasadanam ārabha iti viśākheṣu darbhān ārabhate | [ĀpŚS, 1, 3 11.1]
devabarhir mā tvānvaṅ mā tiryag iti saṃyacchati | [ĀpŚS, 1, 3 12.1]
parva te rādhyāsam ity asidam adhinidadhāti | [ĀpŚS, 1, 3 13.1]
ācchettā te mā riṣam ity ācchinatti | [ĀpŚS, 1, 3 14.1]
saṃnakhaṃ muṣṭiṃ lunoti | [ĀpŚS, 1, 3 15.1]
sa prastaraḥ | [ĀpŚS, 1, 3 16.1]
kulmimātro 'ratniḥ prādeśa ūrvasthi jānvasthi srugdaṇḍa iti vā tiryakpramāṇāni | [ĀpŚS, 1, 3 17.1]
{ĀpŚS, 1, 4}
pṛthivyāḥ saṃpṛcaḥ pāhīty anadho nidadhāti | [ĀpŚS, 1, 4 1.1]
ayujo muṣṭīṃl lunoti | [ĀpŚS, 1, 4 2.1]
tathā nidhanāni | [ĀpŚS, 1, 4 3.1]
teṣāṃ prastaro 'yugartha ity eke | [ĀpŚS, 1, 4 4.1]
prastare yāthākāmī | [ĀpŚS, 1, 4 5.1]
yad anyat pariṣavaṇād utsarjanāc ca tat sarvatrāvartate | [ĀpŚS, 1, 4 6.1]
prastaram eva mantreṇa dāti tūṣṇīm itarad iti vājasaneyakam | [ĀpŚS, 1, 4 7.1]
sarvaṃ lutvā devabarhiḥ śatavalśaṃ virohety ālavān abhimṛśati | [ĀpŚS, 1, 4 8.1]
sahasravalśā vi vayaṃ ruhemety ātmānam | [ĀpŚS, 1, 4 9.1]
adityai rāsnāsīti tridhātu pañcadhātu vā śulbaṃ karoti | [ĀpŚS, 1, 4 10.1]
ayupitā yonir iti pratidadhāti | [ĀpŚS, 1, 4 11.1]
adityai rāsnāsīty udagagraṃ vitatya susaṃbhṛtā tvā saṃbharāmīti tasmin nidhanāni saṃbhṛtyālubhitā yonir ity uttame nidhane prastaram atyādhāyendrāṇyai saṃnahanam iti saṃnahyati | [ĀpŚS, 1, 4 12.1]
pūṣā te granthiṃ grathnātv iti granthiṃ karoti | [ĀpŚS, 1, 4 13.1]
sa te māsthād iti purastātpratyañcaṃ granthim upagūhati paścāt prāñcaṃ vā | [ĀpŚS, 1, 4 14.1]
āpas tvām aśvinau tvām ṛṣayaḥ sapta māmṛjuḥ | [ĀpŚS, 1, 4 15.1]
barhiḥ sūryasya raśmibhir uṣasāṃ ketum ārabha iti barhir ārabhate | [ĀpŚS, 1, 4 15.2]
indrasya tvā bāhubhyām udyaccha ity udyacchate | [ĀpŚS, 1, 4 15.3]
bṛhaspater mūrdhnā harāmīti śīrṣann adhinidhatte | [ĀpŚS, 1, 4 15.4]
{ĀpŚS, 1, 5}
{ĀpŚS, 6, 1}
agnihotraṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 1 1.1]
adhivṛkṣasūrya āviḥsūrye vā dhṛṣṭir asi brahma yacchety upaveṣam ādāya gārhapatyam abhimantrayate sugārhapatya iti | [ĀpŚS, 6, 1 2.1]
athainaṃ bodhayaty udbudhyasvāgne prati jāgṛhy enam iṣṭāpūrte saṃsṛjethām ayaṃ ca | [ĀpŚS, 6, 1 3.1]
asmin sadhasthe adhy uttarasmin viśve devā yajamānaś ca sīdateti | [ĀpŚS, 6, 1 3.2]
uddharety eva sāyam āha yajamānaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 1 4.1]
uddhareti prātaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 1 4.2]
sahasraṃ tena kāmadugho 'varunddhe | [ĀpŚS, 6, 1 5.1]
vācā tvā hotrā prāṇenodgātrā cakṣuṣādhvaryuṇā manasā brahmaṇā śrotreṇāgnīdhaitais tvā pañcabhir daivyair ṛtvigbhir uddharāmīti gārhapatyād āhavanīyaṃ jvalantam uddharati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 1 6.1]
bhūr bhuvaḥ suvar uddhriyamāṇa uddhara pāpmano mā yad avidvān yac ca vidvāṃś cakāra | [ĀpŚS, 6, 1 7.1]
ahnā yad enaḥ kṛtam asti pāpaṃ sarvasmān moddhṛto muñca tasmād ity uddhriyamāṇam abhimantrayate yajamānaḥ sāyam | [ĀpŚS, 6, 1 7.2]
rātryā yad enaḥ kṛtam asti pāpaṃ sarvasmān moddhṛto muñca tasmād iti prātaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 1 7.3]
agnipataye 'gnaye me viddhy agnipataye 'gnaye me mṛḍa | [ĀpŚS, 6, 1 8.1]
amṛtāhutim amṛtāyāṃ juhomy agniṃ pṛthivyām amṛtasya jityai | [ĀpŚS, 6, 1 8.2]
tayānantaṃ kāmam ahaṃ jayāni prajāpatir yaṃ prathamo jigāyāgnim agnau svāhā | [ĀpŚS, 6, 1 8.3]
{ĀpŚS, 6, 2}
agne samrāḍ ajaikapād āhavanīya divaḥ pṛthivyāḥ paryantarikṣāllokaṃ vinda yajamānāya | [ĀpŚS, 6, 2 1.1]
pṛthivyās tvā mūrdhan sādayāmi yajñiye loke | [ĀpŚS, 6, 2 1.2]
yo no agne niṣṭyo yo 'niṣṭyo 'bhidāsatīdam ahaṃ taṃ tvayābhinidadhāmīti purastāt parikramyodaṅmukhaḥ pratyaṅmukho vā sāyam āyatane 'gniṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 2 1.3]
prāṅmukhaḥ prātaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 2 1.4]
svayaṃ yajamāna idhmān āharati viśvadānīm ābharanto nātureṇa manasā | [ĀpŚS, 6, 2 2.1]
agne mā te prativeśā riṣāmety etayā | [ĀpŚS, 6, 2 2.2]
yad agne yāni kāni cety etābhiḥ pañcabhiḥ pratimantram agniṣu mahata idhmān ādadhāti | [ĀpŚS, 6, 2 3.1]
āhavanīye varṣiṣṭham | [ĀpŚS, 6, 2 4.1]
yathāhitās tenānupūrvyeṇāhavanīyād vā prakramya | [ĀpŚS, 6, 2 5.1]
tathāgnir ādheyo yathāhutir na vyaveyāt | [ĀpŚS, 6, 2 6.1]
nāntarāgnī saṃcarati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 2 7.1]
yadi pūrvo 'nugataḥ saṃcaryam | [ĀpŚS, 6, 2 8.1]
paścāddhi sa tarhi gataḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 2 9.1]
kāmaṃ hute saṃcaryam ity eke | [ĀpŚS, 6, 2 10.1]
naktam āhavanīyaṃ dhārayati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 2 11.1]
nityo gataśriyo dhriyate | [ĀpŚS, 6, 2 12.1]
nityaṃ gārhapatyam | [ĀpŚS, 6, 2 13.1]
tathānvāhāryapacanaṃ yadi mathitvāhito bhavati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 2 14.1]
yady āhāryo 'harahar enaṃ dakṣiṇata āharanti | [ĀpŚS, 6, 2 15.1]
upavasatha evainam āhareyur navāvasāna evainam āhareyur iti vājasaneyakam | [ĀpŚS, 6, 2 16.1]
{ĀpŚS, 6, 3}
parisamūhanenāgnīn alaṃkurvanti | [ĀpŚS, 6, 3 1.1]
purastād alaṃkārāḥ sāyam upariṣṭād alaṃkārāḥ prātaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 3 2.1]
etad vā viparītam | [ĀpŚS, 6, 3 3.1]
ubhayato 'laṃkārāḥ sāyaṃ tathā prātar ity eke | [ĀpŚS, 6, 3 3.2]
agne gṛhapate śundhasveti gārhapatyam agne vahne śundhasveti dakṣiṇāgnim agne samrāṭ śundhasvety āhavanīyam agne sabhya śundhasveti sabhyam agne pariṣadya śundhasvety āvasathyam | [ĀpŚS, 6, 3 4.1]
udagagraiḥ prāgagraiś ca darbhais tṛṇair vāgnīn paristṛṇāty agnim agnī vā | [ĀpŚS, 6, 3 5.1]
khādiraḥ sruvo vaikaṅkaty agnihotrahavaṇī bāhumātry aratnimātrī vā | [ĀpŚS, 6, 3 6.1]
prasṛtākṛtir āryakṛtāgnihotrasthāly ūrdhvakapālācakravartā bhavati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 3 7.1]
dakṣiṇena vihāram agnihotrī tiṣṭhati tāṃ yajamāno 'bhimantrayata iḍāsi vratabhṛd ahaṃ nāv ubhayor vrataṃ cariṣyāmi surohiṇy ahaṃ nāv ubhayor vrataṃ cariṣyāmīḍa ehi mayi śrayasvera ehy adita ehi gaur ehi śraddha ehi satyena tvāhvayāmīti | [ĀpŚS, 6, 3 8.1]
atha vedideśam abhimṛśatīyam asi tasyās te 'gnir vatsaḥ sā me svargaṃ ca lokam amṛtaṃ ca dhukṣveti | [ĀpŚS, 6, 3 9.1]
pūṣāsīti dakṣiṇato vatsam upasṛjya prācīm āvṛtya dogdhy udīcīṃ prācīm udīcīṃ vā | [ĀpŚS, 6, 3 10.1]
na śūdro duhyāt | [ĀpŚS, 6, 3 11.1]
asato vā eṣa sambhūto yacchūdraḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 3 12.1]
duhyād vā | [ĀpŚS, 6, 3 13.1]
yad eva gārhapatye 'dhiśrayati pavayaty evainat | [ĀpŚS, 6, 3 14.1]
agnihotrasthālyā dohanena ca dogdhi | [ĀpŚS, 6, 3 15.1]
{ĀpŚS, 6, 4}
pūrvau duhyāj jyeṣṭhasya jyaiṣṭhineyasya yo vā gataśrīḥ syāt | [ĀpŚS, 6, 4 1.1]
aparau duhyāt kaniṣṭhasya kāniṣṭhineyasya yo vānujāvaro yo vā bubhūṣet | [ĀpŚS, 6, 4 1.2]
na stanān saṃmṛśati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 4 2.1]
yathopalambhaṃ nitye kalpe dogdhi | [ĀpŚS, 6, 4 3.1]
pūrvavad upasṛṣṭāṃ duhyamānāṃ dhārāghoṣaṃ ca yajamāno 'numantrayate | [ĀpŚS, 6, 4 4.1]
astamite dogdhi | [ĀpŚS, 6, 4 5.1]
amnar astamite hotavyam | [ĀpŚS, 6, 4 6.1]
samudro vā eṣa yad ahorātras tasyaite gādhe tīrthe yat saṃdhī tasmāt saṃdhau hotavyam iti śailālibrāhmaṇaṃ bhavati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 4 7.1]
nakṣatraṃ dṛṣṭvā pradoṣe niśāyāṃ vā sāyam | [ĀpŚS, 6, 4 8.1]
uṣasy upodayaṃ samayāviṣita udite vā prātaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 4 9.1]
yad udite juhoty agniṣṭomaṃ tenāvarunddhe yan madhyaṃdine juhoty ukthyaṃ tenāvarunddhe yad aparāhṇe juhoti ṣoḍaśinaṃ tenāvarunddhe yat pūrvarātre juhoti prathamaṃ tena rātriparyāyam āpnoti yan madhyarātre juhoti madhyamaṃ tena rātriparyāyam āpnoti yad apararātre juhoti jaghanyaṃ tena rātriparyāyam āpnoti | [ĀpŚS, 6, 4 10.1]
sa na manyeta sarveṣv eteṣu kāleṣu hotavyam āpadi hutam ity eva pratīyād iti vijñāyate | [ĀpŚS, 6, 4 11.1]
yo homakālaḥ so 'ṅgānām | [ĀpŚS, 6, 4 12.1]
{ĀpŚS, 6, 5}
patnīvad asyāgnihotraṃ bhavati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 5 1.1]
sva āyatane patny upaviśati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 5 2.1]
apareṇāhavanīyaṃ dakṣiṇātikramyopaviśya yajamāno vidyud asi vidya me pāpmānam ṛtāt satyam upaimi mayi śraddhety apa ācāmati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 5 3.1]
ṛtaṃ tvā satyena pariṣiñcāmīti sāyaṃ pariṣiñcati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 5 4.1]
satyaṃ tvartena pariṣiñcāmīti prātaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 5 4.2]
āhavanīyam agre 'tha gārhapatyam atha dakṣiṇāgnim api vā gārhapatyam āhavanīyaṃ dakṣiṇāgniṃ yathā vāhitāḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 5 4.3]
yajñasya saṃtatir asi yajñasya tvā saṃtatim anusaṃtanomīti gārhapatyāt prakramya saṃtatām udakadhārāṃ srāvayaty āhavanīyāt | [ĀpŚS, 6, 5 5.1]
dhṛṣṭir asi brahma yacchety upaveṣam ādāya bhūtakṛta sthāpoḍhaṃ janyaṃ bhayam apoḍhāḥ senā abhītvarīr iti gārhapatyād udīco 'ṅgārān nirūhya vyantān gārhapatyena kṛtvā sagarā sthety abhimantrya japaty agnaya ādityaṃ gṛhṇāmy ahne rātrim iti sāyam | [ĀpŚS, 6, 5 6.1]
ādityāyāgniṃ gṛhṇāmi rātryā ahar iti prātaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 5 6.2]
iḍāyāḥ padaṃ ghṛtavac carācaraṃ jātavedo havir idaṃ juṣasva | [ĀpŚS, 6, 5 7.1]
ye grāmyāḥ paśavo viśvarūpā virūpās teṣāṃ saptānām iha rantir astu | [ĀpŚS, 6, 5 7.2]
rāyaspoṣāya suprajāstvāya suvīryāyeti teṣv agnihotram adhiśrayati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 5 7.3]
{ĀpŚS, 6, 6}
reto vā agnihotram | [ĀpŚS, 6, 6 1.1]
na suśṛtaṃ kuryād retaḥ kūlayen no 'śṛtam antarevaiva syāt | [ĀpŚS, 6, 6 1.2]
samudantaṃ hotavyam | [ĀpŚS, 6, 6 2.1]
udantīkṛtya pratiṣicyam | [ĀpŚS, 6, 6 3.1]
apratiṣekyaṃ syāt tejaskāmasya brahmavarcasakāmasya pāpmānaṃ tustūrṣamāṇasyātho sarvebhyaḥ kāmebhyo 'tho yaḥ kāmayeta vīro ma ājāyeteti | [ĀpŚS, 6, 6 4.1]
amnar adhiśritaṃ vā | [ĀpŚS, 6, 6 5.1]
adabdhena tvā cakṣuṣāvekṣa iti tṛṇena jvalatāvekṣate | [ĀpŚS, 6, 6 6.1]
dohanasaṃkṣālanaṃ sruva ānīya haras te mā vinaiṣam iti tena pratiṣiñcaty apāṃ vā stokena | [ĀpŚS, 6, 6 7.1]
udbhava sthodahaṃ prajayā pra paśubhir bhūyāsaṃ haras te mā vigād udyan suvargo lokas triṣu lokeṣu rocayeti punar evāvekṣyāntaritaṃ rakṣo 'ntaritā arātayo 'pahatā vyṛddhir apahataṃ pāpaṃ karmāpahataṃ pāpasya pāpakṛtaḥ pāpaṃ karma yo naḥ pāpaṃ karma cikīrṣati pratyag enam ṛccheti triḥ paryagnikṛtvā gharmo 'si rāyaspoṣavanir ihorjaṃ dṛṃheti vartma kurvan prāg udvāsayaty udak prāgudag vā | [ĀpŚS, 6, 6 8.1]
na vartma karotīty eke | [ĀpŚS, 6, 6 9.1]
iha prajāṃ paśūn dṛṃheti trir bhūmau pratiṣṭhāpya subhūtakṛta stha pratyūḍhaṃ janyaṃ bhayaṃ pratyūḍhāḥ senā abhītvarīr iti gārhapatye 'ṅgārān pratyūhya | [ĀpŚS, 6, 6 10.1]
{ĀpŚS, 6, 7}
devasya tvā savituḥ prasava iti sruksruvam ādāya pratyuṣṭaṃ rakṣaḥ pratyuṣṭā arātaya ity āhavanīye gārhapatye vā pratitapyāriṣṭo yajamānaḥ patnī ceti saṃmṛśya hiraṇyayaṣṭir asy amṛtapalāśā sroto yajñānām ity agnihotrahavaṇīm abhimantryom unneṣyāmi havyaṃ devebhyaḥ pāpmano yajamānam iti sāyam āha | [ĀpŚS, 6, 7 1.1]
om unnayāmīti prātaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 7 1.2]
havir devānām asi mṛtyor me 'bhayaṃ svasti me 'stv abhayaṃ me astv ity upāṃśūktvom unnayety uccair anujānāti | [ĀpŚS, 6, 7 2.1]
apacāre yajamānasya svayam ātmānam anujānīyāt | [ĀpŚS, 6, 7 2.2]
unnīyamāna ubhau vācaṃ yacchata ā homāt | [ĀpŚS, 6, 7 3.1]
na cābhimīlate tiṣṭhati ca yajamānaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 7 4.1]
unnīta upaviśati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 7 5.1]
catur unnayati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 7 6.1]
yaṃ kāmayeta putrāṇām ayam ṛdhnuyād iti taṃ prati pūrṇam unnayet | [ĀpŚS, 6, 7 7.1]
yadi kāmayeta jyeṣṭhato 'sya prajārdhukā syād iti pūrṇaṃ prathamam unnayet tata ūnataramūnataram | [ĀpŚS, 6, 7 8.1]
kaniṣṭhata ity etad viparītam | [ĀpŚS, 6, 7 8.2]
sarve samāvadvīryā iti samam | [ĀpŚS, 6, 7 8.3]
yathopalambhaṃ nitye kalpa unnayati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 7 9.1]
{ĀpŚS, 6, 8}
agnaye ca tvā pṛthivyai connayāmīti prathamaṃ vāyave ca tvāntarikṣāya ceti dvitīyaṃ sūryāya ca tvā dive ceti tṛtīyaṃ candramase ca tvā nakṣatrebhyaś ceti caturtham | [ĀpŚS, 6, 8 1.1]
adbhyaś ca tvauṣadhībhyaś ceti pañcamaṃ jamadagnīnām | [ĀpŚS, 6, 8 2.1]
bhūr iḍā bhuva iḍā suvar iḍā karad iḍā pṛthag iḍeti vā pratimantram | [ĀpŚS, 6, 8 3.1]
paśūn me yacchety apareṇa gārhapatyam unnayanadeśe 'bhitarāṃ vā sādayitvā gārhapatye hastaṃ pratāpya saṃmṛśati sajūr devaiḥ sāyaṃyāvabhiḥ sāyaṃyāvāno devāḥ svasti saṃpārayantu paśubhiḥ saṃpṛcīya prajāṃ dṛṃheti sāyam | [ĀpŚS, 6, 8 4.1]
sajūr devaiḥ prātaryāvabhiḥ prātaryāvāṇo devāḥ svasti saṃpārayantu paśubhiḥ saṃpṛcīya prajāṃ dṛṃheti prātaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 8 4.2]
daśahotrā cābhimṛśya pālāśīṃ samidhaṃ prādeśamātrīm upari dhārayan gārhapatyasya samayārcir harati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 8 5.1]
urv antarikṣaṃ vīhīty uddravati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 8 6.1]
uddravan daśahotāraṃ vyācaṣṭe | [ĀpŚS, 6, 8 7.1]
samaṃ prāṇair harati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 8 8.1]
svāhāgnaye vaiśvānarāyeti madhyadeśe niyacchati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 8 9.1]
vātāya tvety udgṛhṇāti | [ĀpŚS, 6, 8 10.1]
upa preta saṃyatadhvaṃ māntargāta bhāginaṃ bhāgadheyāt saptarṣīṇāṃ sukṛtāṃ yatra lokas tatremaṃ yajñaṃ yajamānaṃ ca dhehy upa pratnam upa bhūr bhuvaḥ suvar āyur me yacchety apareṇāhavanīyaṃ darbheṣu sādayati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 8 11.1]
{ĀpŚS, 6, 9}
yasyāgnāv uddhriyamāṇe hūyate vasuṣu hutaṃ bhavati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 9 1.1]
nihito dhūpāyañchete rudreṣu | [ĀpŚS, 6, 9 1.2]
prathamam idhmam arcir ālabhata ādityeṣu | [ĀpŚS, 6, 9 1.3]
sarva eva sarvaśa idhma ādīpto bhavati viśveṣu deveṣu | [ĀpŚS, 6, 9 1.4]
nitarām arcir upāvaiti lohinīkeva bhavatīndre hutaṃ bhavati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 9 1.5]
aṅgārā bhavanti tebhyo 'ṅgārebhyo 'rcir udeti prajāpatāv eva | [ĀpŚS, 6, 9 1.6]
śaro 'ṅgārā adhyūhante tato nīlopakāśo 'rcir udeti brahmaṇi hutaṃ bhavati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 9 1.7]
yad aṅgāreṣu vyavaśānteṣu lelāyad vīva bhāti tad devānām āsyaṃ tasmāt tathā hotavyaṃ yathāsye 'pidadhāty evaṃ tad iti vijñāyate | [ĀpŚS, 6, 9 2.1]
vidyud asi vidya me pāpmānam ṛtāt satyam upaimīti hoṣyann apa upaspṛśya pālāśīṃ samidham ādadhāty ekāṃ dve tisro vā | [ĀpŚS, 6, 9 3.1]
eṣā te agne samid iti | [ĀpŚS, 6, 9 4.1]
hiraṇyayaṃ tvā vaṃśaṃ svargasya lokasya saṃkramaṇaṃ dadhāmīti dvitīyām | [ĀpŚS, 6, 9 4.2]
rajatāṃ tvā haritagarbhām agnijyotiṣam akṣitiṃ kāmadughāṃ svargyāṃ svargāya lokāya rātrim iṣṭakām upadadhe tayā devatayāṅgirasvad dhruvā sīdeti sāyaṃ tṛtīyām | [ĀpŚS, 6, 9 4.3]
hariṇīṃ tvā rajatagarbhāṃ sūryajyotiṣam akṣitiṃ kāmadughāṃ svargyāṃ svargāya lokāyāhar iṣṭakām upadadha iti prātaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 9 4.4]
{ĀpŚS, 6, 10}
samidham ādhāya prāṇyāpānya nimīlya vīkṣya hutvā dhyāyed yat kāmaḥ syāt | [ĀpŚS, 6, 10 1.1]
hutvā mahad abhivīkṣate | [ĀpŚS, 6, 10 2.1]
ādīptāyāṃ juhoti śyāvāyāṃ vā yadā vā samatītārcir lelāyatīva | [ĀpŚS, 6, 10 3.1]
dhūpāyatyāṃ grāmakāmasya jvalatyāṃ brahmavarcasakāmasyāṅgāreṣu tejaskāmasya | [ĀpŚS, 6, 10 3.2]
dvyaṅgule mūlāt samidham abhijuhoti | [ĀpŚS, 6, 10 4.1]
abhikrāmaṃ sāyaṃ juhoty avakrāmaṃ prātaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 10 5.1]
ubhayatra vābhikrāmam | [ĀpŚS, 6, 10 6.1]
bhūr bhuvaḥ suvar iti hoṣyañ japati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 10 7.1]
agnir jyotir jyotir agniḥ svāheti sāyam agnihotraṃ juhoti | [ĀpŚS, 6, 10 8.1]
sūryo jyotir jyotiḥ sūryaḥ svāheti prātaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 10 8.2]
saṃsṛṣṭahomaṃ vāgnir jyotir jyotiḥ sūryaḥ svāheti sāyaṃ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 10 9.1]
sūryo jyotir jyotir agniḥ svāheti prātaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 10 9.2]
iṣe tveti sruṅmukhād avācīnaṃ sāyaṃ lepam avamārṣṭy ūrje tveti | [ĀpŚS, 6, 10 10.1]
ūrdhvaṃ prātaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 10 10.2]
oṣadhībhyas tvauṣadhīr jinveti barhiṣi lepaṃ nimṛjya varco me yaccheti srucaṃ sādayitvāgne gṛhapate mā mā saṃtāpsīr ātmann amṛtam adhiṣi prajā jyotir adabdhena tvā cakṣuṣā pratīkṣa iti gārhapatyaṃ pratīkṣya bhūr bhuvaḥ suvar ity uttarām āhutiṃ pūrvārdhe samidhi juhoti tūṣṇīṃ vā | [ĀpŚS, 6, 10 11.1]
na samid abhihotavā ity eke | [ĀpŚS, 6, 10 12.1]
{ĀpŚS, 6, 11}
varṣīyasīm uttarām āhutiṃ hutvā bhūyo bhakṣāyāvaśinaṣṭi | [ĀpŚS, 6, 11 1.1]
yaṃ kāmayeta pāpīyān syād iti bhūyas tasya pūrvaṃ hutvottaraṃ kanīyo juhuyāt | [ĀpŚS, 6, 11 2.1]
hutvā srucam udgṛhya rudra mṛḍānārbhava mṛḍa dhūrta namas te astu paśupate trāyasvainam iti triḥ srucāgnim udañcam ativalgayati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 11 3.1]
pūrvaval lepam avamṛjya prācīnāvītī svadhā pitṛbhyaḥ pitṝñ jinveti dakṣiṇena vediṃ bhūmyāṃ lepaṃ nimṛjya prajāṃ me yaccheti srucaṃ sādayitvā vṛṣṭir asi vṛśca me pāpmānam ṛtāt satyam upāgām iti hutvāpa upaspṛśyāntarvedi sruk | [ĀpŚS, 6, 11 4.1]
athāṅgulyāpādāya pūṣāsīti lepaṃ prāśnāty aśabdaṃ kurvann atihāya dataḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 11 4.2]
apa ācamyaivaṃ punaḥ prāśyācamya barhiṣopayamyodaṅṅ āvṛtyotsṛpya garbhebhyas tvā garbhān prīṇīhy āgneyaṃ haviḥ prajananaṃ me astu daśavīraṃ sarvagaṇaṃ svastaye | [ĀpŚS, 6, 11 5.1]
ātmasani prajāsani paśusany abhayasani lokasani vṛṣṭisani | [ĀpŚS, 6, 11 5.2]
agniḥ prajāṃ bahulāṃ me karotv annaṃ payo reto asmāsu dhehi | [ĀpŚS, 6, 11 5.3]
rāyaspoṣam iṣam ūrjam asmāsu dīdharat svāhety udagdaṇḍayā prāgdaṇḍayā vā srucācāmati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 11 5.4]
{ĀpŚS, 6, 12}
sauryaṃ havir iti prātarmantraṃ saṃnamati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 12 1]
dviḥ srucaṃ nirlihyādbhiḥ pūrayitvocchiṣṭabhājo jinveti parācīnaṃ ninīyācamyāgreṇāhavanīyaṃ darbhair agnihotrahavaṇīṃ prakṣālayati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 12 2]
na māṃsadhautasya devā bhuñjata iti vijñāyate | [ĀpŚS, 6, 12 3]
adbhiḥ srucaṃ pūrayitvā sarpebhyas tvā sarpāñ jinveti pratidiśaṃ vyutsicya sarpān pipīlikā jinva sarpetarajanāñ jinva sarpadevajanāñ jinveti tisraḥ sruca utsicya caturthīṃ pūrayitvā pṛthivyām amṛtaṃ juhomi svāhety apareṇāhavanīyaṃ ninīya śeṣaṃ patnyā añjalau gṛhebhyas tvā gṛhāñ jinveti | [ĀpŚS, 6, 12 4]
yadi patnī nānuṣyād devānāṃ patnībhyo 'mṛtaṃ juhomi svāheti patnyāyatane ninayet | [ĀpŚS, 6, 12 5]
aparaṃ srucy ānīya vipruṣāṃ śāntir asīty unnayanadeśe ninīyāhavanīye srucaṃ pratāpya hasto 'vadheyo hasto vā pratāpya srucy avadheyaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 12 6]
tayodag uddiśati saptarṣibhyas tvā saptarṣīñ jinveti | [ĀpŚS, 6, 12 7]
{ĀpŚS, 6, 13}
agne gṛhapate pariṣadya juṣasva svāheti sruveṇa gārhapatye juhoty ekāṃ dve tisraś catasro vā | [ĀpŚS, 6, 13 1.1]
agnaye gṛhapataye rayipataye puṣṭipataye kāmāyānnādyāya svāhety etām eke samāmananti | [ĀpŚS, 6, 13 2.1]
samabhyuccayavad eke | [ĀpŚS, 6, 13 3.1]
agne 'dābhya pariṣadya juṣasva svāheti sruveṇānvāhāryapacane juhoty ekāṃ dve tisraś catasro vā | [ĀpŚS, 6, 13 4.1]
annapate annasya no dehīti dvitīyām | [ĀpŚS, 6, 13 5.1]
aprāśya vāparayor juhuyāt | [ĀpŚS, 6, 13 6.1]
āhavanīye homo nāparayoḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 13 7.1]
yad āhavanīye hutvāparayor juhuyād yathā svargāl lokāt pratyavarohet tādṛk tad iti vijñāyate | [ĀpŚS, 6, 13 8.1]
sarve vā ete homārthā ādhīyante | [ĀpŚS, 6, 13 9.1]
daśa sampadyante | [ĀpŚS, 6, 13 9.2]
daśākṣarā virāḍ virājā yajñaḥ saṃmita iti bahvṛcabrāhmaṇaṃ bhavati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 13 9.3]
dīdihi dīdidāsi dīdāyety eṣo 'gnyupasamindhana āmnātaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 13 10.1]
dīdihi dīdidāsi dīdāya dīdyāsaṃ dīdyasveti vā pratimantram | [ĀpŚS, 6, 13 11.1]
yathāhitās tenānupūrvyeṇāhavanīyād vā prakramya | [ĀpŚS, 6, 13 12.1]
antarvedy apo ninīya | [ĀpŚS, 6, 13 13.1]
{ĀpŚS, 6, 14}
pūrvavad agnīn pariṣiñcati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 14 1.1]
na dhārām | [ĀpŚS, 6, 14 1.2]
apiprer agne svāṃ tanvam ayāḍ dyāvāpṛthivī ūrjam asmāsu dhehīty agnihotrasthālyāṃ tṛṇam aṅktvānupraharati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 14 2.1]
sā hy agnihotrasya saṃsthitiḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 14 3.1]
na barhir anupraharet | [ĀpŚS, 6, 14 4.1]
asaṃsthito vā eṣa yajño yad agnihotram ity uktam | [ĀpŚS, 6, 14 4.2]
agnihotrasthālīṃ prakṣālyākṣitam akṣityai juhomi svāhety unnayanadeśe ninayati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 14 5.1]
antarvedi vā | [ĀpŚS, 6, 14 5.2]
vṛṣṭir asi vṛśca me pāpmānam ṛtāt satyam upāgām apsu śraddhety apa ācamya yajamāno 'ntarvedi mārjayate 'nnādāḥ sthānnādo bhūyāsaṃ yaśaḥ stha yaśasvī bhūyāsaṃ śraddhā stha śraddhiṣīyeti | [ĀpŚS, 6, 14 6.1]
āpo ha śleṣma prathamaṃ saṃbabhūva yena dhṛto varuṇo yena mitraḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 14 7.1]
yenendraṃ devā abhyaṣiñcanta rājyāya tenāhaṃ mām abhiṣiñcāmi varcasa iti śirasy apa ānayate | [ĀpŚS, 6, 14 7.2]
dvayoḥ payasā paśukāmasya juhuyāt | [ĀpŚS, 6, 14 8.1]
agnihotrasthālyā pūrvāṃ dogdhi | [ĀpŚS, 6, 14 9.1]
dohanenottarām | [ĀpŚS, 6, 14 9.2]
adhiśritya pūrvam uttaram ānayati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 14 10.1]
yasya rudraḥ paśūñchamāyetaitayaivāvṛtā dvayoḥ payasā sāyaṃ prātar juhuyāt | [ĀpŚS, 6, 14 11.1]
tac ced atihanyāt sajūr jātavedo diva ā pṛthivyā asya haviṣo ghṛtasya vīhi svāheti sāyaṃ prātar ājyena juhuyāt | [ĀpŚS, 6, 14 12.1]
anāramaty agne duḥśīrtatano juṣasva svāheti dvādaśāham ājyena hutvā tata ūrdhvaṃ na sūrkṣet | [ĀpŚS, 6, 14 13.1]
{ĀpŚS, 6, 15}
payasā paśukāmasya juhuyād dadhnendriyakāmasya yavāgvā grāmakāmasyaudanenānnādyakāmasya taṇḍulair ojaskāmasya | [ĀpŚS, 6, 15 1.1]
balakāmasyety eke | [ĀpŚS, 6, 15 1.2]
māṃsena yaśaskāmasya somena brahmavarcasakāmasyājyena tejaskāmasya | [ĀpŚS, 6, 15 1.3]
pratiṣekaṃ yavāgūṃ śrapayati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 15 2.1]
śṛtāṃ yajuṣā pratiṣiñcati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 15 3.1]
evaṃ māṃsam | [ĀpŚS, 6, 15 4.1]
nājyaṃ pratiṣiñcati haras te mā vinaiṣam iti | [ĀpŚS, 6, 15 5.1]
dve darbhāgre pratyasyaty ekaṃ vā | [ĀpŚS, 6, 15 5.2]
na dadhy adhiśrayati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 15 6.1]
śṛtaṃ hi tan na pratiṣiñcati pratiṣiktaṃ hi tad ātañcaneneti vijñāyate | [ĀpŚS, 6, 15 6.2]
evaṃ taṇḍulān odanaṃ somaṃ ca | [ĀpŚS, 6, 15 7.1]
ājyena taṇḍulair odanena somena vā juhuyād yasyāpratiṣekyaṃ syāt | [ĀpŚS, 6, 15 8.1]
ājyena tejaskāmaḥ saṃvatsaraṃ juhuyād dvādaśāhaṃ vā | [ĀpŚS, 6, 15 9.1]
na rājanyasya juhuyāt | [ĀpŚS, 6, 15 10.1]
homakāle gṛhebhyo brāhmaṇāyānnaṃ prahiṇuyāt teno haivāsya hutaṃ bhavati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 15 11.1]
nityam agnyupasthānaṃ vācayitavyaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 15 12.1]
yo vā somayājī satyavādī tasya juhuyāt | [ĀpŚS, 6, 15 13.1]
ahar ahar yajamānaḥ svayam agnihotraṃ juhuyāt | [ĀpŚS, 6, 15 14.1]
parvaṇi vā | [ĀpŚS, 6, 15 15.1]
brahmacārī vā juhuyād brahmaṇā hi sa parikrīto bhavati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 15 16.1]
kṣīrahotā vā juhuyād dhanena hi sa parikrīto bhavatīti bahvṛcabrāhmaṇam | [ĀpŚS, 6, 15 16.2]
{ĀpŚS, 6, 16}
agnyupasthānaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 16 1.1]
upatiṣṭhata iti codyamāna āhavanīyam evopatiṣṭheta | [ĀpŚS, 6, 16 2.1]
vacanād anyam | [ĀpŚS, 6, 16 2.2]
uttarām āhutim upotthāya kavātiryaṅṅ ivopatiṣṭheta | [ĀpŚS, 6, 16 3.1]
upaprayanto adhvaram iti ṣaḍbhiḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 16 4.1]
agnīṣomāv imaṃ su ma iti saptamyā pūrvapakṣe | [ĀpŚS, 6, 16 5.1]
aindrāgnyā saptamyāparapakṣe | [ĀpŚS, 6, 16 5.2]
dadhikrāvṇo akāriṣam ity ubhayatrāṣṭamyā | [ĀpŚS, 6, 16 6.1]
mamāgne varco vihaveṣv astv iti catasraḥ purastād agnīṣomīyāyāḥ pūrvapakṣe | [ĀpŚS, 6, 16 7.1]
tathaindrāgnyā aparapakṣe | [ĀpŚS, 6, 16 7.2]
agna āyūṃṣi pavasa iti ṣaḍbhiḥ saṃvatsare saṃvatsare sadā vā | [ĀpŚS, 6, 16 8.1]
pavamānahavīṃṣi vā saṃvatsare saṃvatsare nirvaped etāsāṃ sthāne | [ĀpŚS, 6, 16 9.1]
āyurdā agna iti siddham ā citrāvasoḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 16 10.1]
triś citrāvasunā sāyam upatiṣṭhate | [ĀpŚS, 6, 16 11.1]
trir arvāg vasunā prātar arvāg vaso svasti te pāram aśīya | [ĀpŚS, 6, 16 11.2]
indhānās tvā śataṃ himā ity upasthāyendhānās tvā śataṃ himāḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 16 12.1]
agneḥ samid asy abhiśastyā mā pāhi somasya samid asi paraspā ma edhi yamasya samid asi mṛtyor mā pāhīti catasraḥ samidha ekaikasminn ādhāya saṃ tvam agne sūryasya varcasāgathā ity anuvākaśeṣeṇopasthāya vayaṃ soma vrate tava manas tanūṣu bibhrataḥ prajāvanto aśīmahīti mukhaṃ vimṛṣṭe | [ĀpŚS, 6, 16 12.2]
{ĀpŚS, 6, 17}
saṃpaśyāmi prajā aham iti gṛhān prekṣate | [ĀpŚS, 6, 17 1.1]
ambhaḥ sthāmbho vo bhakṣīyeti goṣṭham upatiṣṭhate | [ĀpŚS, 6, 17 2.1]
revatī ramadhvam ity antarāgnī tiṣṭhañ japati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 17 3.1]
saṃhitāsi viśvarūpīr iti vatsam abhimṛśati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 17 4.1]
saṃhitāsi viśvarūpeti vatsām | [ĀpŚS, 6, 17 5.1]
bhuvanam asi sahasrapoṣaṃ puṣeti vā vatsam | [ĀpŚS, 6, 17 6.1]
upa tvāgne dive diva iti tisṛbhir gāyatrībhir gārhapatyam upatiṣṭhate 'gne tvaṃ no antama iti catasṛbhiś ca dvipadābhiḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 17 7.1]
sa no bodhi śrudhī havam uruṣyā ṇo aghāyataḥ samasmād ity eṣā caturthī bhavati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 17 8.1]
ūrjā vaḥ paśyāmy ūrjā mā paśyateti gṛhān prekṣate paśūn vā | [ĀpŚS, 6, 17 9.1]
mahi trīṇām avo 'stu dyukṣaṃ mitrasyāryamṇaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 17 10.1]
durādharṣaṃ varuṇasya | [ĀpŚS, 6, 17 10.2]
nahi teṣām amā cana nādhvasu vāraṇeṣv ā | [ĀpŚS, 6, 17 10.3]
īśe ripur aghaśaṃsaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 17 10.4]
te hi putrāso aditeś chardir yacchanty ajasram | [ĀpŚS, 6, 17 10.5]
vi dāśuṣe vāryāṇīti prājāpatyena tṛcenopatiṣṭhate | [ĀpŚS, 6, 17 10.6]
yaṃ kāmayeta svasti punar āgacched iti tam etābhir anvīkṣeta | [ĀpŚS, 6, 17 11.1]
svasty eva punar āgacchatīty ayajñasaṃyuktaḥ kalpaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 17 11.2]
mā naḥ śaṃso araruṣo dhūrtiḥ praṇaṅ martyasya | [ĀpŚS, 6, 17 12.1]
rakṣā ṇo brahmaṇaspate | [ĀpŚS, 6, 17 12.2]
yo revān yo amīvahā vasuvit puṣṭivardhanaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 17 12.3]
sa naḥ siṣaktu yas turaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 17 12.4]
pari te dūḍabho ratho 'smāṁ aśnotu viśvataḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 17 12.5]
yena rakṣasi dāśuṣaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 17 12.6]
{ĀpŚS, 6, 18}
tat savitur vareṇyaṃ somānaṃ svaraṇaṃ mitrasya carṣaṇīdhṛtaḥ pra sa mitra kadā cana starīr asi kadā cana prayucchasi pari tvāgne puraṃ vayam ity upasthāya | [ĀpŚS, 6, 18 1.1]
nimṛdo 'si ny ahaṃ taṃ mṛdyāsaṃ yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣma iti dakṣiṇasya padaḥ pārṣṇyā nimṛdnīyād yadi pāpīyasā spardheta | [ĀpŚS, 6, 18 2.1]
prabhūr asi prāhaṃ tam abhibhūyāsaṃ yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣma iti dakṣiṇataḥ pado nigṛhṇīyād yadi sadṛśena | [ĀpŚS, 6, 18 2.2]
abhibhūr asy abhy ahaṃ taṃ bhūyāsaṃ yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣma iti prapadena yadi śreyasā | [ĀpŚS, 6, 18 2.3]
pūṣā mā paśupāḥ pātu pūṣā mā pathipāḥ pātu pūṣā mādhipāḥ pātu pūṣā mādhipatiḥ pātv iti lokān upasthāya prācī dig agnir devatāgniṃ sa ṛcchatu yo maitasyai diśo 'bhidāsati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 18 3.1]
dakṣiṇā dig indro devatendraṃ sa ṛcchatu yo maitasyai diśo 'bhidāsati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 18 3.2]
pratīcī dik somo devatā somaṃ sa ṛcchatu yo maitasyai diśo 'bhidāsati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 18 3.3]
udīcī diṅ mitrāvaruṇau devatā mitrāvaruṇau sa ṛcchatu yo maitasyai diśo 'bhidāsati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 18 3.4]
ūrdhvā dig bṛhaspatir devatā bṛhaspatiṃ sa ṛcchatu yo maitasyai diśo 'bhidāsati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 18 3.5]
iyaṃ dig aditir devatāditiṃ sa ṛcchatu yo maitasyai diśo 'bhidāsatīti yathāliṅgaṃ diśa upasthāya | [ĀpŚS, 6, 18 3.6]
{ĀpŚS, 6, 19}
agnīn upasamādhāya dharmo mā dharmaṇaḥ pātu vidharmo mā vidharmaṇaḥ pātv āyuś ca prāyuś ca cakṣuś ca vicakṣuś ca prāṅ cāvāṅ coruga urugasya te vācā vayaṃ saṃ bhaktena gamemahīty upasthāyāgna āyūṃṣi pavasa ity āgnipāvamānībhyāṃ gārhapatyam upatiṣṭhate | [ĀpŚS, 6, 19 1.1]
agne gṛhapata iti ca | [ĀpŚS, 6, 19 2.1]
putrasya nāma gṛhṇāti tām āśiṣam āśāse tantava ity ajātasya | [ĀpŚS, 6, 19 2.2]
amuṣmā iti jātasya | [ĀpŚS, 6, 19 2.3]
yat kiṃcāgnihotrī kāmayeta tad agnīn yāceta | [ĀpŚS, 6, 19 3.1]
upainaṃ tan namatīti vijñāyate | [ĀpŚS, 6, 19 3.2]
upastheyo 'gnī3r nopastheyā3 ity uktam | [ĀpŚS, 6, 19 4.1]
naktam upatiṣṭhate na prātaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 19 5.1]
na prātar agnim upa canāvarohen na prātar āhitāgniś cana manyeteti vājasaneyakam | [ĀpŚS, 6, 19 6.1]
bhūr bhuvaḥ suvaḥ suprajāḥ prajayā bhūyāsaṃ suvīro vīraiḥ suvarcā varcasā supoṣaḥ poṣair ity evopatiṣṭheteti vājasaneyakam | [ĀpŚS, 6, 19 7.1]
bhartuṃ vaḥ śakeyaṃ śraddhā me mā vyāgād iti vā | [ĀpŚS, 6, 19 7.2]
vātsapreṇaiva sāyaṃ prātar upatiṣṭhetety eke | [ĀpŚS, 6, 19 8.1]
goṣūktenāśvasūktena vā | [ĀpŚS, 6, 19 9.1]
{ĀpŚS, 6, 20}
prātaravanekena prātar upastheyaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 20 1.1]
adhiśrita unnīyamāne vā mamāgne varco vihaveṣv astv iti catasro japitvāpāṃ pate yo 'pāṃ bhāgaḥ sa ta eṣa pratiṣiktā arātayaḥ pratiṣiktā arātayaḥ pratiṣiktā arātaya iti trir bhūmau pratiṣicya kālāya vāṃ jaitriyāya vām audbhettriyāya vām avanenije sukṛtāya vām | [ĀpŚS, 6, 20 2.1]
idam ahaṃ duradmanyāṃ niṣplāvayāmi bhrātṛvyāṇāṃ sapatnānām ahaṃ bhūyāsam uttamaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 20 2.2]
apāṃ maitrād ivodakam iti hastau prakṣālya śriyaṃ dhātar mayi dhehi śriyo mādhipatiṃ kuru | [ĀpŚS, 6, 20 2.3]
viśām īśāno maghavendro mā yaśasā nayad iti japitvātharvyuṣṭā devajūtā vīḍu chapathajambhanīḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 20 2.4]
āpo malam iva prāṇijann asmatsu śapathāṁ adhīty ācamyendriyāvatīm adyāhaṃ vācam udyāsaṃ dīrghaprāṇo 'cchinno 'dabdho gopāḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 20 2.5]
ajasraṃ daivyaṃ jyotiḥ sauparṇaṃ cakṣuḥ suśrutau karṇau devaśrutau karṇau keśā barhiḥ śikhā prastaro yathāsthānaṃ kalpayadhvaṃ śaṃ hṛdayāyādo mā mā hāsiṣṭeti yathāliṅgam aṅgāni saṃmṛśya | [ĀpŚS, 6, 20 2.6]
{ĀpŚS, 6, 21}
varco 'si varco mayi dhehy āyukṛd āyuḥpatnī svadhā vo goptryo me stha gopāyata mā rakṣata mātmasado me stha | [ĀpŚS, 6, 21 1.1]
mā naḥ kaścit praghān mā prameṣmahy upa pratnam upa bhūr bhuvaḥ suvar āyur me yacchateti sarvān upasthāyottareṇānuvākenāhavanīyaṃ gharmā jaṭharānnādaṃ mām adyāsmiñ jane kurutam annādo 'ham adyāsmiñ jane bhūyāsam anannādaḥ sa yo 'smān dveṣṭi | [ĀpŚS, 6, 21 1.2]
kavī mātariśvānā paśumantaṃ mām adyāsmiñ jane kurutaṃ paśumān aham adyāsmiñ jane bhūyāsam apaśuḥ sa yo 'smān dveṣṭi | [ĀpŚS, 6, 21 1.3]
yamāṅgirasā yaśasvinaṃ mām adyāsmiñ jane kurutaṃ yaśasvy aham adyāsmiñ jane bhūyāsam ayaśāḥ sa yo 'smān dveṣṭi | [ĀpŚS, 6, 21 1.4]
agne yo no anti śapati yaś ca dūre samāno agne araṇo durasyuḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 21 1.5]
vaiśvānareṇa sayujā sajoṣās taṃ pratyañcaṃ saṃdaha jātavedaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 21 1.6]
agne yat te 'rcis tena taṃ pratyarca yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣmo 'gne yat te śocis tena taṃ pratiśoca yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣmo 'gne yat te tapas tena taṃ pratitapa yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣmo 'gne yat te haras tena taṃ pratihara yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣmo 'gne yat te tejas tena taṃ pratititigdhi yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 21 1.7]
{ĀpŚS, 6, 22}
agne rucāṃ pate namas te ruce rucaṃ mayi dhehi | [ĀpŚS, 6, 22 1.1]
arvāgvaso svasti te pāram aśīyārvāgvaso svasti te pāram aśīyārvāgvaso svasti te pāram aśīya | [ĀpŚS, 6, 22 1.2]
tantur asi tato mā chitthā asau svasti te 'stv asau svasti te 'stv asau svasti te 'stv iti putrāṇāṃ nāmāni gṛhṇāti tristrir ekaikasya | [ĀpŚS, 6, 22 1.3]
svasti vo 'stu ye mām anustha ṣaṇ morvīr aṃhasas pāntu dyauś ca pṛthivī cāpaś cauṣadhayaś cork ca sūnṛtā ca | [ĀpŚS, 6, 22 1.4]
yathā ha tyad vasavo gauryaṃ citpadi ṣitām amuñcatā yajatrāḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 22 1.5]
evo ṣv asman muñcatā vyaṃhaḥ pra tāry agne prataraṃ na āyuḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 22 1.6]
vayaḥ suparṇā upa sedur indraṃ priyamedhā ṛṣayo nādhamānāḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 22 1.7]
apa dhvāntam ūrṇuhi pūrdhi cakṣur mumugdhy asmān nidhayeva baddhān | [ĀpŚS, 6, 22 1.8]
agna āyūṃṣi pavase dadhikrāvṇo akāriṣam iti dve mamāgne varco vihaveṣv astv iti catasro 'gnīṣomāv imaṃ su ma ity eṣā | [ĀpŚS, 6, 22 1.9]
tat savitur vṛṇīmahe vayaṃ devasya bhojanam | [ĀpŚS, 6, 22 1.10]
śreṣṭhaṃ sarvadhātamaṃ turaṃ bhagasya dhīmahi | [ĀpŚS, 6, 22 1.11]
asya hi svayaśastaraṃ savituḥ kaccana priyam | [ĀpŚS, 6, 22 1.12]
na minanti svarājyam | [ĀpŚS, 6, 22 1.13]
{ĀpŚS, 6, 23}
adyā no deva savitaḥ prajāvat sāvīḥ saubhagaṃ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 23 1.1]
parā duḥṣvapniyaṃ suva | [ĀpŚS, 6, 23 1.2]
viśvāni deva savitar duritāni parā suva | [ĀpŚS, 6, 23 1.3]
yad bhadraṃ tan ma ā suva | [ĀpŚS, 6, 23 1.4]
anāgaso aditaye vayaṃ devasya savituḥ save | [ĀpŚS, 6, 23 1.5]
viśvā vāmāni dhīmahi | [ĀpŚS, 6, 23 1.6]
sa hi ratnāni dāśuṣe suvāti savitā bhagaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 23 1.7]
taṃ citraṃ bhāgam īmahe | [ĀpŚS, 6, 23 1.8]
vāmam adya savitar vāmam u śvo dive dive vāmam asmabhyaṃ sāvīḥ saubhagam | [ĀpŚS, 6, 23 1.9]
vāmasya hi kṣayasya deva bhūrer ayā dhiyā vāmabhājaḥ syāma | [ĀpŚS, 6, 23 1.10]
dīkṣā tapo manaso mātariśvā bṛhaspatir vāco asyāḥ sa yoniḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 23 1.11]
vedāṃsi vidyā mayi santu cāravo 'gnīṣomā yaśo asmāsu dhattam | [ĀpŚS, 6, 23 1.12]
agnir yena virājati somo yena virājati sūryo yena virājati virāḍ yena virājati tenāhaṃ viśvatas pari virājyāsam ihaikavṛd ity upasthāyāgnes tṛṇāny apacinoti | [ĀpŚS, 6, 23 1.13]
tejasvīha brahmavarcasī bhavatīti vijñāyate | [ĀpŚS, 6, 23 1.14]
{ĀpŚS, 6, 24}
pravatsyan saṃpreṣyaty agnīn samādhehīti | [ĀpŚS, 6, 24 1.1]
jvalata upatiṣṭhate | [ĀpŚS, 6, 24 2.1]
paśūn naḥ śaṃsya pāhi tān no gopāyāsmākaṃ punarāgamād ity āhavanīyam | [ĀpŚS, 6, 24 3.1]
prajāṃ no narya pāhi tāṃ no gopāyāsmākaṃ punarāgamād iti gārhapatyam | [ĀpŚS, 6, 24 3.2]
annaṃ no budhnya pāhi tan no gopāyāsmākaṃ punarāgamād ity anvāhāryapacanam | [ĀpŚS, 6, 24 3.3]
antarāgnī tiṣṭhañ japatīmān no mitrāvaruṇā gṛhān gopāyataṃ yuvam | [ĀpŚS, 6, 24 4.1]
avinaṣṭān avihṛtān pūṣainān abhirakṣatv āsmākaṃ punarāgamād iti | [ĀpŚS, 6, 24 4.2]
pūrvavad virāṭkramair upasthāyāśitvā pravasatham eṣyann āhāgnīn samādhehīti | [ĀpŚS, 6, 24 5.1]
jvalata upatiṣṭhate prajāṃ me narya pāhi tāṃ me gopāyāsmākaṃ punarāgamād iti gārhapatyam | [ĀpŚS, 6, 24 6.1]
annaṃ me budhnya pāhi tan me gopāyāsmākaṃ punarāgamād ity anvāhāryapacanam | [ĀpŚS, 6, 24 6.2]
paśūn me śaṃsya pāhi tān me gopāyāsmākaṃ punarāgamād ity āhavanīyam | [ĀpŚS, 6, 24 6.3]
mama nāma prathamaṃ jātaveda iti ca | [ĀpŚS, 6, 24 7.1]
vāgyato 'bhipravrajati mā pragāma patho vayaṃ mā yajñād indra sominaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 24 8.1]
māntaḥsthur no arātayaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 24 8.2]
ud asmāṁ uttarān nayāgne ghṛtenāhuta | [ĀpŚS, 6, 24 8.3]
rāyaspoṣeṇa saṃsṛja prajayā ca bahūn kṛdhīti | [ĀpŚS, 6, 24 8.4]
ārād agnibhyo vācaṃ visṛjate | [ĀpŚS, 6, 24 9.1]
{ĀpŚS, 6, 25}
pravasan kāle vihāram abhimukho 'gnyupasthānaṃ japati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 25 1.1]
ihaiva san tatra sato vo agnayaḥ prāṇena vācā manasā bibharmi | [ĀpŚS, 6, 25 2.1]
tiro mā santam āyur mā prahāsīj jyotiṣā vo vaiśvānareṇopatiṣṭha iti yady anupasthāya pravased etayaivopatiṣṭhate | [ĀpŚS, 6, 25 2.2]
samidhaḥ kṛtvā pratyeti | [ĀpŚS, 6, 25 3.1]
yathā ha vā itaṃ pitaraṃ proṣivāṃsaṃ putrāḥ pratyādhāvanty evaṃ ha vā etam agnayaḥ pratyādhāvanti | [ĀpŚS, 6, 25 4.1]
sa śakalān dārūṇi vāharann eti yathaiva tat putrebhya āharann eti | [ĀpŚS, 6, 25 4.2]
tādṛk tad iti vijñāyate | [ĀpŚS, 6, 25 4.3]
ārād agnibhyo vācaṃ yacchati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 25 5.1]
yady enaṃ rājā pitācāryo vāntareṇāgnīn syāc chadirdarśe nainam ādriyeta | [ĀpŚS, 6, 25 6.1]
viśvadānīm ābharanto 'nātureṇa manasā | [ĀpŚS, 6, 25 7.1]
agne mā te prativeśā riṣāma | [ĀpŚS, 6, 25 7.2]
namas te astu mīḍhuṣe namas ta upasadvane | [ĀpŚS, 6, 25 7.3]
agne śumbhasva tanvaḥ saṃ mā rayyā sṛjety abhyaiti | [ĀpŚS, 6, 25 7.4]
agnīn samādhehīti | [ĀpŚS, 6, 25 8.1]
jvalata upatiṣṭhate | [ĀpŚS, 6, 25 9.1]
paśūn naḥ śaṃsyājūgupas tān naḥ punar dehīty āhavanīyam abhiprāṇyāgne sahasrākṣa śatamūrdhañchataṃ te prāṇāḥ sahasram apānāḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 25 10.1]
tvaṃ sāhasrasya rāya īśiṣe sahasradhārasya payasaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 25 10.2]
tasya no rāsva tasya te bhakṣīya tasya te vayaṃ bhūyiṣṭhabhājo bhūyāsmety āhavanīyam | [ĀpŚS, 6, 25 10.3]
{ĀpŚS, 6, 26}
prajāṃ no naryājūgupas tāṃ naḥ punar dehīti gārhapatyam abhiprāṇyāgne gṛhapate sugṛhapatir ahaṃ tvayā gṛhapatinā bhūyāsaṃ sugṛhapatir mayā tvaṃ gṛhapatinā bhūyāḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 26 1.1]
śataṃ himā dvā yū rādhāṃsīt saṃpṛñcānāv asaṃpṛñcānau tanva iti gārhapatyam | [ĀpŚS, 6, 26 1.2]
annaṃ no budhnyājūgupas tan naḥ punar dehīty anvāhāryapacanam abhiprāṇyāntarāgnī tiṣṭhañ japati yathā pravatsyadupasthāne | [ĀpŚS, 6, 26 2.1]
ajūgupatam abhyarākṣīd iti mantraṃ saṃnamati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 26 3.1]
mama nāma tava ca jātaveda iti catasṛbhir āhavanīyam | [ĀpŚS, 6, 26 4.1]
prajāṃ me naryājūgupas tāṃ me punar dehīti gārhapatyam abhyapānyānnaṃ me budhnyājūgupas tan me punar dehīty anvāhāryapacanam abhyapānya paśūn me śaṃsyājūgupas tān me punar dehīty āhavanīyam abhyapānya pūrvavad virāṭkramair upatiṣṭhate | [ĀpŚS, 6, 26 5.1]
ajūgupa iti mantraṃ saṃnamati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 26 5.2]
agnyupasthānavad atra samidho diśāṃ copasthānam | [ĀpŚS, 6, 26 6.1]
navamīṃ ced ati pravasen mitro janān yātayati prajānann iti maitryopasthāya mano jyotir juṣatām ity āhutiṃ juhuyāt | [ĀpŚS, 6, 26 7.1]
samidha āhutim upasthānam ity evam anupūrvāṇy eke samāmananti | [ĀpŚS, 6, 26 8.1]
{ĀpŚS, 6, 27}
tad āhur nāgnir upastheyaḥ kaḥ śreyāṃsaṃ viṣuptaṃ bodhayiṣyatīti | [ĀpŚS, 6, 27 1.1]
abhayaṃkarābhayaṃ me kuru svasti me 'stv abhayaṃ me astv ity eva brūyāt | [ĀpŚS, 6, 27 1.2]

namo vo 'stu pravatsyāmi namo vo 'stu prāvātsyam iti bahvṛcāḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 27 2.1]
gṛhā mā bibhīta mā vepiḍhvam ūrjaṃ bibhrata emasi | [ĀpŚS, 6, 27 3.1]
ūrjaṃ bibhrad vaḥ suvaniḥ sumedhā gṛhān aimi manasā modamānaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 27 3.2]
yeṣām adhyeti pravasan yeṣu saumanaso bahuḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 27 3.3]
gṛhān upahvayāmahe te no jānantu jānataḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 27 3.4]

upahūtā iha gāva upahūtā ajāvayaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 6, 27 3.7]
atho annasya kīlāla upahūto gṛheṣu na iti gṛhān abhyeti | [ĀpŚS, 6, 27 3.8]

irāṃ vahanto ghṛtam ukṣamāṇās teṣv ahaṃ sumanāḥ saṃviśāmīti praviśya japati | [ĀpŚS, 6, 27 5.2]
saṃviśan vā | [ĀpŚS, 6, 27 5.3]
{ĀpŚS, 6, 28}

yajño bhūtvā yajñam āsīda svāṃ yoniṃ jātavedo bhuva ājāyamānaḥ sa kṣaya ehīti hastaṃ pratāpya mukhāyāharate | [ĀpŚS, 6, 28 11.2]

{ĀpŚS, 6, 29}

{ĀpŚS, 6, 30}

{ĀpŚS, 6, 31}

{ĀpŚS, 7, 1}

{ĀpŚS, 7, 3}

{ĀpŚS, 7, 4}

siṃhīḥ asi iti uttaravedyām nivapati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 4 675886_1]
etena eva yaḥ dvitīyasyām iti dvitīyam yaḥ tṛtīyasyām iti tṛtīyam | [ĀpŚS, 7, 4 675887_1]
tūṣṇīm caturtham hṛtvā uru prathasva uru te yajñapatiḥ prathatām iti prathayitvā dhruvā asi iti śamyayā saṃhatya devebhyaḥ kalpasva iti abhimantrya devebhyaḥ śundhasva iti adbhiḥ avokṣya devebhyaḥ śumbhasva iti sikatābhiḥ avakīrya prokṣaṇī śeṣam uttaratas uttaravedyai ninīya āpaḥ ripram nirvahata iti sphyena udīcīm ekasphyām niḥsārya vibhrāj bṛhat pibatu somyam madhu āyuḥ dadhat yajñapatau a vihrutam vāta jūtaḥ yaḥ abhirakṣati tmanā prajāḥ piparti bahudhā virājati iti uttaravedyāḥ antān kalpayati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 4 675889_1]
saṃmṛśati iti eke | [ĀpŚS, 7, 4 675890_1]
{ĀpŚS, 7, 5}
atha asyāḥ madhye prādeśa mātrīm go pada mātrīm aśva śapha mātrīm vā uttaranābhim catur sraktim kṛtvā catur śikhaṇḍe yuvatī kanīne ghṛta pratīke bhuvanasya madhye tayoḥ devāḥ adhisaṃvasantaḥ uttame nāke iha mādayantām iti ubhe abhimantrya indraghoṣaḥ tvā vasubhiḥ purastāt pātu iti etaiḥ yathāliṅgam uttaravedim prokṣati tvaṣṭā tvā rūpaiḥ upariṣṭāt pātu iti madhyam | [ĀpŚS, 7, 5 675892_1]
prokṣaṇī śeṣam dakṣiṇatas uttaravedyai ninayet śucā tvā arpayāmi iti dveṣyam manasā dhyāyan | [ĀpŚS, 7, 5 675894_1]
pūrva vat ekasphyām dakṣiṇatas niḥsārya juhvām pañca gṛhītam gṛhītvā sarvatra hiraṇyam upāsyan uttaravedim uttaranābhim vā vyāghārayati dakṣiṇam aṃsam uttarām śroṇim dakṣiṇām uttaram aṃsam madhyam iti siṃhīḥ asi iti etaiḥ pratimantram | [ĀpŚS, 7, 5 675895_1]
bhūtebhyaḥ tvā iti srucam udgṛhya pautudravaiḥ paridhibhiḥ uttaravedim paridadhāti viśvāyuḥ asi iti madhyamam dhruva kṣit asi iti dakṣiṇam acyuta kṣit asi iti uttaram | [ĀpŚS, 7, 5 675897_1]
paridhi saṃdhinā sarva āhutīḥ juhoti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 5 675898_1]
{ĀpŚS, 7, 6}
agneḥ bhasma asi iti uttaravedyām saṃbhārān nivapati gulgulu sugandhi tejanam śvetām ūrṇā stukām petvasya antarāśṛṅgīyām lūnasya a lūna pūrvasya vā | [ĀpŚS, 7, 6 675899_1]
vyāghāraṇa prabhṛti saṃbhāra nivapana antam uttaravedyām upari agnau dhāryamāṇe eke samāmananti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 6 675900_1]
prokṣa antām kṛtvā udumbara śākhābhiḥ plakṣa śākhābhiḥ vā pracchādya vasati yadi a sadyaskālaḥ paśuḥ bhavati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 6 675901_1]
āhavanīye praṇayanīyam idhmam ādīpya sikatābhiḥ upayamya agnaye praṇīyamānāya anubrūhi iti saṃpreṣyati praṇīyamānāya anubrūhi iti vā | [ĀpŚS, 7, 6 675902_1]
udyamya agnim āhavanīye udyata homam juhoti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 6 675904_1]
prathamāyām tris anūktāyām upayamanībhiḥ upayamya harati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 6 675906_1]
ūrṇāvantaṃ prathamaḥ sīda yonim iti hotur abhijñāyāgne bādhasva vi mṛdho nudasvāpāmīvā apa rakṣāṃsi sedha | [ĀpŚS, 7, 6 7.1]
asmāt samudrād bṛhato divo no 'pāṃ bhūmānam upa naḥ sṛjeha | [ĀpŚS, 7, 6 7.2]
yajña pratitiṣṭha sumatau suśevā ā tvā vasūni purudhā viśantu | [ĀpŚS, 7, 6 7.3]
dīrgham āyur yajamānāya kṛṇvann athāmṛtena jaritāram aṅgdhīha yajñaḥ pratyaṣṭhād iti saṃbhāreṣu pratiṣṭhāpya | [ĀpŚS, 7, 6 7.4]
{ĀpŚS, 7, 7}
agneḥ purīṣam asi iti uttaratas upayamanīḥ nyupya manuṣvat tvā nidhīmahi manuṣvat samidhīmahi agne manuṣvat aṅgiraḥ devān devāyate yaja iti upasamidhya dvādaśa gṛhītena srucam pūrayitvā sapta te agne samidhaḥ sapta jihvāḥ iti saptavatyā pūrṇāhutim juhoti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 7 675912_1]
agniḥ vāyuḥ ādityaḥ viṣṇuḥ yajñam nayatu prajānan mā enam yajña hanaḥ vidan devebhyaḥ yajñam prabrūtāt pra pra yajñapatim tira svāhā iti catasraḥ atimuktīḥ juhoti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 7 675913_1]
eṣa paśubandhasya āhavanīyaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 7, 7 675914_1]
yatas praṇayati sa gārhapatyaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 7, 7 675914_2]
praṇīte ced agnihotra kālaḥ etasmin eva agnihotram juhuyāt | [ĀpŚS, 7, 7 675915_1]
evam anyatra viprakrānte tantre | [ĀpŚS, 7, 7 675916_1]
idhmābarhiḥ āharati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 7 675917_1]
trayoviṃśati dāruḥ idhmaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 7, 7 675918_1]
āśvavālaḥ prastaraḥ | [ĀpŚS, 7, 7 675918_2]
aikṣavī vidhṛtī | [ĀpŚS, 7, 7 675918_3]
kārṣmarya mayāḥ paridhayaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 7, 7 675918_4]
{ĀpŚS, 7, 8}
agnīn paristīrya pāṇi prakṣālana ādi karma pratipadyate | [ĀpŚS, 7, 8 675919_1]
yathārtham pātrāṇi prayunakti sphyam agnihotrahavaṇīm vasā homa havanīm dvitīyām juhūm pṛṣadājya dhānīm dvitīyām upabhṛtam dve ājya sthālyau hṛdayaśūlam asim kumbhīm plakṣa śākhām śākhāpavitram kārṣmarya mayyau vapāśrapaṇyau dvi śūlām eka śūlām ca audumbaram maitrāvaruṇa daṇḍam āsya daghnam cubuka daghnam vā raśane ca | [ĀpŚS, 7, 8 675920_1]
pavitre kṛtvā yajamāna vācam yaccha iti saṃpreṣyati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 8 675922_1]
vāgyataḥ pātrāṇi saṃmṛśya prokṣaṇīḥ saṃskṛtya brāhmaṇam āmantrya pātrāṇi prokṣati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 8 675923_1]
atra vācam visṛjate | [ĀpŚS, 7, 8 675923_2]
sphyam ādāya uttaram parigrāham parigṛhya darśa pūrṇamāsa vat saṃpreṣyati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 8 675924_1]
ājyena dadhnā udehi iti saṃpraiṣa antam namati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 8 675925_1]
srucām saṃmārjana kāle sruvam saṃmṛjya tasya āvṛtā svadhitim juhū vat vasā homa havanīm upabhṛt vat pṛṣadājya dhānīm | [ĀpŚS, 7, 8 675926_1]
ājyam nirupya dadhi nirvapati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 8 675928_1]
adhiśrayaṇa varjam dadhani kriyate | [ĀpŚS, 7, 8 675929_1]
na etasya dadhnaḥ saṃskāraḥ vidyate iti aparam | [ĀpŚS, 7, 8 675930_1]
{ĀpŚS, 7, 9}
ājya grahaṇa kāle catur juhvām gṛhṇāti catuḥ upabhṛti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 9 675931_1]
dadhani ājyam ānīya mahīnām payaḥ asi iti pṛṣadājya dhānyām pañca gṛhītam pṛṣadājyam jyotiḥ asi viśva rūpam viśveṣām devānām samidh iti vā | [ĀpŚS, 7, 9 675932_1]
catuḥ dhruvāyām | [ĀpŚS, 7, 9 675933_1]
sādana kāle ājyāni sādayati upabhṛt vat pṛṣadājya dhānīm | [ĀpŚS, 7, 9 675934_1]
pūrvavat ājyāni abhimantrya agreṇa āhavanīyam yūpa avaṭam parilikhati ardham antarvedi ardham bahirvedi | [ĀpŚS, 7, 9 675936_1]
pūrvavat abhreḥ ādānam parilekhanaḥ ca | [ĀpŚS, 7, 9 675937_1]
atha khanati yathā na āvis uparam bhaviṣyati iti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 9 675938_1]
agreṇa avaṭam prāñcam yūpam nidhāya yat te śikvaḥ parāvadhīt takṣā hastena vāsyā āpaḥ tat sarvam jīvalāḥ śundhantu śucayaḥ śucim iti yūpam prakṣālya atha enam yavamatībhiḥ prokṣati pṛthivyai tvā iti mūlam antarikṣāya tvā iti madhyam dive tvā iti agram | [ĀpŚS, 7, 9 675940_1]
śundhatām lokaḥ pitṛṣadanaḥ iti prokṣaṇī śeṣam avaṭe avanīya yavaḥ asi iti yavam avāsya pitṝṇām sadanam asi iti barhiṣā avastīrya su āveśaḥ asi iti prathama parāpātinam śakalam avāsya ghṛtena dyāvāpṛthivī āpṛṇethām iti sruveṇa śakale hutvā | [ĀpŚS, 7, 9 675942_1]
{ĀpŚS, 7, 10}
yūpāya ajyamānāya anubrūhi iti saṃpreṣyati ajyamānāya anubrūhi añjmaḥ yūpam anubrūhi iti vā | [ĀpŚS, 7, 10 675943_1]
atha enam asaṃskṛtena ājyena yajamānaḥ agratas śakalena anakti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 10 675944_1]
aindram asi iti caṣālam aktvā su pippalābhyaḥ tvā oṣadhībhyaḥ iti pratimucya devaḥ tvā savitā madhvā anaktu iti sruveṇa saṃtatam a vicchindan agniṣṭhām aśrim anakti ā uparāt | [ĀpŚS, 7, 10 675945_1]
raśanā deśe tris sarvatas yūpam saṃmṛśati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 10 675946_1]

yam kāmayeta tejasā enam iti uktam | [ĀpŚS, 7, 10 675952_1]
agram āhavanīyam upanatam yūpasya avanatam mūlam | [ĀpŚS, 7, 10 675953_1]
an āvis uparam kṛtvā brahma vanim tvā kṣatra vanim iti pradakṣiṇam pāṃsubhiḥ paryūhya brahma dṛṃha kṣatram dṛṃha iti maitrāvaruṇa daṇḍena samam bhūmi paridṛṃhaṇam kṛtvā | [ĀpŚS, 7, 10 675954_1]
{ĀpŚS, 7, 11}
unnambhaya pṛthivīm iti adbhiḥ pariṣiñcati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 11 675955_1]

devasya tvā savituḥ prasave iti raśanām ādāya viṣṇoḥ karmāṇi paśyata iti sa raśanena pāṇinā yūpam unmārṣṭi | [ĀpŚS, 7, 11 675958_1]

parivīḥ asi iti nābhi daghne raśanayā tris pradakṣiṇam yūpam parivyayati madhya deśe vā | [ĀpŚS, 7, 11 675962_1]
yam kāmayeta ūrjā enam iti uktam | [ĀpŚS, 7, 11 675963_1]

yam kāmayeta pumān asya jāyeta iti ā antam tasya praveṣṭya aṇimati sthavimat pravīya divaḥ sūnuḥ asi iti svarum ādāya antarikṣasya tvā sānau avagūhāmi iti uttareṇa agniṣṭhām madhyame raśanā guṇe avagūhati uttame sarveṣu vā | [ĀpŚS, 7, 11 675966_1]
dvayoḥ adharayoḥ iti vājasaneyakam | [ĀpŚS, 7, 11 675968_1]
{ĀpŚS, 7, 12}
paśum snapayanti kūṭa karṇa kāṇa khaṇḍa baṇḍa śloṇa sapta śapha varjam | [ĀpŚS, 7, 12 675969_1]
yadi aṅga hīnaḥ syāt aṅgataḥ vā virujyeta atha ekeṣām vaiṣṇavīm āgnāvaiṣṇavīm sārasvatīm bārhaspatyām iti ca hutvā prayojayet | [ĀpŚS, 7, 12 675971_1]
yaḥ a panna dat malam tat paśūnām iti vijñāyate | [ĀpŚS, 7, 12 675972_1]
iṣe tvā iti barhiṣī ādatte upavīḥ asi iti plakṣa śākhām bahu parṇa śākhām a pratiśuṣka agrām a suṣirām | [ĀpŚS, 7, 12 675973_1]

tṛṇena upākaroti iti eke | [ĀpŚS, 7, 12 675976_1]
barhirbhyām plakṣa śākhayā ca purastāt pratyañcam paśum upākaroti upa u devān daivīḥ viśaḥ prajāpateḥ jāyamānāḥ iti ca etābhyām upaspṛśan indra agnibhyām tvā juṣṭam upākaromi iti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 12 675977_1]
pañca kṛtvas devatā upadeśanam upākaraṇe niyojane prokṣaṇe vapāyāḥ uddharaṇe hṛdayasya abhighāraṇe iti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 12 675979_1]
prajānantaḥ pratigṛhṇanti pūrve iti pañca hutvā agnim manthati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 12 675980_1]
api vā agnim mathitvā upākuryāt | [ĀpŚS, 7, 12 675981_1]
agneḥ janitram asi iti adhimanthanam śakalam nidadhāti vṛṣaṇau sthaḥ iti prāñcau darbhau | [ĀpŚS, 7, 12 675982_1]

devaḥ vām savitā madhvā anaktu iti ājya sthālyāḥ bile aṅktvā ghṛtena akte vṛṣaṇam dadhāthām iti ubhe abhimantrya āyuḥ asi iti samavadhāya | [ĀpŚS, 7, 12 675986_1]
{ĀpŚS, 7, 13}
agnaye mathyamānāya anubrūhi iti saṃpreṣyati mathyamānāya anubrūhi iti vā | [ĀpŚS, 7, 13 675987_1]

sāvitreṇa raśanām ādāya paśoḥ dakṣiṇe bāhau parivīya ūrdhvam utkṛṣya ṛtasya tvā deva haviḥ pāśena ārabhe iti dakṣiṇe ardha śirasi pāśena akṣṇayā pratimucya dharṣa mānuṣān iti uttaratas yūpasya niyunakti dakṣiṇatas aikādaśinān | [ĀpŚS, 7, 13 675997_1]
adbhyaḥ tvā oṣadhībhyaḥ prokṣāmi iti prokṣati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 13 675999_1]
apām peruḥ asi iti pāyayati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 13 676000_1]
svāttam cit sa devam havyam āpaḥ devīḥ svadata enam iti upariṣṭāt adhastāt sarvatas ca prokṣya vedam nidhāya sāmidhenībhyaḥ pratipadyate | [ĀpŚS, 7, 13 676001_1]
{ĀpŚS, 7, 14}
srucyam āghārya pratyākramya juhvā paśum samanakti sam te prāṇaḥ vāyunā gacchatām iti śirasi sam yajatraiḥ aṅgāni iti aṃsa uccalayoḥ sam yajñapatiḥ āśiṣā iti śroṇyām | [ĀpŚS, 7, 14 676002_1]
dhruvā samañjana ādi karma pratipadyate | [ĀpŚS, 7, 14 676006_1]
samānam ā pravarāt | [ĀpŚS, 7, 14 676006_2]
ṣaṭ ṛtvijaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 7, 14 676007_1]
daivam ca mānuṣam ca hotārau vṛtvā punar āśrāvya maitrāvaruṇam pravṛṇīte mitrāvaruṇau praśāstārau praśāstrāt iti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 14 676008_1]
tiṣṭhati paśau ekādaśa prayājān yajati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 14 676009_1]
samidbhyaḥ preṣya iti prathamam saṃpreṣyati preṣya preṣya iti itarān | [ĀpŚS, 7, 14 676010_1]
caturtha aṣṭamayoḥ pratisamānīya daśa iṣṭvā ekādaśāya ājyam avaśinaṣṭi | [ĀpŚS, 7, 14 676012_1]
tān yajamānaḥ prākṛtaiḥ āditas caturbhiḥ caturaḥ anumantrya caturthasya anumantraṇena duraḥprabhṛtīn trīn uttamena śeṣam pratyākramya juhvā svaru svadhitī anakti tris svarum sakṛt svadhiteḥ anyatarām dhārām | [ĀpŚS, 7, 14 676014_1]
svarum antardhāya svadhitinā paśum samanakti ghṛtena aktau paśum trāyethām iti śirasi na vā svadhitinā svaruṇā eva | [ĀpŚS, 7, 14 676016_1]
aktayā śṛtasya avadyati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 14 676018_1]
paśum itarayā viśāsti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 14 676018_2]
śamitre svadhitim prayacchan āha śamitar eṣā te aśriḥ spaṣṭā astu iti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 14 676019_1]
{ĀpŚS, 7, 15}
paryagnaye kriyamāṇāya anubrūhi iti saṃpreṣyati paryagnaye anubrūhi iti vā | [ĀpŚS, 7, 15 676020_1]
āhavanīyāt ulmukam ādāya āgnīdhraḥ pari vāja patiḥ kaviḥ iti tris pradakṣiṇam paryagnikaroti paśum yūpam āhavanīyam śāmitra deśam cātvālam | [ĀpŚS, 7, 15 676022_1]
ājyāni ca iti eke | [ĀpŚS, 7, 15 676023_1]
pratyapisṛjya ulmukam tris pratiparyeti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 15 676024_1]

paśupateḥ paśavaḥ virūpāḥ sadṛśāḥ uta teṣām yam vavrire devāḥ tam svarāj anumanyatām iti dvitīyām | [ĀpŚS, 7, 15 676027_1]
ye badhyamānam iti pramucyamāne pramuñcamānāḥ iti praṇīyamāne | [ĀpŚS, 7, 15 676028_1]
revatīḥ yajñapatim priyadhā viśata iti vapāśrapaṇībhyām paśum anvārabhete adhvaryuḥ yajamānaḥ ca | [ĀpŚS, 7, 15 676030_1]
āśrāvya pratyāśrāvite saṃpreṣyati upapreṣya hotar havyā devebhyaḥ iti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 15 676031_1]
pra asmai agnim bharata stṛṇīta barhiḥ iti hotuḥ abhijñāya āhavanīyāt ulmukam ādāya āgnīdhraḥ pūrvaḥ pratipadyate | [ĀpŚS, 7, 15 676032_1]
śamitā paśum nayati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 15 676033_1]
uro antarikṣa iti antarā cātvāla utkarau udañcam paśum nayanti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 15 676034_1]
nānā prāṇaḥ yajamānasya paśunā iti adhvaryuḥ japati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 15 676035_1]
{ĀpŚS, 7, 16}
ūvadhya goham pārthivam khanatāt iti abhijñāya ūvadhya goham khanati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 16 676036_1]
abhiparyagnikṛte deśe ulmukam nidadhāti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 16 676037_1]
sa śāmitraḥ | [ĀpŚS, 7, 16 676038_1]
tam dakṣiṇena pratyañcam paśum avasthāpya pṛthivyāḥ saṃpṛcaḥ pāhi iti tasya adhastāt barhiḥ upāsyati upākaraṇayoḥ anyatarat | [ĀpŚS, 7, 16 676039_1]
tasmin saṃjñapayanti pratyak śirasam udīcīna pādam | [ĀpŚS, 7, 16 676040_1]
a māyum kṛṇvantam saṃjñapayata iti uktvā parāṅ āvartate adhvaryuḥ | [ĀpŚS, 7, 16 676041_1]
svar vid asi svar vittvā svar ihi svar mahyam svar paśubhyaḥ loka vid asi lokam vittvā lokam ihi lokam mahyam lokam paśubhyaḥ gātu vid asi gātum vittvā gātum ihi gātum mahyam gātum paśubhyaḥ nātha vid asi nātham vittvā nātham ihi nātham mahyam nātham paśubhyaḥ na vai u etat mriyase na riṣyasi devāṁ id eṣi pathibhiḥ su gebhiḥ yatra yanti su kṛtaḥ na api duṣkṛtaḥ tatra tvā devaḥ savitā dadhātu āśānām tvā āśā pālebhyaḥ iti eṣā | [ĀpŚS, 7, 16 676048_1]
viśvā āśā madhunā saṃsṛjāmy anamīvā āpa oṣadhayo bhavantu | [ĀpŚS, 7, 16 7.8]
ayaṃ yajamāno mṛdho vyasyatām | [ĀpŚS, 7, 16 7.9]
a gṛbhītāḥ paśavaḥ santu sarve iti uktvā parāṅ āvartate yajamānaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 7, 16 676051_1]
nānā prāṇaḥ yajamānasya paśunā iti adhvaryuḥ japati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 16 676052_1]
{ĀpŚS, 7, 17}
yāsām ūdhar catur bilam madhoḥ pūrṇam ghṛtasya ca tāḥ naḥ santu payasvatīḥ asmin goṣṭhe vayaḥ vṛdhaḥ iha paśavaḥ viśva rūpāḥ ramantām asmin yajñe viśva vidaḥ ghṛtācīḥ agnim kulāyam abhisaṃvasānāḥ asmāṁ avantu payasā ghṛtena iti pṛṣadājyam avekṣamāṇau vāgyatau āsāte adhvaryuḥ yajamānaḥ ca | [ĀpŚS, 7, 17 676056_1]
indrasya bhāgaḥ suvite dadhātanemaṃ yajñaṃ yajamānaṃ ca sūrau | [ĀpŚS, 7, 17 2.1]
yaḥ naḥ dveṣṭi anu tam ravasva anāgasaḥ yajamānasya vīrāḥ iti ca vāśyamāne avekṣete | [ĀpŚS, 7, 17 676058_1]
yat paśuḥ māyum akṛta iti saṃjñapte saṃjñapta homam juhoti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 17 676059_1]
śamitāraḥ upetana iti vapāśrapaṇībhyām paśum upaitaḥ adhvaryuḥ yajamānaḥ ca | [ĀpŚS, 7, 17 676060_1]
paśoḥ pāśam pramuñcati aditiḥ pāśam pramumoktu etam iti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 17 676061_1]
saṃveṣṭya raśanām grīvāsu nidhāya eka śūlayā upasajya cātvāle udasyati arātīyantam adharam karomi iti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 17 676062_1]
yadi abhicaret arātīyantam adharam kṛṇomi yam dviṣmaḥ tasmin pratimuñcāmi pāśam iti tayā vṛkṣam sthāṇum stambham vā apidadhyāt | [ĀpŚS, 7, 17 676063_1]
{ĀpŚS, 7, 18}
tatas pratiprasthātā patnīm udānayati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 18 676064_1]
namaḥ te ātāna iti patnī ādityam upatiṣṭhate | [ĀpŚS, 7, 18 676065_1]

anumantrayate iti eke | [ĀpŚS, 7, 18 676066_2]
āpaḥ devīḥ śuddhāyuvaḥ iti cātvāle patnī apaḥ avamṛśati ṛtvijaḥ yajamānaḥ ca | [ĀpŚS, 7, 18 676067_1]
na patnī iti eke | [ĀpŚS, 7, 18 676068_1]
adbhiḥ paśoḥ sarvān prāṇān āpyāyayati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 18 676069_1]

etat vā viparītam | [ĀpŚS, 7, 18 676071_1]
vāc te āpyāyatām iti etaiḥ yathāliṅgam | [ĀpŚS, 7, 18 676072_1]
yā te prāṇān śuc jagāma iti hṛdaya deśam | [ĀpŚS, 7, 18 676073_1]
meḍhram te āpyāyatām iti meḍhram | [ĀpŚS, 7, 18 676074_1]
śuddhāḥ caritrāḥ iti pādān | [ĀpŚS, 7, 18 676075_1]
ekaikam āpyāyya japati śam adbhyaḥ iti purā stokānām bhūmeḥ prāpaṇāt | [ĀpŚS, 7, 18 676076_1]
śam oṣadhībhyaḥ śam pṛthivyai iti bhūmyām śeṣam ninīya oṣadhe trāyasva enam iti upākaraṇayoḥ avaśiṣṭam dakṣiṇena nābhim antardhāya svadhite mā enam hiṃsīḥ iti svadhitinā pārśvataḥ tiryak āchyati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 18 676077_1]
barhiṣaḥ agram savyena pāṇinā ādatte | [ĀpŚS, 7, 18 676078_1]
atha madhyam yatas āchyati tat ubhayatas lohitena aṅktvā rakṣasām bhāgaḥ asi iti uttaram aparam avāntaradeśam nirasya atha enat savyena padā abhitiṣṭhati idam aham rakṣaḥ avabādhe idam aham rakṣaḥ adhamam tamaḥ nayāmi iti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 18 676079_1]
{ĀpŚS, 7, 19}
iṣe tvā iti vapām utkhidya ghṛtena dyāvāpṛthivī prorṇvāthām iti vapayā dvi śūlām pracchādya ūrje tvā iti taniṣṭhe antataḥ eka śūlayā upatṛṇatti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 19 676080_1]
devebhyaḥ kalpasva iti abhimantrya devebhyaḥ śundhasva iti adbhiḥ avokṣya devebhyaḥ śumbhasva iti svadhitinā vapām nimṛjya a chinnaḥ rāyaḥ su vīraḥ indra agnibhyām tvā juṣṭām utkṛntāmi iti utkṛntati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 19 676081_1]
muṣṭinā śamitā vapoddharaṇam apidhāya āste ā vapāyāḥ homāt | [ĀpŚS, 7, 19 676082_1]
pratyuṣṭam rakṣaḥ pratyuṣṭāḥ arātayaḥ iti śāmitre vapām pratitapya namaḥ sūryasya saṃdṛśe iti ādityam upasthāya uru antarikṣam anu ihi iti abhipravrajati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 19 676083_1]
ulmuka eka deśam ādāya āgnīdhraḥ pūrvaḥ pratipadyate | [ĀpŚS, 7, 19 676084_1]
vapāśrapaṇī punar anvārabhate yajamānaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 7, 19 676085_1]
ulmuka eka deśam āhavanīye pratyapisṛjati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 19 676086_1]
nirdagdham rakṣaḥ nirdagdhāḥ arātayaḥ iti āhavanīyasya antame aṅgāre vapām nikūḍya antarā yūpam āhavanīyam ca dakṣiṇā atihṛtya pratiprasthātre prayacchati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 19 676087_1]
tām dakṣiṇatas āsīnaḥ pratiprasthātā āhavanīye śrapayati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 19 676088_1]
{ĀpŚS, 7, 20}
vāyo vīhi stokānām iti barhiṣaḥ agram adhastāt vapāyāḥ upāsyati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 20 676089_1]
tvām u te dadhire havya vāham iti sruveṇa vapām abhijuhoti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 20 676090_1]
prādurbhūteṣu stokeṣu stokebhyaḥ anubrūhi iti saṃpreṣyati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 20 676091_1]
a lohinīm su śṛtām kṛtvā su pippalāḥ oṣadhīḥ kṛdhī iti dakṣiṇasyām vedi śroṇyām barhiṣi plakṣa śākhāyām āsādya prayutā dveṣāṃsi iti vapāśrapaṇī pravṛhya nidhāya ghṛtavati śabde juhū upabhṛtau ādāya dakṣiṇā atikramya āśrāvya pratyāśrāvite saṃpreṣyati svāhākṛtībhyaḥ preṣya svāhākṛtibhyaḥ preṣya iti vā | [ĀpŚS, 7, 20 676092_1]

etat vā viparītam | [ĀpŚS, 7, 20 676094_1]
na upabhṛtam | [ĀpŚS, 7, 20 676095_1]
ājyabhāgau yajati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 20 676096_1]
tau na paśau karoti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 20 676097_1]
na some iti eke | [ĀpŚS, 7, 20 676098_1]
svāhā devebhyaḥ iti pūrvam parivapyam hutvā juhvām upastīrya hiraṇya śakalam avadhāya kṛtsnām vapām avadāya hiraṇya śakalam upariṣṭāt kṛtvā abhighārayati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 20 676099_1]
evam pañca avattā bhavati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 20 676100_1]

{ĀpŚS, 7, 21}
indra agnibhyām chāgasya vapāyāḥ medasaḥ anubrūhi indra agnibhyām chāgasya vapāyāḥ medasaḥ preṣya iti saṃpraiṣau | [ĀpŚS, 7, 21 676102_1]
jātavedaḥ vapayā gaccha devān iti vaṣaṭkṛte hutvā pratyākramya devebhyaḥ svāhā iti uttaram parivapyam hutvā vapoddharaṇam abhighārayati uttaratas tiṣṭhan | [ĀpŚS, 7, 21 676103_1]
pratiprasthātā āhavanīye vapāśrapaṇī praharati svāhā ūrdhva nabhasam mārutam gacchatam iti prācīm dvi śūlām pratīcīm eka śūlām | [ĀpŚS, 7, 21 676104_1]

tisraḥ | [ĀpŚS, 7, 21 676109_1]
idam āpaḥ pravahatāvadyaṃ ca malaṃ ca yat | [ĀpŚS, 7, 21 6.3]

āpo mā tasmād enaso viśvān muñcatv aṃhasaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 7, 21 6.5]

{ĀpŚS, 7, 22}

haviṣkṛtā vācam visṛjya paśum viśāsti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 22 676119_1]

gudam mā nirvleṣīḥ iti saṃpreṣyati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 22 676123_1]
mā viparyāsta ity artho bhavati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 22 8]
udak pavitre kumbhyām paśum avadhāya śūle praṇīkṣya hṛdayam śāmitre śrapayati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 22 676125_1]
avahanana ādi karma pratipadyate | [ĀpŚS, 7, 22 676126_1]
vapayā pracarya puroḍāśena pracarati śṛte vā paśau | [ĀpŚS, 7, 22 676127_1]
indra agnibhyām puroḍāśasya anubrūhi indra agnibhyām puroḍāśasya preṣya iti saṃpraiṣau indra agnibhyām puroḍāśasya avadīyamānasya anubrūhi indra agnibhyām puroḍāśasya preṣya iti vā | [ĀpŚS, 7, 22 676129_1]
agnaye anubrūhi agnaye preṣya iti sviṣṭakṛtaḥ saṃpraiṣau | [ĀpŚS, 7, 22 676131_1]
{ĀpŚS, 7, 23}
prāśitram avadāya iḍām na yajamāna bhāgam | [ĀpŚS, 7, 23 676132_1]
haviḥ āhuti prabhṛti iḍā antaḥ saṃtiṣṭhate | [ĀpŚS, 7, 23 676133_1]
upahutām maitrāvaruṇa ṣaṣṭhāḥ bhakṣayitvā pūrvavat prastare mārjayitvā sruveṇa pṛṣadājyasya upahatya vedena upayamya tris pṛcchati śṛtam haviḥ śamitar iti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 23 676134_1]
śṛtam iti itaraḥ pratyāha ardha adhve dvitīyam prāpya tṛtīyam | [ĀpŚS, 7, 23 676135_1]
pūṣā mā paśu pāḥ pātu iti prathame abhipravrajati pūṣā mā pathipāḥ pātu iti dvitīye pūṣā mā adhipāḥ pātu iti tṛtīye | [ĀpŚS, 7, 23 676137_1]
śūlāt pravṛhya hṛdayam kumbhyām avadhāya sam te manasā manaḥ iti pṛṣadājyena hṛdayam abhighārayati uttaratas parikramya | [ĀpŚS, 7, 23 676140_1]

paśum haran pārśvatas hṛdayaśūlam dhārayati an upaspṛśan ātmānam itarān ca | [ĀpŚS, 7, 23 676143_1]
antarā yūpam āhavanīyam ca dakṣiṇā atihṛtya pañcahotrā ṣaḍḍhotrā vā dakṣiṇasyām vedi śroṇyām āsādya catasṛṣu upastṛṇīte juhū upabhṛtoḥ vasā homa havanyām samavatta dhānyām iti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 23 676144_1]
juhū upabhṛtoḥ hiraṇya śakalau avadhāya barhiṣi plakṣa śākhāyām avadānāni avadyan saṃpreṣyati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 23 676145_1]
{ĀpŚS, 7, 24}
manotāyai haviṣo 'vadīyamānasyānubrūhīti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 24 1]
hṛdayasyāgre 'vadyati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 24 2.1]
atha jihvāyā atha vakṣaso yāthākāmītareṣām | [ĀpŚS, 7, 24 2.2]
madhyato gudasyāvadyatīty uktam | [ĀpŚS, 7, 24 3]
yathoddhṛtaṃ vā | [ĀpŚS, 7, 24 4]
daivatānāṃ dvir dvir avadāya juhvām avadadhāti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 24 5.1]
upabhṛti sauviṣṭakṛtānāṃ sakṛtsakṛt | [ĀpŚS, 7, 24 5.2]
gudaṃ traidhaṃ vibhajya sthavimad upayaḍbhyo nidhāya madhyamaṃ dvaidhaṃ vibhajya daivateṣv avadadhāti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 24 6.1]
aṇimat sauviṣṭakṛteṣu | [ĀpŚS, 7, 24 6.2]
api vā dvaidhaṃ vibhajya sthavimad upayaḍbhyo nidhāyetarat traidhaṃ vibhajya madhyaṃ dvaidhaṃ vibhajya daivateṣv avadadhāti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 24 7.1]
aṇimat sauviṣṭakṛteṣu sthaviṣṭham iḍāyām | [ĀpŚS, 7, 24 7.2]
tredhā medo 'vadyati dvibhāgaṃ srucos tṛtīyaṃ samavattadhānyām | [ĀpŚS, 7, 24 8]
yūṣe medo 'vadhāya medasā srucau prāvṛtya hiraṇyaśakalāv upariṣṭātkṛtvābhighārayati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 24 9]
samavattadhānyāṃ ṣaḍ ādyānīḍām avadyati vaniṣṭhuṃ saptamam | [ĀpŚS, 7, 24 10.1]
ṣaḍbhyo vā vaniṣṭhoḥ saptamāt | [ĀpŚS, 7, 24 10.2]
anasthibhir iḍāṃ vardhayati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 24 11]

{ĀpŚS, 7, 25}
apāṃ tvauṣadhīnāṃ rasaṃ gṛhṇāmīti vasāhomahavanyāṃ vasāhomaṃ gṛhṇāti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 25 1]
svadhitinā dhārāṃ chinatti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 25 2]
dviḥ pañcāvattinaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 7, 25 3]
śrīr asīti pārśvena vasāhomaṃ prayauti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 25 4]

svadhitinā vā prayauti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 25 5.2]
svadhitināpidadhātīty eke | [ĀpŚS, 7, 25 5.3]
atha yan na śīrṣṇo 'vadyati nāṃsayor nāṇūkasya nāparasakthyor anavadānīyāni | [ĀpŚS, 7, 25 6]

atha haviṣā pracarati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 25 8]
indrāgnibhyāṃ chāgasya haviṣo 'nubrūhīndrāgnibhyāṃ chāgasya haviṣaḥ preṣyeti saṃpraiṣau | [ĀpŚS, 7, 25 9]
yājyāyā ardharce pratiprasthātā vasāhomaṃ juhoti ghṛtaṃ ghṛtapāvānaḥ pibateti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 25 10]
udrekeṇa diśaḥ pradiśa iti pratidiśaṃ juhoti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 25 11.1]
madhye pañcamena | [ĀpŚS, 7, 25 11.2]
prāñcam uttamaṃ saṃsthāpya namo digbhya ity upatiṣṭhate | [ĀpŚS, 7, 25 12]
vaṣaṭkṛte juhoti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 25 13]
atra vā diśaḥ pratiyajet | [ĀpŚS, 7, 25 14.1]
upariṣṭād vā vanaspateḥ sviṣṭakṛto vā | [ĀpŚS, 7, 25 14.2]
pratyākramya juhvām upastīrya sakṛt pṛṣadājyasyopahatya dvir abhighārya vanaspataye 'nubrūhi vanaspataye preṣyeti saṃpraiṣau | [ĀpŚS, 7, 25 15.1]
vaṣaṭkṛte juhoti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 25 15.2]
sviṣṭakṛdvad yajamāno 'numantrayate | [ĀpŚS, 7, 25 16]
upary āhavanīye juhvām aupabhṛtāni viparyasyann āhāgnaye sviṣṭakṛte 'nubrūhy agnaye sviṣṭakṛte preṣyeti saṃpraiṣau | [ĀpŚS, 7, 25 17]

{ĀpŚS, 7, 26}
atreḍāyā niravadānam eke samāmananti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 26 1]

meda upastīrya medasābhighārayati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 26 3]
yaṃ kāmayetāpaśuḥ syād ity amedaskaṃ tasmā ity uktam | [ĀpŚS, 7, 26 4]
upahūtāṃ maitrāvaruṇaṣaṣṭhā bhakṣayanti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 26 5.1]
pratiprasthātā saptamaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 7, 26 5.2]

adhyūdhnīṃ hotre harati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 26 7]
agnīd aupayajān aṅgārān āharopayaṣṭar upasīda brahman prasthāsyāmaḥ samidham ādhāyāgnīt paridhīṃś cāgniṃ ca sakṛt sakṛt saṃmṛḍḍhīti saṃpreṣyati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 26 8]
āgnīdhrād aupayajān aṅgārān āharati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 26 9.1]
hotrīya upayajati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 26 9.2]
śāmitrān nirūḍhapaśubandha uttarasyāṃ vediśroṇyām | [ĀpŚS, 7, 26 10]
gudakāṇḍam ekādaśadhā tiryak chittvāsaṃbhindann aparyāvartayann anūyājānāṃ vaṣaṭkṛte vaṣaṭkṛta ekaikaṃ gudakāṇḍaṃ pratiprasthātā hastena juhoti samudraṃ gaccha svāhety etaiḥ pratimantram | [ĀpŚS, 7, 26 11]
sarvāṇi hutvādbhyas tvauṣadhībhya iti barhiṣi lepaṃ nimṛjya mano me hārdi yaccheti japati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 26 12.1]
pṛṣadājyaṃ juhvām ānīya pṛṣadājyadhānīm upabhṛtaṃ kṛtvā tenaikādaśānūyājān yajati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 26 12.2]
devebhyaḥ preṣyeti prathamaṃ saṃpreṣyati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 26 13.1]
preṣya preṣyetītarān | [ĀpŚS, 7, 26 13.2]
tān yajamānaḥ prākṛtair anumantrayate | [ĀpŚS, 7, 26 14]
{ĀpŚS, 7, 27}
prathamenādyāṃś caturo daśamaṃ ca | [ĀpŚS, 7, 27 1.1]
dvitīyena prāg vanaspateḥ | [ĀpŚS, 7, 27 1.2]
uttamena śeṣam | [ĀpŚS, 7, 27 1.3]
uttarayor vikāreṣūbhau hotāraṃ codayato 'dhvaryur maitrāvaruṇaś ca yajeti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 27 2]
atra svaror añjanam eke samāmananti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 27 3]
pratyākramya juhvāṃ svarum avadhāyānūyājānte juhoti dyām te dhūmo gacchatv antarikṣam arciḥ pṛthivīṃ bhasmanā pṛṇasva svāheti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 27 4]
samānam ā pratyāśrāvaṇāt | [ĀpŚS, 7, 27 5]
sūktavākapraiṣo vikriyate | [ĀpŚS, 7, 27 6]
taṃ maitrāvaruṇo brūyād agnim adya hotāram avṛṇīteti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 27 7]
dhruvāvarjaṃ catasṛbhiḥ paridhīn abhijuhoti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 27 8]
dakṣiṇena vihāraṃ jāghanīṃ hṛtvā tayā patnīḥ saṃyājayanti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 27 9]
ājyena somatvaṣṭārāv iṣṭvottānāyai jāghanyai devānāṃ patnībhyo 'vadyati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 27 10.1]
nīcyā agnaye gṛhapataye | [ĀpŚS, 7, 27 10.2]
uttānāyai hotra iḍām avadyati nīcyā agnīdhe | [ĀpŚS, 7, 27 11]
tāṃ patnyai prayacchati tāṃ sādhvaryave 'nyasmai vā brāhmaṇāya | [ĀpŚS, 7, 27 12]
bāhuṃ śamitre | [ĀpŚS, 7, 27 13]
taṃ sa brāhmaṇāya yady abrāhmaṇo bhavati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 27 14]
yajña yajñaṃ gaccheti trīṇi samiṣṭayajūṃṣi hutvānupaspṛśan hṛdayaśūlam udaṅ paretyāsaṃcare 'pa upaninīya śuṣkārdrayoḥ saṃdhāv udvāsayati śug asīti dveṣyaṃ manasā dhyāyan | [ĀpŚS, 7, 27 15]
sumitrā na āpa oṣadhaya iti tasmiṃś cātvāle vā sahapatnīkā mārjayitvā dhāmno dhāmno rājann ud uttamam ity ādityam upasthāyaidho 'sy edhiṣīmahīty āhavanīye samidha ādhāyāpo anvacāriṣam ity upatiṣṭhante | [ĀpŚS, 7, 27 16]
{ĀpŚS, 7, 28}
iṣṭividho vā anyaḥ paśubandhaḥ somavidho 'nyaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 7, 28 1.1]
sa yatraitad apaḥ praṇayati pūrṇapātraṃ ninayati viṣṇukramān krāmati sa iṣṭividho 'to 'nyaḥ somavidha iti vājasaneyakam | [ĀpŚS, 7, 28 1.2]
yūpaṃ yajamāna upatiṣṭhate namaḥ svarubhyaḥ sannān māvagātāpaścāddaghvānnam bhūyāsam | [ĀpŚS, 7, 28 2.1]
śṛṅgāṇīvecchṛṅgiṇāṃ saṃdadṛśrire caṣālavantaḥ svaravaḥ pṛthivyām | [ĀpŚS, 7, 28 2.2]
te devāsaḥ svaravas tasthivāṃso namaḥ sakhibhyaḥ sannān māvagāta | [ĀpŚS, 7, 28 2.3]
āśāsānaḥ suvīryam iti ca | [ĀpŚS, 7, 28 2.4]
upasthāya yajña śaṃ ca ma iti japati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 28 3]
āhutyai vā etaṃ vanaspatibhyaḥ pracyāvayanty upayajya manuṣyāḥ prayānti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 28 4.1]
yūpo vai yajñasya duriṣṭam āmuñcate | [ĀpŚS, 7, 28 4.2]
yad yūpam upaspṛśed duriṣṭaṃ yajñasyāmuñcet tam abhimantrayeta vāyav eṣa te vāyav ity ekam | [ĀpŚS, 7, 28 4.3]
vāyav etau te vāyav iti dvau | [ĀpŚS, 7, 28 4.4]
vāyav ete te vāyav iti bahūn | [ĀpŚS, 7, 28 4.5]
aindrāgno nirūḍhapaśubandhaḥ sauryaḥ prājāpatyo vā | [ĀpŚS, 7, 28 5]
tena saṃvatsare saṃvatsare yajeta | [ĀpŚS, 7, 28 6.1]
ṣaṭsu ṣaṭsu māseṣv ity eke | [ĀpŚS, 7, 28 6.2]
ṛtuvyāvṛttau sūyavasa āvṛttimukha āvṛttimukhe vā | [ĀpŚS, 7, 28 7]
māṃsīyanti ha vā agnayo 'juhvato yajamānasya | [ĀpŚS, 7, 28 8.1]
te yajamānam eva dhyāyanti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 28 8.2]
yajamānaṃ saṃkalpayanti | [ĀpŚS, 7, 28 8.3]
pacanti ha vā anyeṣv agniṣu vṛthāmāṃsam | [ĀpŚS, 7, 28 8.4]
athaiteṣāṃ nānyā māṃsāśā vidyate | [ĀpŚS, 7, 28 8.5]
yasyo caite bhavanti taṃ tato nānījānaṃ paśunā saṃvatsaro 'tīyāt | [ĀpŚS, 7, 28 8.6]
āyuṣyo ha vā asyaiṣa ātmaniṣkrayaṇa iti vājasaneyakaṃ bhavati bhavati | [ĀpŚS, 7, 28 8.7]
{ĀpŚS, 13, 23}
prāyaṇīyāvad udayanīyā | [ĀpŚS, 13, 23 1]
tasyām eva sthālyām aniṣkasitāyāṃ śrapayati tad barhis tan mekṣaṇam | [ĀpŚS, 13, 23 2]
śālāmukhīye pracaranti | [ĀpŚS, 13, 23 3]
teṣv eva deśeṣv agnim ājyabhāgānāṃ prathamaṃ yajati pathyāṃ svastim uttamām | [ĀpŚS, 13, 23 4]
yāḥ prāyaṇīyasya yājyā ity uktam | [ĀpŚS, 13, 23 5]
maitrāvaruṇīṃ gāṃ vaśām anūbandhyām ālabhate | [ĀpŚS, 13, 23 6]
tasyā nirūḍhapaśubandhavatkalpaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 13, 23 7]
mitrāvaruṇābhyāṃ gor vapāyā medaso 'nubrūhi mitrāvaruṇābhyāṃ gor vapāyā medasaḥ preṣyeti saṃpraiṣau | [ĀpŚS, 13, 23 8]
evam avadāneṣu haviṣa ityantau namati | [ĀpŚS, 13, 23 9]
tisro 'nūbandhyā eke samāmananti | [ĀpŚS, 13, 23 10]

dvirūpā maitrāvaruṇī bahurūpā vaiśvadevī rohiṇī bārhaspatyā | [ĀpŚS, 13, 23 12]
upāṃśu vaiśvadevyā madhyataś caranti | [ĀpŚS, 13, 23 13]
tā na sarvatrālabheta vājapeye rājasūye sattre sahasre sarvavedase vā | [ĀpŚS, 13, 23 14]
yaḥ kāmayeta sarvo me yajñaḥ syāt sarasa iti sa etās tisro 'nūbandhyā ālabheta | [ĀpŚS, 13, 23 15]
anūbandhyāvapāyāṃ hutāyāṃ dakṣiṇe vedyante yajamānaḥ keśaśmaśru vāpayate | [ĀpŚS, 13, 23 16]
anūbandhyāyāḥ paśupuroḍāśam | [ĀpŚS, 13, 23 17]
{ĀpŚS, 16, 1}
agnim ceṣyamāṇaḥ amāvāsyāyām paurṇamāsyām ekāṣṭakāyām vā ukhām saṃbharati | [ĀpŚS, 16, 1 676263_1]
aṣāḍhām adhikṛtya eke samāmananti | [ĀpŚS, 16, 1 676264_1]
bṛhaspati purohitāḥ devāḥ devānām devāḥ devāḥ prathama jāḥ devāḥ deveṣu parākramadhvam prathamāḥ dvitīyeṣu dvitīyāḥ tṛtīyeṣu tris ekādaśāḥ tris trayastriṃśāḥ anu vaḥ ārabhe idam śakeyam yat idam karomi te mā avata te mā jinvata asmin brahman asmin kṣatre asyām āśiṣi asyām purodhāyām asmin karman asyām deva hūtyām iti caturgṛhītam juhoti | [ĀpŚS, 16, 1 676265_1]
juhūm sruvam ca saṃmṛjya juhvām aṣṭa gṛhītam gṛhītvā yuñjānaḥ prathamam manaḥ iti yajuḥ aṣṭamābhiḥ ṛgbhiḥ ekām āhutim juhoti antarvedi ūrdhvaḥ tiṣṭhan | [ĀpŚS, 16, 1 676266_1]
yam kāmayeta pāpīyān syāt iti ekaikam tasya juhuyāt jihmaḥ tiṣṭhan | [ĀpŚS, 16, 1 676267_1]
yadi kāmayeta chandāṃsi yajña yaśasena arpayeyam iti uktam | [ĀpŚS, 16, 1 676268_1]
ṛcā stomam samardhaya iti aparam caturgṛhītam gṛhītvā devasya tvā savituḥ prasave iti caturbhiḥ abhrim ādatte vaiṇavīm kalmāṣīm suṣirām asuṣirām vā ubhayataḥkṣṇūm anyatarataḥkṣṇūm vā prādeśa mātrīm aratni mātrīm vyāyāma mātrīm aparimitām vā khādirīm pālāśīm audumbarīm arka mayīm kārṣmarya mayīm vaikaṅkatīm śamī mayīm vā yaḥ vā yajñiyaḥ vṛkṣaḥ phalagrahiḥ | [ĀpŚS, 16, 1 676269_1]
{ĀpŚS, 16, 2}
imām agṛbhṇan raśanām ṛtasya iti aśvābhidhānīm raśanām ādāya pratūrtam vājin ā drava iti aśvam abhidadhāti tūṣṇīm gardabhasya ādāya yuñjāthām rāsabham yuvam iti gardabham | [ĀpŚS, 16, 2 676270_1]
yoge yoge tavastaram iti tisṛbhiḥ aśva prathamāḥ abhipravrajanti yatra mṛdam khaniṣyantaḥ syuḥ | [ĀpŚS, 16, 2 676272_1]
yadi kāmayeta pāpavasyasam syāt iti gardabha prathamāḥ gaccheyuḥ | [ĀpŚS, 16, 2 676273_1]
agnim purīṣyam aṅgirasvat acchehi iti japati | [ĀpŚS, 16, 2 676274_1]
agnim purīṣyam aṅgirasvat acchemaḥ iti yena dveṣyeṇa saṃgacchate tam abhimantrayate | [ĀpŚS, 16, 2 676275_1]
a paśyan nirdiśati | [ĀpŚS, 16, 2 676275_2]
agnim purīṣyam aṅgirasvat bhariṣyāmaḥ iti valmīka vapām ā sūryasya udetoḥ tām uddhatya upatiṣṭhate | [ĀpŚS, 16, 2 676276_1]
anu agniḥ uṣasām agram akhyat iti valmīka vapāyāḥ prakrāmati | [ĀpŚS, 16, 2 676277_1]
āgatya vājī adhvanaḥ ākramya vājin pṛthivīm iti dvābhyām mṛtkhanam aśvam ākramayya dyauḥ te pṛṣṭham iti aśvasya pṛṣṭham saṃmārṣṭi | [ĀpŚS, 16, 2 676278_1]
abhi tiṣṭha pṛtanyataḥ adhare santu śatravaḥ indraḥ iva vṛtrahā tiṣṭha apaḥ kṣetrāṇi saṃjayan abhiṣṭhitaḥ asi iti yam dveṣṭi tam adhaspadam aśvasya manasā dhyāyati | [ĀpŚS, 16, 2 676279_1]
utkrāma udakramīt iti dvābhyām mṛtkhanāt udañcam aśvam utkramayya apaḥ devīḥ upasṛja iti aśvasya pade apaḥ upasṛjya pade hiraṇyam nidhāya | [ĀpŚS, 16, 2 676280_1]
{ĀpŚS, 16, 3}
jigharmi agnim ā tvā jigharmi iti manasvatībhyām ekām āhutim hiraṇye hutvā apādāya hiraṇyam pari vāja patiḥ kaviḥ agniḥ iti tisṛbhiḥ abhryā mṛtkhanam parilikhati bāhyām bāhyām varṣīyasīm | [ĀpŚS, 16, 3 676281_1]
devasya tvā savituḥ prasave iti dvābhyām khanati | [ĀpŚS, 16, 3 676282_1]
apām pṛṣṭham asi iti puṣkara parṇam āhṛtya etayā eva viveṣṭya śarma ca sthaḥ varma ca stha iti dvābhyām uttareṇa mṛtkhanam kṛṣṇājinam prācīna grīvam uttara loma āstṛṇāti upariṣṭāt puṣkara parṇam uttānam | [ĀpŚS, 16, 3 676283_1]
purīṣyaḥ asi viśva bharāḥ iti mṛtkhanam abhimantrya tvām agne puṣkarāt adhi iti kṛṣṇājine puṣkara parṇe ca saṃbharati catasṛbhiḥ tisṛbhiḥ vā gāyatrībhiḥ brāhmaṇasya triṣṭubbhiḥ rājanyasya jagatībhiḥ vaiśyasya | [ĀpŚS, 16, 3 676284_1]
yam kāmayeta vasīyān syāt iti ubhayībhiḥ tasya saṃbharet | [ĀpŚS, 16, 3 676285_1]
aṣṭābhiḥ saṃbharati | [ĀpŚS, 16, 3 676286_1]
janiṣva hi jenya iti mṛdam abhimṛśya mṛtkhanam saṃlobhya sam te vāyuḥ iti mṛtkhane apaḥ ānīya samudyamya kṛṣṇājinasya antān su jātaḥ jyotiṣā saha iti kṣaumeṇa mauñjena arka mayeṇa vā dāmnā upanahyati | [ĀpŚS, 16, 3 676287_1]
ud u tiṣṭha su adhvara ūrdhvaḥ u su naḥ ūtaye iti sāvitrībhyām uttiṣṭhati | [ĀpŚS, 16, 3 676288_1]
sa jātaḥ garbhaḥ asi iti harati | [ĀpŚS, 16, 3 676289_1]
sthiraḥ bhava vīḍu aṅgaḥ iti gardabhasya pṛṣṭhe ādadhāti | [ĀpŚS, 16, 3 676290_1]
śivaḥ bhava prajābhyaḥ iti āhitam abhimantrayate | [ĀpŚS, 16, 3 676291_1]
praitu vājī kanikradat iti tisṛbhiḥ a tvaramāṇāḥ pratyāyanti | [ĀpŚS, 16, 3 676292_1]
agnim purīṣyam aṅgirasvat bharāmaḥ iti yena dveṣyeṇa saṃgacchate tam abhimantrayate | [ĀpŚS, 16, 3 676293_1]
a paśyan nirdiśati | [ĀpŚS, 16, 3 676293_2]
uttareṇa vihāram pariśrite oṣadhayaḥ prati gṛhṇīta agnim etam iti dvābhyām oṣadhīṣu puṣpavatīṣu phalavatīṣu upāvaharati | [ĀpŚS, 16, 3 676294_1]
{ĀpŚS, 16, 4}
vi pājasā iti visrasya āpaḥ hi ṣṭhā mayobhuvaḥ iti tisṛbhiḥ apaḥ upasṛjya mitraḥ saṃsṛjya pṛthivīm iti dvābhyām saṃsarjanīyaiḥ saṃsṛjati arma kapālaiḥ piṣṭaiḥ veṇu aṅgāraiḥ vrīhi tuṣaiḥ palāśa kaṣāyeṇa śarkarābhiḥ piṣṭābhiḥ kṛṣṇājina lomabhiḥ aja lomabhiḥ iti yat ca anyat dṛḍha arthe upa ardham manyate | [ĀpŚS, 16, 4 676295_1]
rudrāḥ saṃbhṛtya pṛthivīm iti mṛdam saṃkṣipya saṃsṛṣṭām vasubhiḥ iti tisṛbhiḥ kartre prayacchati | [ĀpŚS, 16, 4 676297_1]
makhasya śiraḥ asi iti piṇḍam kṛtvā yajñasya pade stha iti kṛṣṇājinam puṣkara parṇam ca abhimṛśati mṛdi vā aṅguṣṭhābhyām nigṛhṇāti | [ĀpŚS, 16, 4 676298_1]
vasavaḥ tvā kṛṇvantu gāyatreṇa chandasā iti caturbhiḥ mahiṣī ukhām karoti bahu bhāryasya adhvaryuḥ eka bhāryasya | [ĀpŚS, 16, 4 676299_1]
kriyamāṇām etaiḥ eva yajamānaḥ anumantrayate tri uddhim pañca uddhim aparimita uddhim vā catur aśrām parimaṇḍalām vā prādeśa mātrīm ūrdhva pramāṇena aratni mātrīm tiryak pramāṇena vyāyāma mātrīm samanta parimāṇena aparimitām vā | [ĀpŚS, 16, 4 676300_1]
pañca prādeśām iṣu mātrīm vā yadi pañca paśavaḥ bhavanti iti vājasaneyakam | [ĀpŚS, 16, 4 676302_1]
kurvan catasraḥ aśrīḥ pratidiśam unnayati aṣṭa aśrim vā | [ĀpŚS, 16, 4 676303_1]
nava aśrim abhicarataḥ kuryāt | [ĀpŚS, 16, 4 676305_1]
{ĀpŚS, 16, 5}
adityai rāsnā asi iti rāsnām karoti | [ĀpŚS, 16, 5 676306_1]
aśrīṇām rāsnāyāḥ ca saṃdhau dvau caturaḥ ṣaṭ aṣṭau vā stanān karoti | [ĀpŚS, 16, 5 676307_1]
aditiḥ te bilam gṛhṇātu iti bilam kṛtvā kṛtvāya sā mahīm ukhām iti uttaratas sikatāsu pratiṣṭhāpya mitra etām tam ukhām paridadāmi abhittyai eṣā mā bhedi iti mitrāya paridadāti | [ĀpŚS, 16, 5 676308_1]
yaḥ ukhām karoti saḥ aṣāḍhām etasyāḥ eva mṛdaḥ tūṣṇīm catur aśrām tri ālikhitām iṣṭakām | [ĀpŚS, 16, 5 676309_1]

{ĀpŚS, 16, 14}
apavṛtte dīkṣā parimāṇe apeta vīta iti gārhapatya citeḥ āyatanam vyāyāma mātram caturasram parimaṇḍalam vā uddhatya hariṇyā palāśa śākhayā śamī śākhayā vā saṃmṛjya prācīm udīcīm vā śākhām udasitvā śam naḥ devīḥ abhiṣṭaye iti adbhiḥ avokṣya agneḥ bhasma asi iti sikatāḥ nivapati saṃjñānam iti ūṣān | [ĀpŚS, 16, 14 676457_1]
tān nivapan yat adaḥ candramasi kṛṣṇam tat iha astu iti manasā dhyāyati | [ĀpŚS, 16, 14 676459_1]
sam yāḥ vaḥ priyāḥ tanuvaḥ iti ūṣān sikatāḥ ca saṃsṛjya citaḥ stha paricitaḥ iti ekaviṃśatyā śarkarābhiḥ gārhapatya citeḥ āyatanam pariśrayati | [ĀpŚS, 16, 14 676460_1]
tisraḥ tisraḥ saṃhitāḥ | [ĀpŚS, 16, 14 676461_1]
vrajam kṛṇudhvam sa hi vaḥ nṛpāṇaḥ varma sīvyadhvam bahulā pṛthūni puraḥ kṛṇudhvam āyasīḥ adhṛṣṭāḥ mā vaḥ susrot camasaḥ dṛṃhata tam iti śarkarāḥ abhimantrya ayam saḥ agniḥ iti catasraḥ madhye prācīḥ iṣṭakāḥ gārhapatya citau upadadhāti iḍām agne ayam te yoniḥ ṛtviyaḥ iti dve purastāt samīcī tiraścī vā | [ĀpŚS, 16, 14 676463_1]
evam paścāt cit asi paricit asi iti | [ĀpŚS, 16, 14 676465_1]
avaśiṣṭam trayodaśabhiḥ lokaṃpṛṇābhiḥ pracchādayati | [ĀpŚS, 16, 14 676466_1]
lokam pṛṇa tāḥ asya sūdadohasaḥ iti dvābhyām dvābhyām mantrābhyām ekaikām lokaṃpṛṇām upadadhāti | [ĀpŚS, 16, 14 676467_1]
sarvāsu iṣṭakāsu tayādevatam antatas dadhāti | [ĀpŚS, 16, 14 676468_1]
{ĀpŚS, 16, 15}
cātvālasthānāt purīṣam āhṛtya pṛṣṭo divīti vaiśvānaryarcā citāv anuvyūhati | [ĀpŚS, 16, 15 1.1]
sā citir bhavati | [ĀpŚS, 16, 15 2.1]
pañcacitīkaṃ cinvīta prathamaṃ cinvānaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 16, 15 3.1]
tricitīkaṃ dvitīyam | [ĀpŚS, 16, 15 3.2]
ekacitīkaṃ tṛtīyam | [ĀpŚS, 16, 15 3.3]
ekacitīkān evāta ūrdhvaṃ cinvīta | [ĀpŚS, 16, 15 4.1]
ajījanann amṛtaṃ martyāsa iti gārhapatyacitim abhimṛśya samitam iti tasyāṃ catasṛbhir ukhyaṃ saṃnivapati | [ĀpŚS, 16, 15 5.1]
vijñāyate ca vi vā etau dviṣāte yaś cokhāyāṃ yaś ca cīyate | [ĀpŚS, 16, 15 6.1]
brahma yajuḥ | [ĀpŚS, 16, 15 6.2]
yat saṃnyupya viharati brahmaṇaivainau saṃśāstīti | [ĀpŚS, 16, 15 6.3]
sākaṃ hi śucinā śuciḥ praśāstā kratunājani | [ĀpŚS, 16, 15 7.1]
vidvāṁ asya vratā dhruvā vayā ivānurohata iti saṃnyuptāv abhimantrya māteva putram iti śikyād ukhāṃ nirūhya yad asya pāre rajasa iti vaiśvānaryā śikyam ādatte | [ĀpŚS, 16, 15 7.2]
nairṛtīr iṣṭakāḥ kṛṣṇās tisras tuṣapakvās tāḥ śikyaṃ rukmasūtram āsandīṃ cādāya dakṣiṇam aparam avāntaradeśaṃ gatvā namaḥ su te nirṛta iti svakṛta iriṇe pradare vā śikyaṃ nidhāya tasyeṣṭakābhiḥ pāśam abhyupadadhāti | [ĀpŚS, 16, 15 8.1]
yasyās te asyāḥ krūra āsañ juhomīty etābhis tisṛbhiḥ parācīr asaṃspṛṣṭā dakṣiṇāpavargam | [ĀpŚS, 16, 15 9.1]
na tayādevataṃ karoti | [ĀpŚS, 16, 15 10.1]
{ĀpŚS, 16, 16}
yat te devī nirṛtir ābabandheti śikyajālenaināḥ pracchādya rukmasūtram āsandīṃ ca parastān nidhāyāpāsmad etu nirṛtir nehāsyā api kiṃcana | [ĀpŚS, 16, 16 1.1]
agotāṃ nāṣṭrāṃ pāpmānaṃ sarvaṃ tad apahanmahe | [ĀpŚS, 16, 16 1.2]
apāsman nairṛtān pāśān mṛtyūn ekaśataṃ caye | [ĀpŚS, 16, 16 1.3]
apāsya ye sināḥ pāśā mṛtyūn ekaśataṃ suve | [ĀpŚS, 16, 16 1.4]
ye te pāśā ekaśataṃ mṛtyo martyāya hantave | [ĀpŚS, 16, 16 1.5]
tān yajñasya māyayā sarvān avayajāmahe | [ĀpŚS, 16, 16 1.6]
devīm ahaṃ nirṛtiṃ bādhamānaḥ piteva putraṃ dasaye vacobhiḥ | [ĀpŚS, 16, 16 1.7]
viśvasya yā jāyamānasya veda śiraḥ śiraḥ prati sūrī vicaṣṭa ity etābhiś catasṛbhir upahitā abhimantrya yad asya pāre rajasa iti vaiśvānaryā pariṣicya bhūtyai nama ity upasthāyāpratīkṣam āyanti | [ĀpŚS, 16, 16 1.8]
nirṛtyā antarhityā iti vijñāyate | [ĀpŚS, 16, 16 2.1]
śaṃ no devīr abhiṣṭaya ity adbhir mārjayante | [ĀpŚS, 16, 16 3.1]
ūrjaṃ bibhrad vasumanāḥ sumedhā gṛhān aimi manasā modamānaḥ suvarcāḥ | [ĀpŚS, 16, 16 4.1]
aghoreṇa cakṣuṣāhaṃ śivena gṛhāṇāṃ paśyan vaya uttirāṇi | [ĀpŚS, 16, 16 4.2]
gṛhāṇām āyuḥ pra vayaṃ tirāmo gṛhā asmākaṃ pra tirantv āyuḥ | [ĀpŚS, 16, 16 4.3]
gṛhān ahaṃ sumanasaḥ prapadye 'vīraghno vīravataḥ suvīrān iti gṛhān abhyeti | [ĀpŚS, 16, 16 4.4]
niveśanaḥ saṃgamano vasūnām ity āhavanīyaṃ gārhapatyaṃ vopatiṣṭhante | [ĀpŚS, 16, 16 5.1]
{ĀpŚS, 16, 17}
rājño nivapanādi karma pratipadyate | [ĀpŚS, 16, 17 1.1]
prāyaṇīyayā pracarya vediṃ vimimīte | [ĀpŚS, 16, 17 2.1]
haviṣkṛtā vācaṃ visṛjyeti vājasaneyakam | [ĀpŚS, 16, 17 3.1]

haviṣkṛtā vācaṃ visṛjyeti vājasaneyakam | [ĀpŚS, 16, 17 6.1]

ātmā catuḥpuruṣaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 16, 17 11.1]
aratninā dakṣiṇato dakṣiṇaṃ pakṣaṃ pravardhayati | [ĀpŚS, 16, 17 12.1]
evam uttarata uttaram | [ĀpŚS, 16, 17 13.1]
prādeśena vitastyā vā paścāt puccham | [ĀpŚS, 16, 17 14.1]

{ĀpŚS, 16, 18}
saṃ varatrā dadhātaneti saṃpreṣyati | [ĀpŚS, 16, 18 1.1]

ud yojanam antaryāmam īṣāṃ khagalyaṃ śapham | [ĀpŚS, 16, 18 4.1]

malimluco nāmāsi trayodaśo māsa indrasya varmāsīndrasya śarmāsīndrasya varūtham asi taṃ tvā prapadye | [ĀpŚS, 16, 18 9.1]
{ĀpŚS, 16, 19}
gāyatrīṃ lomabhiḥ praviśāmi | [ĀpŚS, 16, 19 1.1]

{ĀpŚS, 16, 20}
yām oṣadhīnāṃ nādhigacchet tasyāḥ sthāne sthāne yavān madhumiśrān vapet | [ĀpŚS, 16, 20 1.1]
uptā me 'sīti vā manasā dhyāyet | [ĀpŚS, 16, 20 2.1]
adhigatāyāṃ yaḥ prathama idhma āgacchet tasminn enām upasaṃnahyet | [ĀpŚS, 16, 20 3.1]
ye vanaspatīnāṃ phalagrahayas tān idhma upasaṃnahya prokṣet | [ĀpŚS, 16, 20 4.1]
mā no hiṃsīj janitā yaḥ pṛthivyā iti catasṛbhir digbhyo loṣṭān samasyati ye 'ntarvidhād bahirvidham āpannā bhavanti | [ĀpŚS, 16, 20 5.1]
yaṃ dviṣyād yatra sa syāt tasyai diśo jaghanyaṃ loṣṭam āhared iṣam ūrjam aham ita ādada iti | [ĀpŚS, 16, 20 6.1]
ghṛtena sīteti sītāntarālāny abhimṛśati | [ĀpŚS, 16, 20 7.1]
uttaravediṃ vā | [ĀpŚS, 16, 20 7.2]
uttaravedim upavapati yāvān agniḥ | [ĀpŚS, 16, 20 8.1]
vyāghāraṇāntāṃ kṛtvāgne tava śravo vaya iti ṣaḍbhiḥ sikatā nyupya cita stha paricita ity aparimitābhiḥ śarkarābhir āhavanīyaciter āyatanaṃ pariśrayati yathā gārhapatyasyaivam | [ĀpŚS, 16, 20 9.1]
trisaptābhiḥ paśukāmasya | [ĀpŚS, 16, 20 10.1]

daśabhirdaśabhir annādyakāmasya | [ĀpŚS, 16, 20 10.3]
aparimitābhir aparimitakāmasya | [ĀpŚS, 16, 20 10.4]
yaṃ kāmayetāpaśuḥ syād ity aparimitya tasyety uktam | [ĀpŚS, 16, 20 11.1]
āpyāyasva sametu ta iti sikatā vyūhati | [ĀpŚS, 16, 20 12.1]
uttarayā triṣṭubhā rājanyasya | [ĀpŚS, 16, 20 13.1]

{ĀpŚS, 16, 21}
ātithyāyā dhrauvād ity etadādi karma pratipadyate | [ĀpŚS, 16, 21 1.1]
paurvāhṇikībhyāṃ pracaryāgreṇa prāgvaṃśaṃ lohite carmaṇy ānaḍuhe prācīnagrīva uttaralomni prathamasyāś citer iṣṭakāḥ saṃsādayati | [ĀpŚS, 16, 21 2.1]
api vā tisraḥ svayamātṛṇṇās tisraś ca viśvajyotiṣaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 16, 21 2.2]
tā darbhāgramuṣṭinājyena vyavokṣya samudyamya cityagnibhyaḥ praṇīyamānebhyo 'nubrūhīti saṃpreṣyati | [ĀpŚS, 16, 21 3.1]

śvetam aśvaṃ purastān nayanti | [ĀpŚS, 16, 21 5.1]
prajāpatis tvā sādayatu tayā devatayāṅgirasvad dhruvā sīdety uttaravedim abhimṛśya mayi gṛhṇāmy agre agniṃ yo no agniḥ pitara iti dvābhyām ātmann agniṃ gṛhītvā yās te agne samidha iti svayaṃcityābhimṛśati | [ĀpŚS, 16, 21 6.1]
iṣṭakābhir agniṃ cinoty adhvaryur yajamāno vā | [ĀpŚS, 16, 21 7.1]

tam ālabhyendraṃ viśvā avīvṛdhann ity uttareṇa pucchāpyayam antarvidha ākramaṇaṃ pratīṣṭakām upadadhyāt | [ĀpŚS, 16, 21 12.1]
uttarataḥ paścād vopacāro 'gniḥ | [ĀpŚS, 16, 21 13.1]
