sakṛd vāntataḥ | [ĀpŚS, 16, 21 14.2]
{ĀpŚS, 16, 22}
tat tvā yāmi brahmaṇā vandamāna iti śālāmukhīye hutvā prāñcam aśvam abhy asthād viśvā iti dakṣiṇena padā darbhastambam ākramayya pradakṣiṇam āvartayitvā yad akranda iti punar evākramayati | [ĀpŚS, 16, 22 1.1]
apāṃ pṛṣṭham asīty aśvasya pade puṣkaraparṇam uttānam upadhāyāpāṃ nidhiṃ gāyeti saṃpreṣyati | [ĀpŚS, 16, 22 2.1]
brahma jajñānam iti puṣkaraparṇa upariṣṭān nirbādhaṃ rukmam upadhāya hiraṇyagarbhaḥ samavartatāgra iti tasmin hiraṇmayaṃ puruṣaṃ prācīnam uttānaṃ dakṣiṇenātṛṇṇaṃ prāṅmukha upadhāya puruṣasāma gāyeti saṃpreṣyati | [ĀpŚS, 16, 22 3.1]
drapsaś caskandeti puruṣam abhimṛśya namo astu sarpebhya iti tisṛbhir abhimantrya kṛṇuṣva pāja iti pañcabhir uttaravedivat puruṣaṃ vyāghārya srucāv upadadhātīty uktam | [ĀpŚS, 16, 22 4.1]
api vāgnes tvā tejasā sādayāmīty ājyasya pūrṇāṃ kārṣmaryamayīṃ dakṣiṇena puruṣam | [ĀpŚS, 16, 22 5.1]
indrasya tvaujasā sādayāmīti dadhnaḥ pūrṇām audumbarīm uttareṇa puruṣam | [ĀpŚS, 16, 22 5.2]
agnir mūrdheti kārṣmaryamayīm upatiṣṭhate | [ĀpŚS, 16, 22 6.1]
bhuvo yajñasyety audumbarīm | [ĀpŚS, 16, 22 6.2]

{ĀpŚS, 16, 23}
dhruvāsi dharuṇāstṛteti svayamātṛṇṇām abhimṛśyāśvenopaghrāpya prajāpatis tvā sādayatu pṛthivyāḥ pṛṣṭha ity aviduṣā brāhmaṇena saha madhye 'gner upadadhāti | [ĀpŚS, 16, 23 1.1]
bhūr iti caitayā vyāhṛtyā | [ĀpŚS, 16, 23 1.2]
cittiṃ juhomīti svayamātṛṇṇāyāṃ hutvānuprāṇiti | [ĀpŚS, 16, 23 2.1]
avidvān brāhmaṇo varaṃ dadāty ekaṃ dvau trīn vā | [ĀpŚS, 16, 23 3.1]
āsīnaḥ prathamāṃ svayamātṛṇṇām upadadhāti | [ĀpŚS, 16, 23 4.1]
ūrdhvajñur dvitīyām | [ĀpŚS, 16, 23 4.2]
tiṣṭhaṃs tṛtīyām | [ĀpŚS, 16, 23 4.3]
svayamātṛṇṇāyāṃ sāma gāyeti saṃpreṣyati | [ĀpŚS, 16, 23 5.1]
evaṃ dvitīyāṃ tṛtīyāṃ copadhāya saṃpreṣyati | [ĀpŚS, 16, 23 6.1]
yadi manyeta yajamānaḥ pūrvo mātikrānto bhrātṛvya iti pratho 'sīty upahitāṃ prācīm udūhet | [ĀpŚS, 16, 23 7.1]
yadi vāparaḥ pṛthivy asīti pratīcīm | [ĀpŚS, 16, 23 7.2]
sadṛṅ yadi bhūr asi bhuvanam asīti vicālayet | [ĀpŚS, 16, 23 7.3]
tejo 'si tejo me yaccheti hiraṇyeṣṭakām | [ĀpŚS, 16, 23 8.1]
pṛthivy udapuram anneneti maṇḍaleṣṭakām | [ĀpŚS, 16, 23 9.1]
bhūr asi bhuvanasya retaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 16, 23 10.1]
iṣṭakā svargo lokaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 16, 23 10.2]
vācā tvānvārohāmi | [ĀpŚS, 16, 23 10.3]
agnir jyotir jyotir agniḥ | [ĀpŚS, 16, 23 10.4]
tayā devatayāṅgirasvad dhruvā sīda | [ĀpŚS, 16, 23 10.5]
sūr asi suvanasya retaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 16, 23 10.6]
iṣṭakā svargo lokaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 16, 23 10.7]
manasā tvānvārohāmi | [ĀpŚS, 16, 23 10.8]
sūryo jyotir jyotiḥ sūryaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 16, 23 10.9]
tayā devatayāṅgirasvad dhruvā sīdety anvārohe dve | [ĀpŚS, 16, 23 10.10]
{ĀpŚS, 16, 24}
kāṇḍāt kāṇḍāt prarohantīti dvābhyāṃ dūrveṣṭakāṃ saloṣṭaṃ haritaṃ dūrvāstambam apracchinnāgraṃ yathāsyopahitasya svayamātṛṇṇāyām agraṃ prāpnuyād iti | [ĀpŚS, 16, 24 1.1]
prabāhug iṣṭakāyāṃ hiraṇyaśakalāv adhyūhya yās te agne sūrye ruca iti dvābhyāṃ vāmabhṛtam | [ĀpŚS, 16, 24 2.1]
virāḍ jyotir iti tisro retaḥsicaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 16, 24 3.1]

sarvā madhyamāyām vivayasaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 16, 24 4.2]
ekāṃ prathamāyām ekām uttamāyāṃ sthavirasya | [ĀpŚS, 16, 24 4.3]
anyatarām upadadhyād dveṣyasya | [ĀpŚS, 16, 24 5.1]
yajuṣemāṃ cāmūṃ copadadhāti | [ĀpŚS, 16, 24 6.1]
manasā madhyamām | [ĀpŚS, 16, 24 6.2]
bṛhaspatis tvā sādayatu pṛthivyāḥ pṛṣṭhe jyotiṣmatīm iti viśvajyotiṣam | [ĀpŚS, 16, 24 7.1]
agner yāny asīti dve saṃyānyau | [ĀpŚS, 16, 24 8.1]

avakāsu sādayatīty eke | [ĀpŚS, 16, 24 11.1]
aṣāḍhāsīti dvābhyām aṣāḍhām upariṣṭāllakṣmāṇam | [ĀpŚS, 16, 24 12.1]
yaṃ kāmayeta vasīyānt syād ity uttaralakṣmāṇaṃ tasyety uktam | [ĀpŚS, 16, 24 13.1]
gharmeṣṭakām upadhāya kulāyinīm | [ĀpŚS, 16, 24 14.1]
tayoḥ pravargye mantrau | [ĀpŚS, 16, 24 15.1]
{ĀpŚS, 16, 25}
madhu vātā ṛtāyata iti tisṛbhir dadhnā madhumiśreṇa kūrmam abhyajya mahī dyauḥ pṛthivī ca na iti purastāt svayamātṛṇṇāyāḥ pratyañcaṃ jīvantaṃ prāṅmukha upadadhāti | [ĀpŚS, 16, 25 1.1]
catasra āśāḥ pracarantv agnaya iti vopadhāyāvakābhiḥ parītasya jālena pracchādya śaṅkubhiḥ pariṇihatyāpāṃ gambhīraṃ gaccha mā tvā sūryaḥ parītāpsīn mo agnir vaiśvānaraḥ | [ĀpŚS, 16, 25 2.1]
aghoraḥ prajā abhivipaśyānu tvā divyā vṛṣṭiḥ sacatām | [ĀpŚS, 16, 25 2.2]

{ĀpŚS, 16, 26}
yacciddhi tvaṃ gṛhe gṛha ulūkhalaka yujyase | [ĀpŚS, 16, 26 1.1]
iha dyumattamaṃ vada jayatām iva dundubhir iti prādeśamātraṃ catuḥsrakty audumbaram ulūkhalam uttare 'ṃse prayunakti | [ĀpŚS, 16, 26 1.2]
aparimitaṃ musalam | [ĀpŚS, 16, 26 2.1]
uta sma te vanaspate vāto vi vāty agram it | [ĀpŚS, 16, 26 3.1]
atho indrāya pātave sunu somam ulūkhaleti sarvauṣadhasya pūrayitvāvahaty edaṃ viṣṇur vicakrama iti madhye 'gner upadadhāti | [ĀpŚS, 16, 26 3.2]
tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam iti musalam | [ĀpŚS, 16, 26 4.1]
divo vā viṣṇav iti śūrpam | [ĀpŚS, 16, 26 5.1]
syūtā devebhir amṛtenāgā ukhāṃ svasāram adhi vedim asthāt | [ĀpŚS, 16, 26 6.1]

dadhnā madhunā sikatābhir vā sarvair vā | [ĀpŚS, 16, 26 6.3]
saṃsṛjya na riktām avekṣeta | [ĀpŚS, 16, 26 7.1]
śugviddhā bhavati | [ĀpŚS, 16, 26 7.2]
athāsyāṃ paya ānayati | [ĀpŚS, 16, 26 8.1]
saṃnyupya pūraṇam eke samāmananti | [ĀpŚS, 16, 26 9.1]
yaṃ kāmayeta kṣodhukaḥ syād ity ūnāṃ tasyety uktam | [ĀpŚS, 16, 26 10.1]
dhruvāsi pṛthivīti madhye 'gner upadadhāti | [ĀpŚS, 16, 26 11.1]
pṛthivi pṛthivyāṃ sīda mātā mātari mātā syonā syonāyām ukhāṃ svasāram adhi vedim asthāt | [ĀpŚS, 16, 26 12.1]

agne yukṣvā hi ye tava yukṣvā hi devahūtamān iti dvābhyām ukhāyāṃ hutvā puruṣaśirasi hiraṇyaśalkān pratyasyati | [ĀpŚS, 16, 26 13.1]
{ĀpŚS, 16, 27}
drapsaś caskandety āsye | [ĀpŚS, 16, 27 1.1]
abhūd idaṃ viśvasya bhuvanasyeti vā | [ĀpŚS, 16, 27 1.2]
ṛce tveti dakṣiṇe 'kṣikaṭe | [ĀpŚS, 16, 27 2.1]
ruce tveti savye | [ĀpŚS, 16, 27 2.2]

jyotiṣe tvety uttarasyām | [ĀpŚS, 16, 27 4.2]

ajā hy agner iti bastasya | [ĀpŚS, 16, 27 18.1]

api vā tasya tasya sthāna upadhāya tasya tasyotsargeṇopatiṣṭhate | [ĀpŚS, 16, 27 20.1]
yaṃ kāmayeta kanīyo 'syānnaṃ syād iti saṃtarāṃ tasyety uktam | [ĀpŚS, 16, 27 21.1]

api vā yajur eva vaden nopadadhyāt | [ĀpŚS, 16, 27 23.1]
{ĀpŚS, 16, 28}
mā chandas tat pṛthivy agnir devatā tenarṣiṇā tena brahmaṇā tayā devatayāṅgirasvad dhruvā sīda | [ĀpŚS, 16, 28 1.1]

puruṣaśiro 'syāḥ śiro bhavati | [ĀpŚS, 16, 28 2.1]
sahasraśīrṣā puruṣa ity upahitāṃ puruṣeṇa nārāyaṇena yajamāna upatiṣṭhate | [ĀpŚS, 16, 28 3.1]
apasyā upadadhāti | [ĀpŚS, 16, 28 4.1]

{ĀpŚS, 16, 29}
ye yajñaṃ samagṛbhṇan devā devebhyas pari | [ĀpŚS, 16, 29 1.1]

tenaitu yajamānaḥ svastyā divo 'dhi pṛṣṭham asthād iti pañca hiraṇyeṣṭakāḥ pratidiśam | [ĀpŚS, 16, 29 1.10]
ekāṃ madhye | [ĀpŚS, 16, 29 1.11]
āyave svāhāyoṣkṛte svāhāyoṣpatvane svāhā viṣṇave svāhā bṛhaspataye svāheti pañcopadhāyādbhyaḥ sambhūtaḥ pṛthivyai rasāc ca viśvakarmaṇaḥ samavartatādhi | [ĀpŚS, 16, 29 2.1]
tasya tvaṣṭā vidadhad rūpam eti tat puruṣasya viśvam ājānam agra ity etām upadhāyartasad asi satyasad asi tejaḥsad asi varcaḥsad asi yaśaḥsad asi gṛṇānāsi | [ĀpŚS, 16, 29 2.2]

{ĀpŚS, 16, 30}
gūrdo 'si gūrdāya tvā gūrdebhyas tvā gūrde sīda | [ĀpŚS, 16, 30 1.1]

{ĀpŚS, 16, 31}

{ĀpŚS, 16, 32}

{ĀpŚS, 16, 33}

trayastriṃśaṃ te agne pratiṣṭhānaṃ tan me agne pratiṣṭhānam ity etāḥ śirasi pakṣayor madhye pucche vopadadhāti | [ĀpŚS, 16, 33 5.6]
trivṛt te agne śiras tena mā pāhīti saṃnamayaṃs tāṃ tām upatiṣṭhate yajamānaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 16, 33 6.1]
tvām agne vṛṣabham ity ṛṣabham upadhāya lokaṃ pṛṇa tā asya sūdadohasa ity aviśiṣṭam aparimitābhir lokaṃpṛṇābhiḥ pracchādayati | [ĀpŚS, 16, 33 7.1]
sarvān varṇān iṣṭakānāṃ kuryād iti | [ĀpŚS, 16, 33 8.1]
{ĀpŚS, 16, 34}
lekhādhikāro bhavati vijñāyate ca | [ĀpŚS, 16, 34 1.1]

{ĀpŚS, 16, 35}
yo apsv antar agnir yo vṛtre yaḥ puruṣe yo aśmani | [ĀpŚS, 16, 35 1.1]

{ĀpŚS, 17, 12}

tūṣṇīm itarān ṣoḍaśa rathān | [ĀpŚS, 18, 3 3.2]
dakṣiṇākāle saptadaśa rathān dadāti | [ĀpŚS, 18, 3 4.1]
saptadaśānāṃsi saptadaśāśvān saptadaśa hastinaḥ saptadaśa niṣkān saptadaśa dāsyaḥ saptadaśājāḥ saptadaśāvīḥ saptadaśa vāsāṃsi saptadaśa gavāṃ śatāni | [ĀpŚS, 18, 3 4.2]
athaikeṣām | [ĀpŚS, 18, 3 5.1]
saptadaśa gavāṃ śatāni dadāti | [ĀpŚS, 18, 3 5.2]
saptadaśānāṃsi yuktāni saptadaśāśvarathān saptadaśa hastinaḥ saptadaśa niṣkān saptadaśa dāsyaḥ saptadaśa dundubhīn | [ĀpŚS, 18, 3 5.3]
eṣa āpto vājapeyaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 18, 3 6.1]
atha kuruvājapeyaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 18, 3 7.1]
vayaso vayasaḥ saptadaśa saptadaśāni dadāti | [ĀpŚS, 18, 3 8.1]
ekahāyanaprabhṛty ā pañcahāyanebhyo vayāṃsi | [ĀpŚS, 18, 3 9.1]
anudiṣṭāsu dakṣiṇāsu yajuryuktam adhvaryave dadāti | [ĀpŚS, 18, 3 10.1]
śeṣaḥ sādhāraṇaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 18, 3 11.1]
agreṇāhavanīyam udīcaḥ prāco vā rathān avasthāpayanti | [ĀpŚS, 18, 3 12.1]
teṣāṃ dakṣiṇo yajuryuktaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 18, 3 13.1]
agreṇāgnīdhraṃ rājaputro 'vasthāya saptadaśa pravyādhān iṣum asyati | [ĀpŚS, 18, 3 14.1]
yatra jaghanyaṃ nipatati tatraudumbarīṃ kāṣṭhāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ minoti | [ĀpŚS, 18, 3 15.1]
{ĀpŚS, 18, 4}
prāṅ māhendrāt kṛtvā naivāre sarpir ānīya cātvāle 'vadadhāti | [ĀpŚS, 18, 4 1]
taṃ rājaputro gopāyati | [ĀpŚS, 18, 4 2]
cātvāle rathākṣākṛti kāṣṭhaṃ nikhāya tasminn audumbaraṃ rathacakraṃ saptadaśāraṃ pratimuñcati | [ĀpŚS, 18, 4 3]
uttarasyāṃ vediśroṇyāṃ saptadaśa dundubhīn prabadhnanti | [ĀpŚS, 18, 4 4]
viṣṇoḥ kramo 'sīti rathaṃ yajamāno 'bhyaiti | [ĀpŚS, 18, 4 5]
aṅkau nyaṅkāv iti rathacakre abhimṛśati pakṣasī vā | [ĀpŚS, 18, 4 6]
indrāya vācaṃ vadateti dundubhīn saṃhrādayanti | [ĀpŚS, 18, 4 7]
devasyāhaṃ savituḥ prasave bṛhaspatinā vājajitā vājaṃ jeṣam ity audumbaraṃ rathacakraṃ brahmārohati | [ĀpŚS, 18, 4 8]
tam āha vājināṃ sāma gāyeti | [ĀpŚS, 18, 4 9]
tasya cakraṃ triḥ pradakṣiṇam āvartayati | [ĀpŚS, 18, 4 10]
vartamāne brahmā gāyati | [ĀpŚS, 18, 4 11]
devasyāhaṃ savituḥ prasave bṛhaspatinā vājajitā varṣiṣṭhaṃ nākaṃ ruheyam iti yajuryuktaṃ yajamāna ārohati | [ĀpŚS, 18, 4 12]
vājasṛta itarān rathān | [ĀpŚS, 18, 4 13]
vājino vājajito vājaṃ sariṣyanto vājaṃ jeṣyanto bṛhaspater bhāgam avajighrateti naivāram aśvau dhuryāv avaghrāpayati sarvān vā | [ĀpŚS, 18, 4 14]
bṛhaspater bhāge ni mṛḍḍhvam iti praprotheṣu ca lepān nimārṣṭi | [ĀpŚS, 18, 4 15]
aśvājanīty aśvājanīm ādāyādhvaryur yajuryuktam adhiruhyārvāsi saptir asīti tayāśvān samavakṣiṇoti | [ĀpŚS, 18, 4 16]
anabhyāsādayanta itare rathāḥ paścād anuyānti | [ĀpŚS, 18, 4 17]
vājino vājaṃ dhāvateti catasṛbhir dhāvato 'numantrayate | [ĀpŚS, 18, 4 18]
agnir ekākṣareṇeti dhāvatsūjjitīr yajamānaṃ vācayati | [ĀpŚS, 18, 4 19]
lakṣaṇaṃ prāpyodañca āvṛtya pradakṣiṇam āvartayante | [ĀpŚS, 18, 4 20]
mitadrava iti catasṛbhiḥ pratyādhāvato 'numantrayate | [ĀpŚS, 18, 4 21]
{ĀpŚS, 18, 5}
ā mā vājasya prasavo jagamyād iti pratyāsṛteṣu hutvā punar naivāram avaghrāpayati | [ĀpŚS, 18, 5 1.1]
sasṛvāṃsa iti lepāṃś ca nimārṣṭi | [ĀpŚS, 18, 5 1.2]
iyaṃ vaḥ sā satyā saṃdhābhūd iti dundubhivimocanīyaṃ homaṃ juhoti | [ĀpŚS, 18, 5 2.1]
sevān vopaspṛśati | [ĀpŚS, 18, 5 3.1]
kṛṣṇalaṃ kṛṣṇalaṃ vājasṛdbhyaḥ prayacchati | [ĀpŚS, 18, 5 4.1]
tāni pratyādāya brahmaṇe dadāti | [ĀpŚS, 18, 5 5.1]
madhuṣṭhālaṃ ca sauvarṇaṃ śatamānasya kṛtam | [ĀpŚS, 18, 5 5.2]
atra māhendrasya stotram upākaroti | [ĀpŚS, 18, 5 6.1]
aprastute kṣatrasyolbam asīti tārpyaṃ yajamānaḥ paridhatte | [ĀpŚS, 18, 5 7.1]
kṣatrasya yonir asīti darbhamayaṃ patnī | [ĀpŚS, 18, 5 8.1]
jāya ehīti yajamānaḥ patnīm āmantrayate | [ĀpŚS, 18, 5 9.1]
rohāva hītītarā pratyāha | [ĀpŚS, 18, 5 10.1]
trir āmantrayate | [ĀpŚS, 18, 5 11.1]
triḥ pratyāha | [ĀpŚS, 18, 5 11.2]
ahaṃ nāv ubhayoḥ suvo rokṣyāmīti yajamāno 'ntataḥ | [ĀpŚS, 18, 5 12.1]
vājaś ca prasavaś ceti dvādaśa vājaprasavīyān homān hutvāyur yajñena kalpatām iti daśabhiḥ kalpaiḥ sarajase niśrayaṇyā yūpaṃ yajamāna ārohati | [ĀpŚS, 18, 5 13.1]
suvar devāṁ aganmety agraṃ prāpya japati | [ĀpŚS, 18, 5 14.1]
sam ahaṃ prajayā saṃ mayā prajeti gṛhān prekṣate | [ĀpŚS, 18, 5 15.1]
tam āśvatthair āsapuṭair ūṣapuṭair ubhayair vā vaiśyāḥ pratidiśam arpayanti | [ĀpŚS, 18, 5 16.1]
mahartvijo vā dīrghavaṃśeṣu prabadhya | [ĀpŚS, 18, 5 16.2]
annāya tveti purastād adhvaryuḥ | [ĀpŚS, 18, 5 17.1]
annādyāya tveti dakṣiṇato brahmā | [ĀpŚS, 18, 5 17.2]
vājāya tveti paścāddhotā | [ĀpŚS, 18, 5 17.3]
vājajityāyai tvety uttarata udgātā | [ĀpŚS, 18, 5 17.4]
mukhato 'bhighnanti | [ĀpŚS, 18, 5 18.1]
hantāraṃ hantāram abhiparyāvartate | [ĀpŚS, 18, 5 19.1]
iyaṃ te rāṇ mitrāya yantrāya dhartrāya kṛṣyai kṣemāya rayyai poṣāyeti pratyavarohati | [ĀpŚS, 18, 5 20.1]
agreṇa yūpaṃ bastājinaṃ prācīnagrīvam uttaralomāstīrya | [ĀpŚS, 18, 5 21.1]
{ĀpŚS, 18, 6}
tasmiñchatamānaṃ hiraṇyaṃ nidhāyāmṛtaṃ asīti hiraṇye dakṣiṇaṃ pādaṃ yajamānaḥ pratiṣṭhāpayate | [ĀpŚS, 18, 6 1.1]
puṣṭir asi prajananam asīti bastājine savyam | [ĀpŚS, 18, 6 2.1]
tasmād āsandīm ārohati | [ĀpŚS, 18, 6 3.1]
divaṃ proṣṭhinīm āroha tām āruhya prapaśyaikarāṇ manuṣyāṇām ity ārohantam abhimantrayate | [ĀpŚS, 18, 6 4.1]
saptabhiḥ sapta pūrvān annahomāñ juhoti | [ĀpŚS, 18, 6 5.1]
māhendrasya stotraṃ pratyabhiṣicyate yathāgnicityāyām | [ĀpŚS, 18, 6 6.1]

teṣām anabhighāritābhir vapābhiḥ pracarati | [ĀpŚS, 18, 6 8.1]

sārasvatasya paśupuroḍāśena pracarya naivāreṇa pracarati | [ĀpŚS, 18, 6 10.1]
samānaṃ tu sviṣṭakṛdiḍam | [ĀpŚS, 18, 6 11.1]
mahartvijo havirucchiṣṭāśā bhavanti | [ĀpŚS, 18, 6 12.1]
āgnīdhre haviḥśeṣān bhakṣayanti | [ĀpŚS, 18, 6 13.1]
atra sārasvatyantānāṃ daivatena pracarati saṃvādādy eḍāyāḥ | [ĀpŚS, 18, 6 14.1]
kāle vā | [ĀpŚS, 18, 6 14.2]
ṣoḍaśinā pracarya hotṛcamasamukhyāṃś camasān unnīya bṛhataḥ stotram upākaroti | [ĀpŚS, 18, 6 15.1]
pracaraṇakāle hotṛcamasam adhvaryur ādatte | [ĀpŚS, 18, 6 16.1]
camasāṃś camasādhvaryavaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 18, 6 16.2]
ṛtvija itarān somagrahān | [ĀpŚS, 18, 6 16.3]

vājasṛta itarān surāgrahān | [ĀpŚS, 18, 6 17.2]
{ĀpŚS, 18, 7}
saṃpṛca stha saṃ mā bhadreṇa pṛṅkteti prāṅ adhvaryuḥ somagrahair uddravati | [ĀpŚS, 18, 7 1.1]
vipṛca stha vi mā pāpmanā pṛṅkteti pratyaṅ pratiprasthātā surāgrahaiḥ | [ĀpŚS, 18, 7 1.2]
āhavanīyanyante somagrahair avatiṣṭhante | [ĀpŚS, 18, 7 2.1]
mārjālīyanyante surāgrahaiḥ | [ĀpŚS, 18, 7 2.2]
pracarati somagrahaiḥ | [ĀpŚS, 18, 7 3.1]
vaṣaṭkārānuvaṣaṭkārau surāgrahān anuprakampayanti | [ĀpŚS, 18, 7 4.1]
vyākhyātaḥ somasya bhakṣaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 18, 7 5.1]
virāṭchandasa iti bhakṣamantraṃ namati | [ĀpŚS, 18, 7 6.1]
mārutyā avadānīyāni somagrahāṃś cartvigbhya upaharanti | [ĀpŚS, 18, 7 7.1]
anavadānīyāni surāgrahāṃś ca vājasṛdbhyaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 18, 7 7.2]
tāni dakṣiṇasyāṃ vediśroṇyāṃ vimāthīkṛtya bhakṣayanti | [ĀpŚS, 18, 7 8.1]
kakudo rājaputro dhruvagopo naivāragopo vā prāśnīyāt | [ĀpŚS, 18, 7 9.1]
sarvaṃ vā kakudam upariṣṭāt sarvasomebhyaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 18, 7 9.2]
atra sārasvataprabhṛtīnāṃ daivatena pracarati | [ĀpŚS, 18, 7 10.1]
yajñāraṇye pracarantīti vijñāyate | [ĀpŚS, 18, 7 11.1]
tad yatreṣṭā anūyājā bhavanty avyūḍhāḥ srucaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 18, 7 12.1]
tad etaiḥ pracareyuḥ | [ĀpŚS, 18, 7 12.2]
tad u tathā na kuryāt | [ĀpŚS, 18, 7 12.3]
hvalati vā etad yajño yad evaṃ kurvantīti | [ĀpŚS, 18, 7 12.4]
tasmād yatraiva pūrveṣāṃ vapābhiś careyus tad itareṣām | [ĀpŚS, 18, 7 13.1]
yatro haiva havirbhis taddhavirbhiḥ | [ĀpŚS, 18, 7 13.2]
saṃtiṣṭhate vājapeyaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 18, 7 14.1]
teneṣṭvā sautrāmaṇyā yajeta | [ĀpŚS, 18, 7 15.1]
maitrāvaruṇyā vāmikṣayā | [ĀpŚS, 18, 7 15.2]
yāvajjīvaṃ na kaṃcana pratyavarohet | [ĀpŚS, 18, 7 16.1]

śvetacchattrī ha bhavatīti vijñāyate | [ĀpŚS, 18, 7 18.1]
{ĀpŚS, 18, 8}
rājā svargakāmo rājasūyena yajeta | [ĀpŚS, 18, 8 1.1]
śatasahasraṃ dakṣiṇā | [ĀpŚS, 18, 8 2.1]
agniṣṭomaḥ pañcāpavargaḥ prathamam ahaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 18, 8 3.1]
pañca sahasrāṇi pavitre dadāti | [ĀpŚS, 18, 8 4.1]
triṃśatam abhiṣecanīye | [ĀpŚS, 18, 8 4.2]
triṃśataṃ daśapeye | [ĀpŚS, 18, 8 4.3]
daśa keśavapanīye | [ĀpŚS, 18, 8 4.4]
viṃśatiṃ vyuṣṭidvirātre | [ĀpŚS, 18, 8 4.5]
pañca kṣatrasya dhṛtau | [ĀpŚS, 18, 8 4.6]
api vā catvāry abhiṣecanīye | [ĀpŚS, 18, 8 5.1]
pratisāhasrāṇītarāṇy ahāni | [ĀpŚS, 18, 8 6.1]
ṣaṣṭitrīṇi śatāni sahasrāṇāṃ dadātīti bahvṛcabrāhmaṇaṃ bhavati | [ĀpŚS, 18, 8 7.1]
tathā dakṣiṇā atinayed yathāsyāhāni svakālāni syuḥ | [ĀpŚS, 18, 8 8.1]
śeṣam anudiśati | [ĀpŚS, 18, 8 9.1]
śvo bhūta ānumatādibhir aṣṭābhir anvahaṃ yajate | [ĀpŚS, 18, 8 10.1]
piṃṣann ānumataṃ paścād uttarataś ca vyavaśātayati | [ĀpŚS, 18, 8 11.1]
ye pratyañcaḥ śamyāyā avaśīyante tan nairṛtam ekakapālam | [ĀpŚS, 18, 8 12.1]
ya udañcas tān udaṅ paretya valmīkavapām uddhatyedam aham amuṣyāmuṣyāyaṇasya kṣetriyam avayaja iti śuktyā valmīkavapāyāṃ hutvedam aham amuṣyāmuṣyāyaṇasya kṣetriyam apidadhāmīti tayaiva śuktyā valmīkavapām apidadhyāt | [ĀpŚS, 18, 8 13.1]
valmīkavapayā juhoti valmīkavapayāpidadhātīty eke | [ĀpŚS, 18, 8 14.1]
ānumatam āsādya nairṛtena pracarati | [ĀpŚS, 18, 8 15.1]
vīhi svāheti gārhapatye hutvā dakṣiṇāgner ekolmukaṃ dhūpāyaddharati | [ĀpŚS, 18, 8 16.1]
dakṣiṇam aparam avāntaradeśaṃ gatvā svakṛta iriṇe pradare vopasamādhāyaiṣa te nirṛte bhāga ity aṅguṣṭhābhyāṃ visraṃsikākāṇḍābhyāṃ vā nairṛtaṃ sarvahutaṃ juhoti | [ĀpŚS, 18, 8 17.1]
kṛṣṇaṃ vāsaḥ kṛṣṇatūṣaṃ dakṣiṇā | [ĀpŚS, 18, 8 18.1]
kṛṣṇaṃ vāso bhinnāntam ity eke | [ĀpŚS, 18, 8 19.1]
apratīkṣam āyanti nirṛtyā antarhityā iti vijñāyate | [ĀpŚS, 18, 8 20.1]
{ĀpŚS, 18, 9}
svāhā namo ya idaṃ cakāreti punar etya gārhapatye hutvānumatena pracarati | [ĀpŚS, 18, 9 1.1]
dhenur dakṣiṇā | [ĀpŚS, 18, 9 2.1]
ādityaṃ carum ity etābhir anvaham iṣṭvā cāturmāsyāny ālabhate | [ĀpŚS, 18, 9 3.1]
taiḥ saṃvatsaraṃ yajate | [ĀpŚS, 18, 9 4.1]
na śunāsīrīyaṃ pratisamasyati | [ĀpŚS, 18, 9 5.1]
tataś caturhaviṣendraturīyeṇa yajate | [ĀpŚS, 18, 9 6.1]
āgneyam aṣṭākapālam iti | [ĀpŚS, 18, 9 7.1]
vahinī dhenur dakṣiṇā | [ĀpŚS, 18, 9 8.1]
tayā bhrātṛvyavantaṃ priyaṃ vā yājayet | [ĀpŚS, 18, 9 9.1]
etasyā eva rātrer niśāyāṃ pañcedhmīyena yajate | [ĀpŚS, 18, 9 10.1]
caturdhāhavanīyaṃ pratidiśaṃ vyuddhṛtya madhye pañcamaṃ kṛtvā pṛthag idhmān upasamādhāya juhvāṃ pañcagṛhītaṃ gṛhītvā ye devāḥ puraḥsada ity etair yathāliṅgaṃ juhoti | [ĀpŚS, 18, 9 11.1]
madhye pañcamena | [ĀpŚS, 18, 9 11.2]
samūḍhaṃ rakṣa iti madhya idhmān upasamūhyaikadhopasamādhāyāparaṃ pañcagṛhītaṃ gṛhītvāgnaye rakṣoghne svāhety uttarāḥ pañcāhutīr juhoti | [ĀpŚS, 18, 9 12.1]
praṣṭivāhī ratho dakṣiṇā | [ĀpŚS, 18, 9 13.1]
pañcavāhī vā | [ĀpŚS, 18, 9 13.2]
tena yajeta yo rakṣobhyo bibhīyāt piśācebhyo vā | [ĀpŚS, 18, 9 14.1]
vyuṣṭāyāṃ purāgnihotrād apāmārgahomena caranti | [ĀpŚS, 18, 9 15.1]
apāṃ nyayanād apāmārgān āhṛtya tān saktūn kṛtvā dakṣiṇāgner ekolmukaṃ dhūpāyaddharati | [ĀpŚS, 18, 9 16.1]
uttaram aparam avāntaradeśaṃ gatvā svakṛta iriṇe pradare vopasamādhāya devasya tvety anudrutya rakṣaso vadhaṃ juhomīti parṇamayena sruveṇa juhoti | [ĀpŚS, 18, 9 17.1]
hataṃ rakṣa iti sruvam anuprahṛtyāvadhiṣma rakṣa ity upatiṣṭhate | [ĀpŚS, 18, 9 18.1]
yad vaste tad dakṣiṇā | [ĀpŚS, 18, 9 19.1]
varo vā | [ĀpŚS, 18, 9 19.2]
apratīkṣam āyanti rakṣasām antarhityā iti vijñāyate | [ĀpŚS, 18, 9 20.1]
{ĀpŚS, 18, 10}
agnihotraṃ hutvā devikāhavīṃṣi nirvapati | [ĀpŚS, 18, 10 1.1]
dhātre puroḍāśaṃ dvādaśakapālam iti pañca | [ĀpŚS, 18, 10 2.1]
mithunau gāvau dakṣiṇā | [ĀpŚS, 18, 10 3.1]
paśur apy atropālambhyo dhātre | [ĀpŚS, 18, 10 4.1]
na vā | [ĀpŚS, 18, 10 4.2]
āgnāvaiṣṇavam ekādaśakapālam iti trīṇi havīṃṣi | [ĀpŚS, 18, 10 5.1]
teṣāṃ prathamena grāmakāmo yajeta | [ĀpŚS, 18, 10 6.1]
dvitīyena brahmavarcasakāmaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 18, 10 6.2]
tṛtīyena paśukāmaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 18, 10 6.3]
vīrajananam ity eke | [ĀpŚS, 18, 10 7.1]
vaiśvānaraṃ dvādaśakapālaṃ nirvapati | [ĀpŚS, 18, 10 8.1]
hiraṇyaṃ dakṣiṇā | [ĀpŚS, 18, 10 9.1]
vāruṇaṃ yavamayaṃ sarvataḥ prādeśamātraṃ carum | [ĀpŚS, 18, 10 10.1]
aśvo 'vyuptavaho dakṣiṇā | [ĀpŚS, 18, 10 11.1]
bārhaspatyaṃ carum iti dvādaśānvahaṃ ratnināṃ havīṃṣi | [ĀpŚS, 18, 10 12.1]
yasya gṛhe nirvapati tata iṣṭipariveṣaṇaṃ dakṣiṇā ca | [ĀpŚS, 18, 10 13.1]
bhagāya caruś caturtho vāvātāyai gṛhe | [ĀpŚS, 18, 10 14.1]
vicittagarbhā paṣṭhauhī dakṣiṇā | [ĀpŚS, 18, 10 15.1]

{ĀpŚS, 18, 12}

ahaṃ tad asya manasā śivena somaṃ rājānam iha bhakṣayāmīti vā svayaṃ pibet | [ĀpŚS, 19, 3 6.1]
dve srutī aśṛṇavaṃ pitṝṇām ahaṃ devānām uta martyānām | [ĀpŚS, 19, 3 7.1]
tābhyām idaṃ viśvaṃ bhuvanaṃ samety antarā pūrvam aparaṃ ca ketum iti vā valmīkavapāyām avanayet | [ĀpŚS, 19, 3 7.2]
dakṣiṇe 'gnau śatātṛṇṇāṃ sthālīṃ prabaddhāṃ dhārayati | [ĀpŚS, 19, 3 8.1]
tasyā bila udīcīnadaśaṃ pavitraṃ vitatya yan me manaḥ parāgatam iti tasmiñchatamānaṃ hiraṇyaṃ nidhāya somapratīkāḥ pitaras tṛpṇuteti tasmin surāśeṣam ānayati | [ĀpŚS, 19, 3 9.1]
somapratīkāḥ pitaro madantāṃ vyaśema devahitaṃ yad āyuḥ | [ĀpŚS, 19, 3 9.2]
indrapīto vicakṣaṇo vyaśema devahitaṃ yad āyur iti vā | [ĀpŚS, 19, 3 9.3]
sravantīṃ saumībhiḥ pitṛmatībhis tisṛbhistisṛbhir uttarottarābhir upatiṣṭhante | [ĀpŚS, 19, 3 10.1]
tvaṃ soma pracikita ity etā āmnātā bhavanti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 3 11.1]
purastād adhvaryuḥ | [ĀpŚS, 19, 3 12.1]
dakṣiṇato brahmā | [ĀpŚS, 19, 3 12.2]
paścāddhotā | [ĀpŚS, 19, 3 12.3]
yad agne kavyavāhaneti kāvyavāhanībhir dakṣiṇe 'gnau śatātṛṇṇāṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati yadi brāhmaṇo yajate | [ĀpŚS, 19, 3 13.1]
{ĀpŚS, 19, 4}
atha yadi rājanyo vaiśyo vā nādriyeta dakṣiṇam agniṃ praṇayitum | [ĀpŚS, 19, 4 1.1]
svayam etaṃ surāśeṣaṃ vratayann āsīta | [ĀpŚS, 19, 4 2.1]
bārhaspatyasya paśupuroḍāśena pracarya paśubhiḥ pracarya puroḍāśaiḥ pracarati | [ĀpŚS, 19, 4 3.1]
samānaṃ tu sviṣṭakṛdiḍam | [ĀpŚS, 19, 4 4.1]
agnīd aupayajān aṅgārān āharety etadādi pāśukaṃ karma pratipadyate | [ĀpŚS, 19, 4 5.1]
hṛdayaśūlair māsareṇa pātraiś cāvabhṛtham avayanti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 4 6.1]
māsaram ṛjīṣakalpena pratipādayati | [ĀpŚS, 19, 4 7.1]
balkasaṃ māsara ity ācakṣate | [ĀpŚS, 19, 4 8.1]
yas te deva varuṇa gāyatracchandāḥ pāśas taṃ ta etenāvayaje svāhety āśvinapātram avabhṛthe pravidhyati | [ĀpŚS, 19, 4 9.1]
etenaiva triṣṭupchandā iti sārasvatasya | [ĀpŚS, 19, 4 9.2]
jagatīchandā ity aindrasya | [ĀpŚS, 19, 4 9.3]
anuṣṭupchandā iti sataṃ vālasrāvaṃ śyenapattraṃ ca | [ĀpŚS, 19, 4 9.4]
paṅkticchandā iti śūlān | [ĀpŚS, 19, 4 9.5]
tūṣṇīṃ pratyāyanam | [ĀpŚS, 19, 4 10.1]
tayā somavāminaṃ somātipavitaṃ rājānam aparudhyamānam aparuddham abhiṣicyamānam abhiṣiṣicānaṃ vā yājayet | [ĀpŚS, 19, 4 11.1]
abhicaryamāṇo yajeta | [ĀpŚS, 19, 4 12.1]
abhicarann annādyakāmaḥ prajākāmaḥ paśukāmo vā | [ĀpŚS, 19, 4 12.2]
sarveṣv abhiṣekeṣv āmnātā | [ĀpŚS, 19, 4 13.1]
tayā brāhmaṇo rājanyo vaiśyo vā tejaskāmo yajeta | [ĀpŚS, 19, 4 14.1]
{ĀpŚS, 19, 5}
athātaḥ kaukilīṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 19, 5 1.1]
tasyāḥ pūrvavatkalpaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 19, 5 2.1]
nirvapaṇakāla aindraṃ paśum ālabhate | [ĀpŚS, 19, 5 3.1]
ṛṣabho dakṣiṇā | [ĀpŚS, 19, 5 4.1]
ādityaṃ carum | [ĀpŚS, 19, 5 5.1]
vatsaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 19, 5 6.1]
purastād eva kālāyasena kālānuśātanena kālena tasareṇa pakṣmaṇā vrīhiyavaśyāmākān krītvā kṣaume vāsasy upanaddhān vrīhīṃs tokmāni kurvanti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 5 7.1]
yavān īṣadupataptān | [ĀpŚS, 19, 5 7.2]
cūrṇāni tāni dadhnodaśvitā vā saṃsṛjya darbhaiḥ paritaṃsya nidadhāti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 5 8.1]
sa māsaraḥ | [ĀpŚS, 19, 5 9.1]
teṣām eva sthūlacūrṇāni saṃsrāveṇābhiṣiktāni sa nagnahuḥ | [ĀpŚS, 19, 5 10.1]
śyāmākān saktūn kṛtvā surāyāḥ saṃdhānakāle tokmair māsareṇa nagnahunā ca surāṃ saṃsṛjya saktūnāṃ tṛtīyena parikīrya parīto ṣiñcatā sutam ity ekasyā gor dugdhena pariṣicyāpareṇa tṛtīyena parikīryaitayaiva dvayor dugdhenāpareṇa tṛtīyena parikīryaitayaiva tisṛṇāṃ dugdhena tisro rātrīḥ saṃsṛṣṭā vasati | [ĀpŚS, 19, 5 11.1]
{ĀpŚS, 19, 6}
avaṭasthāne kārotaram eke samāmananti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 6 1.1]
vaidalaś carmanaddho bhavati | [ĀpŚS, 19, 6 2.1]
tasmin vaidalaṃ śuṇḍāmukham avadadhāti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 6 3.1]
tasya bilaṃ carmaṇā pariṇaddhaṃ bhavati | [ĀpŚS, 19, 6 4.1]
tasmin yad āsravati sā parisrud bhavati | [ĀpŚS, 19, 6 5.1]
pātrasaṃsādanakāle 'śvibhyāṃ sarasvatyā indrāya sutrāmṇe trīṇi pātrāṇi prayunakti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 6 6.1]
trayān saktūn yavagodhūmānām upavākāsaktūṃś ca śyenapattre vāle droṇe vā | [ĀpŚS, 19, 6 7.1]
ajāvilomnām adhvaryoḥ pavitraṃ bhavati | [ĀpŚS, 19, 6 8.1]
goaśvānāṃ pratiprasthātuḥ | [ĀpŚS, 19, 6 8.2]
ājyaṃ nirupyādhvaryudroṇe prabhūtaṃ payo nirvapati | [ĀpŚS, 19, 6 9.1]
mantravad ity āśmarathyaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 19, 6 10.1]
tūṣṇīm ity ālekhanaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 19, 6 10.2]
ājyam utpūya vālena paya utpunāti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 6 11.1]
prāṅ somo atidruta iti somavāminaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 19, 6 12.1]
pratyaṅ somo atidruta iti somātipavitasya | [ĀpŚS, 19, 6 12.2]
brahma kṣatraṃ pavata iti surāṃ pratiprasthātā | [ĀpŚS, 19, 6 13.1]
pāśukāny ājyāni gṛhītvādhvaryuḥ payograhān gṛhṇāti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 6 14.1]
kuvid aṅgeti sarveṣām ekā purorug ekā puronuvākyaikaḥ praiṣa ekā yājyā | [ĀpŚS, 19, 6 15.1]
{ĀpŚS, 19, 7}
upayāmagṛhīto 'sy aśvibhyāṃ tvā juṣṭaṃ gṛhṇāmīti gṛhītvā yavasaktubhiḥ śrītvā pavitreṇa parimṛjyaiṣa te yonis tejase tveti sādayitvopayāmagṛhīto 'si sarasvatyai tvā juṣṭaṃ gṛhṇāmīti gṛhītvā godhūmasaktubhiḥ śrītvā pavitreṇa parimṛjyaiṣa te yonir vīryāya tveti sādayitvopayāmagṛhīto 'sīndrāya tvā sutrāmṇe juṣṭaṃ gṛhṇāmīti gṛhītvopavākāsaktubhiḥ śrītvā pavitreṇa parimṛjyaiṣa te yonir balāya tveti sādayitvottarair yathāliṅgam upatiṣṭhate | [ĀpŚS, 19, 7 1.1]
surāyāṃ vāla ānīyamānāyāṃ dhārāyāḥ pratiprasthātā surāgrahān gṛhṇāti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 7 2.1]
nānā hi vāṃ devahitaṃ sadaḥ kṛtam iti sarveṣām ekā purorug ekā puronuvākyaikaḥ praiṣa ekā yājyā | [ĀpŚS, 19, 7 3.1]
upayāmagṛhīto 'sy āśvinaṃ tejo 'śvibhyāṃ tvā juṣṭaṃ gṛhṇāmīti gṛhītvā pavitreṇa parimṛjyaiṣa te yonir modāya tveti sādayati | [ĀpŚS, 19, 7 4.1]
upayāmagṛhīto 'si sārasvataṃ vīryaṃ sarasvatyai tvā juṣṭaṃ gṛhṇāmīti gṛhītvā pavitreṇa parimṛjyaiṣa te yonir ānandāya tveti sādayati | [ĀpŚS, 19, 7 5.1]
upayāmagṛhīto 'sy aindraṃ balam indrāya tvā sutrāmṇe juṣṭaṃ gṛhṇāmīti gṛhītvā pavitreṇa parimṛjyaiṣa te yonir mahase tveti sādayati | [ĀpŚS, 19, 7 6.1]
surāvac chrayaṇāni | [ĀpŚS, 19, 7 7.1]
sannān anuvākaśeṣeṇādhvaryur yajamānaś copatiṣṭhate | [ĀpŚS, 19, 7 8.1]
uttareṇa cānuvākena | [ĀpŚS, 19, 7 8.2]
{ĀpŚS, 19, 8}
pūrvavat paśūn upākaroti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 8 1.1]
bārhaspatyavarjaṃ samānam ā paryagnikaraṇāt | [ĀpŚS, 19, 8 2.1]
madhyame paryagnikaraṇaparyāya ulmukaikadeśaṃ khare nyupyopasamādadhāti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 8 3.1]
śeṣeṇa paryagnikṛtvaitad eva paśuśrapaṇārthaṃ praṇayati | [ĀpŚS, 19, 8 4.1]
hutāsu vapāsu catvāriṃśad gā dakṣiṇā dadāti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 8 5.1]
anuśiśuṃ ca vaḍabām | [ĀpŚS, 19, 8 5.2]
atra vā grahān gṛhṇīyuḥ | [ĀpŚS, 19, 8 6.1]
uktaḥ saṃpraiṣaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 19, 8 7.1]
sarva āhavanīye hūyerann ity āśmarathyaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 19, 8 8.1]
dakṣiṇe 'gnau surāgrahā ity ālekhanaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 19, 8 8.2]
surāvantam iti payograhāñ juhoti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 8 9.1]
yas te rasaḥ saṃbhṛta iti surāgrahān | [ĀpŚS, 19, 8 9.2]
tūṣṇīm anuvaṣaṭkṛte hutvā yam aśvinā namucer ity āśvinam adhvaryur bhakṣayati | [ĀpŚS, 19, 8 10.1]
yad atra riptam iti sārasvataṃ pratiprasthātāgnīdhraś ca | [ĀpŚS, 19, 8 11.1]
idaṃ havir ity aindraṃ brahmā yajamānaś ca | [ĀpŚS, 19, 8 12.1]
vyākhyātā surāyāḥ pratipattiḥ | [ĀpŚS, 19, 8 13.1]
dakṣiṇenāhavanīyaṃ payaḥśeṣaṃ pitṛpitāmahaprapitāmahebhyo dadāti pitṛbhyaḥ svadhāvibhyaḥ svadhā nama iti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 8 14.1]
punantu mā pitaraḥ somyāsa ity upatiṣṭhate | [ĀpŚS, 19, 8 15.1]
{ĀpŚS, 19, 9}
athāhutī juhutaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 19, 9 1.1]
ye samānā ity adhvaryuḥ | [ĀpŚS, 19, 9 1.2]
ye sajātā iti pratiprasthātā | [ĀpŚS, 19, 9 1.3]
manotākāle pṛthak pātreṣu paśūnāṃ yūṣāṇi nidadhāti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 9 2.1]
purastātsviṣṭakṛtaḥ śṛṅgaśaphair upahomāñ juhoti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 9 3.1]
aṣṭāvaṣṭāv ekaikasya kuṣṭhikāśaphāḥ | [ĀpŚS, 19, 9 4.1]
āśvinasya yūṣeṇa kuṣṭhikāṃ śaphaṃ ca pūrayitvā sīsena tantram ity aṣṭarcena pratimantraṃ dvābhyāṃ dvābhyāṃ kuṣṭhikāśaphābhyāṃ juhoti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 9 5.1]
uttamāyāṃ śṛṅge anuṣajati | [ĀpŚS, 19, 9 6.1]
hutvā hutvā sveṣv abhiṣecanapātreṣu saṃpātān avanīyāhavanīye kuṣṭhikāśaphān pravidhyati | [ĀpŚS, 19, 9 7.1]
evam uttareṇāṣṭarcena sārasvatasya | [ĀpŚS, 19, 9 8.1]
sarveṇānuvākenaindrasya | [ĀpŚS, 19, 9 9.1]
audumbary āsandy aratnimātraśīrṣaṇyānūcyā nābhidaghnapādā mauñjavivānā | [ĀpŚS, 19, 9 10.1]
mitro 'si varuṇo 'sīti tāṃ yajamānāyatane pratiṣṭhāpayati | [ĀpŚS, 19, 9 11.1]
āsādanopaveśanābhimantraṇāni rājasūyavat | [ĀpŚS, 19, 9 12.1]
tasyāṃ prāṅmukham āsīnaṃ pratyaṅmukhas tiṣṭhann āśvinasaṃpātair abhiṣiñcati devasya tvā savituḥ prasave 'śvinor bāhubhyāṃ pūṣṇo hastābhyām aśvinor bhaiṣajyena tejase brahmavarcasāyābhiṣiñcāmīti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 9 13.1]
evam uttareṇa mantreṇa sārasvatasya | [ĀpŚS, 19, 9 14.1]
uttamenaindrasya | [ĀpŚS, 19, 9 15.1]
{ĀpŚS, 19, 10}
ko 'si katamo 'sīti pāṇī saṃmṛśyādhvaryur vyāhṛtīr juhoti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 10 1.1]
atra rājasūyavan maṅgalyanāmna āhūya śiro me śrīr iti yathāliṅgam aṅgāni saṃmṛśya jaṅghābhyāṃ padbhyām iti pratyavaruhya prati kṣatre pratitiṣṭhāmi rāṣṭra iti japitvā trayā devā ity āhutīr hutvā lomāni prayatir mameti yathāliṅgam aṅgāni saṃmṛśate | [ĀpŚS, 19, 10 2.1]
sviṣṭakṛtprabhṛti samānam āvabhṛthāt | [ĀpŚS, 19, 10 3.1]
yad devā devaheḍanam ity avabhṛthe pañcāhutīr juhotīty āśmarathyaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 19, 10 4.1]
āhavanīye hūyerann ity ālekhanaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 19, 10 4.2]
avabhṛtha nicaṅkaṇety avabhṛthaṃ yajamāno 'bhimantrya sumitrā na āpo drupadād iven mumucāna ity āplutyodvayaṃ tamasas parīty ādityam upasthāya pratiyuto varuṇasya pāśa ity udakāntaṃ pratyasyati | [ĀpŚS, 19, 10 5.1]
paśuvat samidha upasthānaṃ ca | [ĀpŚS, 19, 10 6.1]
samāvavartīty upasthāya bhūḥ svāhety āhutiṃ hutvā pūrvavat pitṛyajñaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 19, 10 7.1]
indrāya vayodhase paśum ālabhate | [ĀpŚS, 19, 10 8.1]
ṛṣabho dakṣiṇā | [ĀpŚS, 19, 10 9.1]
ādityaṃ carum | [ĀpŚS, 19, 10 10.1]
dhenuḥ | [ĀpŚS, 19, 10 11.1]
vijñāyate ca | [ĀpŚS, 19, 10 12.1]
vatsaṃ pūrvasyāṃ dadāti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 10 12.2]
mātaram uttarasyām | [ĀpŚS, 19, 10 12.3]
saṃtiṣṭhate kaukilī | [ĀpŚS, 19, 10 13.1]
tayā svargakāmo yajeta | [ĀpŚS, 19, 10 14.1]
{ĀpŚS, 19, 11}
sāvitraṃ svargakāmaś cinvīta | [ĀpŚS, 19, 11 1.1]
paśubandhe cīyate | [ĀpŚS, 19, 11 2.1]
ceṣyamāṇa upakalpayate pañcāśītiśataṃ hiraṇyeṣṭakā yāvad uttamam aṅguliparu tāvatīḥ śarkarā vābhyaktāś catasraḥ svayamātṛṇṇā aparimitā lokaṃpṛṇāḥ | [ĀpŚS, 19, 11 3.1]
ṣaḍḍhotāram ity etadādi pāśukaṃ karma pratipadyate | [ĀpŚS, 19, 11 4.1]
veditṛtīye yajata iti vijñāyate | [ĀpŚS, 19, 11 5.1]
prāg uttarāt parigrāhāt kṛtvottaravedideśasya madhye śaṅkuṃ nihatya sarvataḥ parimaṇḍalaṃ rathacakramātraṃ sāvitraṃ parilikhya samūlaṃ haritaṃ darbhastambam āhṛtya madhye 'gner nikhāya juhvāṃ pañcagṛhītaṃ gṛhītvā sajūr abdo 'yāvabhir iti darbhastambe pañcāhutīr hutvoddhatyāvokṣya vyāghāraṇāntām uttaravediṃ kṛtvā lekhāyā abhyantaraṃ nava parimaṇḍalā lekhā likhitvā sikatābhir avakīrya darbhaiḥ pracchādya dadhnā madhumiśreṇa śarkarābhir iti bāhyāṃ lekhāṃ sampūrya vasati | [ĀpŚS, 19, 11 6.1]
hute prātar agnihotre prajāpatis tvā sādayatu tayā devatayāṅgirasvad dhruvā sīdety uttaravedim abhimṛśya mayi gṛhṇāmy agre agniṃ yo no agniḥ pitara iti dvābhyām ātmann agniṃ gṛhītvā yās te agne samidha iti svayaṃcityābhimṛśyāgner bhasmāsīti sikatā nivapati | [ĀpŚS, 19, 11 7.1]
saṃjñānam ity ūṣān | [ĀpŚS, 19, 11 7.2]
tān nivapan yad adaś candramasi kṛṣṇaṃ tad ihāstv iti manasā dhyāyati | [ĀpŚS, 19, 11 8.1]
saṃ yā vaḥ priyās tanuva ity ūṣān sikatāś ca saṃsṛjya cita stha paricita ity aparimitābhiḥ śarkarābhiḥ pariśrityāpyāyasva sametu ta iti sikatā vyūhati | [ĀpŚS, 19, 11 9.1]
na lekhāḥ saṃlobhayanti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 11 10.1]
abhyantaraṃ jaghanārdha udapātram upadadhāti vāk tvā samudra upadadhe suprajāvaniṃ rāyaspoṣavaniṃ mahyaṃ vājināyeti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 11 11.1]
{ĀpŚS, 19, 12}
navamyāṃ bāhyāyāṃ lekhāyāṃ pañcadaśa pūrvapakṣasyāhāny upadadhāti saṃjñānaṃ vijñānam iti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 12 1.1]
teṣām antarāleṣv eteṣām ahnāṃ pañcadaśa muhūrtān upadadhāti citraḥ ketur iti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 12 2.1]
athāntarasyāṃ pañcadaśa pūrvapakṣasya rātrīr upadadhāti darśā dṛṣṭeti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 12 3.1]
tāsām antarāleṣv etāsāṃ rātrīṇāṃ pañcadaśa muhūrtān upadadhāti dātā pradāteti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 12 4.1]
athāntarasyāṃ pañcadaśāparapakṣasyāhāny upadadhāti prastutaṃ viṣṭutam iti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 12 5.1]
teṣām antarāleṣv eteṣām ahnāṃ pañcadaśa muhūrtān upadadhāti savitā prasaviteti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 12 6.1]
athāntarasyāṃ pañcadaśāparapakṣasya rātrīr upadadhāti sutā sunvatīti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 12 7.1]
tāsām antarāleṣv etāsāṃ rātrīṇāṃ pañcadaśa muhūrtān upadadhāty abhiśāstānumanteti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 12 8.1]
athāntarasyāṃ dvādaśa pūrvapakṣān upadadhāti pavitraṃ pavayiṣyann iti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 12 9.1]
athāntarasyāṃ dvādaśāparapakṣān upadadhāti sahasvān sahīyān iti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 12 10.1]
athāntarasyāṃ trayodaśa māsanāmāny upadadhāty aruṇo 'ruṇarajā iti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 12 11.1]
atha sikatā upadadhāty ejatkā jovatkā iti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 12 12.1]
athāntarasyāṃ pañcadaśa muhūrtān upadadhātīdānīṃ tadānīm iti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 12 13.1]

atha nābhyāṃ catvāri saṃvatsaranāmāny upadadhāti prajāpatiḥ saṃvatsaro mahān ka iti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 12 15.1]
catasraḥ svayamātṛṇṇā dikṣūpadadhāti bhūr agniṃ ca pṛthivīṃ ca māṃ ceti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 12 16.1]

sā citir bhavati | [ĀpŚS, 19, 12 19.1]
ārohaṇaṃ japati | [ĀpŚS, 19, 12 20.1]
avarohaṇaṃ japati | [ĀpŚS, 19, 12 20.2]

sāhasravat karoti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 12 22.1]
dhenūḥ kṛtvā yajamānaḥ saṃhāravihārābhyām upatiṣṭhate saṃvatsaro 'si parivatsaro 'sīti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 12 23.1]
uttarata uttamāyām iṣṭakāyām arkaparṇenājākṣīraṃ juhoti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 12 24.1]
tvam agne rudra iti śatarudrīyasya rūpam asaṃcare paśūnām arkaparṇa udasyati valmīkavapāyāṃ vāvadadhāti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 12 25.1]

{ĀpŚS, 19, 13}

{ĀpŚS, 19, 14}
etena nāciketo vyākhyātaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 19, 14 1.1]
nātra lekhā bhavanti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 14 2.1]

sa yadīcchet tejasvī yaśasvī brahmavarcasī syām iti prāg dakṣiṇebhyaḥ prāṅ ā hotur dhiṣṇyād utsarped yeyaṃ prāgād yaśasvatī sā mā prorṇotu tejasā yaśasā brahmavarcaseneti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 14 13.1]
atha yadīcched bhūyiṣṭhaṃ me śraddadhīran bhūyiṣṭhā dakṣiṇā nayeyur iti dakṣiṇāsu nīyamānāsu prācy ehi prācy ehīti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 14 14.1]

saṃtiṣṭhate nāciketaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 19, 14 17.1]
etena cāturhotro vyākhyātaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 19, 14 18.1]
yāvatpadaṃ hiraṇyeṣṭakāḥ śarkarā vābhyaktāḥ | [ĀpŚS, 19, 14 19.1]

hṛdayaṃ grahaṃ catvāri padāni saṃbhārāṇāṃ dve patnīnām | [ĀpŚS, 19, 14 20.2]
evaṃ dakṣiṇataḥ prāñcaṃ caturhotāram | [ĀpŚS, 19, 14 21.1]
paścād udañcaṃ pañcahotāram | [ĀpŚS, 19, 14 22.1]

{ĀpŚS, 19, 16}

{ĀpŚS, 19, 17}

{ĀpŚS, 19, 19}
ādityaṃ caruṃ nirvapet saṃgrāmam upaprayāsyan | [ĀpŚS, 19, 19 1.1]

balbajān apīdhme saṃnahyet | [ĀpŚS, 19, 19 4.1]

ardham idhmasyābhyādadhyāt | [ĀpŚS, 19, 19 11.2]
aindram ekādaśakapālaṃ nirvapen mārutaṃ saptakapālaṃ grāmakāmaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 19, 19 12.1]

indraṃ yajety aindrī yājyā | [ĀpŚS, 19, 19 15.4]

bhareṣv indram iti yājyānuvākye bhavataḥ | [ĀpŚS, 19, 19 19.1]
{ĀpŚS, 19, 20}
upādhāyyapūrvayaṃ vāso dakṣiṇā | [ĀpŚS, 19, 20 1.1]
citrāntam ity arthaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 19, 20 2.1]
saṃjñānīṃ pṛthaṅ nirupya sarvataḥ samavadāya sarvā devatā anudrutya saṃpreṣyati | [ĀpŚS, 19, 20 3.1]
agniḥ prathamo vasubhir iti sarvadevatye yājyānuvākye bhavataḥ | [ĀpŚS, 19, 20 4.1]

ye śuklāḥ syus tam ādityaṃ caruṃ nirvapet | [ĀpŚS, 19, 20 9.1]

iha mana ity urasi śeṣaṃ ninayati | [ĀpŚS, 19, 20 12.1]
siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate | [ĀpŚS, 19, 20 13.1]
yadi nāvagacched imam aham ādityebhyo bhāgaṃ nirvapāmy āmuṣmād amuṣyai viśo 'vagantor ity aparoddhur nāma gṛhṇīyāt tasyai ca viśaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 19, 20 14.1]
yadi nāvagacched āśvatthān mayūkhān sapta madhyameṣāyām upahanyād idam aham ādityān badhnāmy āmuṣmād amuṣyai viśo 'vagantor iti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 20 15.1]
trīn prācaś catura udīcaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 19, 20 15.2]
yadi nāvagacched etam evādityaṃ caruṃ nirvapet | [ĀpŚS, 19, 20 16.1]
idhme 'pi mayūkhān saṃnahyet | [ĀpŚS, 19, 20 17.1]
tān sahedhmenābhyādadhyāt | [ĀpŚS, 19, 20 18.1]

siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate | [ĀpŚS, 19, 20 20.1]
{ĀpŚS, 19, 21}

{ĀpŚS, 19, 22}
prathamaṃ puroḍāśam adhiśritya paritapanāntaṃ kṛtvā tasminn uttaraṃ jyāyāṃsam adhiśritya tadantam eva kṛtvā tasminn uttaraṃ jyāyāṃsam adhiśrayati | [ĀpŚS, 19, 22 1.1]
pracaraṇakāle dakṣiṇārdhāt prathamāṃ devatāṃ yajet | [ĀpŚS, 19, 22 2.1]
madhyād dvitīyām | [ĀpŚS, 19, 22 2.2]
uttarārdhāt tṛtīyām | [ĀpŚS, 19, 22 2.3]
sarveṣām abhigamayann avadyatīty uktam | [ĀpŚS, 19, 22 3.1]

madhyamām anūcyottamayā yajet | [ĀpŚS, 19, 22 5.2]
uttamām anūcya prathamayā yajet | [ĀpŚS, 19, 22 5.3]
evaṃ sarvā yājyāḥ puronuvākyāś ca bhavanti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 22 6.1]
sarvapṛṣṭhāṃ nirvapati | [ĀpŚS, 19, 22 7.1]
yad indrāya rāthaṃtarāyeti yathāsamāmnātaṃ dvādaśasūttāneṣu kapāleṣv adhiśrayati | [ĀpŚS, 19, 22 8.1]
pracaraṇakāle pūrvārdhāt prathamāṃ devatāṃ yajati | [ĀpŚS, 19, 22 9.1]
evam itarāḥ pradakṣiṇam uttarāpavargam | [ĀpŚS, 19, 22 10.1]
samantaṃ paryavadyatīty uktam | [ĀpŚS, 19, 22 11.1]
abhi tvā śūra nonuma iti ṣaḍ ṛco vyatyāsam anvāha | [ĀpŚS, 19, 22 12.1]
na bṛhatyā vaṣaṭkuryāt | [ĀpŚS, 19, 22 13.1]
anuvākyāyāś catvāry akṣarāṇi yājyāṃ gamayet | [ĀpŚS, 19, 22 14.1]
anuṣṭubhaṃ ca ha vā etat sampādayanti paṅktiṃ ceti te manyāmahe | [ĀpŚS, 19, 22 15.1]
abhi tvā śūra nonumo 'dugdhā iva dhenavaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 19, 22 16.1]
īśānam asya jagataḥ suvardṛśam īśānam om ity anūcya ndratasthuṣas tvām iddhi havāmaha iti yajet | [ĀpŚS, 19, 22 16.2]
{ĀpŚS, 19, 23}
tvām iddhi havāmahe sātā vājasya kāravaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 19, 23 1.1]
tvāṃ vṛtreṣv indra satpatiṃ naras tvāṃ kāṣṭhom ity anūcya svarvato 'bhi tvā śūra nonuma iti yajet | [ĀpŚS, 19, 23 1.2]
kadācana starīr asīty āsāṃ caturthīṃ dadhāti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 23 2.1]
agnaye bhrājasvate puroḍāśam aṣṭākapālam ity uktam | [ĀpŚS, 19, 23 3.1]

yo jyog āmayāvī syād yo vā kāmayeta sarvam āyur iyām iti tasmā etām iṣṭiṃ nirvapet | [ĀpŚS, 19, 23 10.1]
āgneyādīni pañca | [ĀpŚS, 19, 23 10.2]
pātrasaṃsādanakāle khādiraṃ pātraṃ catuḥsrakti prayunakti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 23 11.1]
sauvarṇaṃ ca pravartaṃ śatamānasya kṛtam | [ĀpŚS, 19, 23 11.2]
atho khalu yāvatīḥ samā eṣyan manyeta tāvanmānaṃ syāt | [ĀpŚS, 19, 23 12.1]
yan navam ait tan navanītam abhavad ity ājyam avekṣyājyagrahaṇakāle tūṣṇīṃ khādire caturgṛhītaṃ gṛhītvā sādanakāla uttareṇa dhruvāṃ khādiraṃ sādayitvā tasmin pravartam avadadhāti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 23 13.1]
{ĀpŚS, 19, 24}

yat khādira ājyaṃ tad agreṇāhavanīyaṃ paryāhṛtya dakṣiṇasyāṃ vediśroṇyāṃ sādayati | [ĀpŚS, 19, 24 3]
tad yajamāno 'vekṣate ghṛtasya dhārām amṛtasya panthām iti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 24 4]

atha yajamāno hiraṇyād ghṛtaṃ niṣpibati | [ĀpŚS, 19, 24 7]

uddhṛtya hiraṇyaṃ prakṣālyāyuṣ ṭe viśvato dadhad iti yajamānāya prayacchati | [ĀpŚS, 19, 24 9]
tad yajamāna ācamya pratigṛhya pradakṣiṇaṃ dakṣiṇe karṇa ābadhnāty āyur asi viśvāyur asi sarvāyur asi sarvam āyur asi sarvaṃ ma āyur bhūyāt sarvam āyur geṣam iti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 24 10]
agnir āyuṣmān ity anuvākaśeṣeṇāsyādhvaryur dakṣiṇaṃ hastaṃ gṛhṇāti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 24 11]
siddham iṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate | [ĀpŚS, 19, 24 12]
{ĀpŚS, 19, 25}
aindrāvaruṇaṃ puroḍāśaṃ nirupyaindrāvaruṇīṃ payasyāṃ nirvapet | [ĀpŚS, 19, 25 1.1]
udvāsyālaṃkṛtya payasyāyāṃ puroḍāśam avadadhāti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 25 2.1]

āgneyādīni sapta | [ĀpŚS, 19, 25 14.2]
agne gobhir na ā gahīty upahomāḥ | [ĀpŚS, 19, 25 15.1]

agnīn anvādhāyāpareṇāhavanīyaṃ dakṣiṇātikramyopaviśya yajamāno mārutam asi marutām oja iti kṛṣṇaṃ vāsaḥ kṛṣṇatūṣaṃ paridhatte | [ĀpŚS, 19, 25 17.1]

{ĀpŚS, 19, 26}
purovāto varṣann ity aṣṭau vātanāmāni hutvāntarvedi kṛṣṇājinaṃ prācīnagrīvam uttaralomāstīrya tasmin kharjūrasaktūn karīrasaktūn vā māndā vāśā iti kṛṣṇamadhuṣā saṃyutya tisraḥ piṇḍīḥ kṛtvā puṣkarapalāśaiḥ saṃveṣṭya samudyamya kṛṣṇājinasyāntān vṛṣṇo aśvasya saṃdānam asīti kṛṣṇena dāmnopanahyati | [ĀpŚS, 19, 26 1]

chadīṃṣīty arthaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 19, 26 3]

ahorātrāv āsaktaṃ bhavati | [ĀpŚS, 19, 26 5]
yadi varṣet piṇḍīr eva juhuyāt | [ĀpŚS, 19, 26 6]
yadi na varṣed devāḥ śarmaṇyā iti madhyamāyām ābadhnīyāt | [ĀpŚS, 19, 26 7]
ahorātrāv āsaktaṃ bhavati | [ĀpŚS, 19, 26 8]
yadi varṣet piṇḍīr eva juhuyāt | [ĀpŚS, 19, 26 9]
yadi na varṣed devāḥ sapītaya iti jaghanyāyām ābadhnīyāt | [ĀpŚS, 19, 26 10]
ahorātrāv āsaktaṃ bhavati | [ĀpŚS, 19, 26 11]
yadi varṣet piṇḍīr eva juhuyāt | [ĀpŚS, 19, 26 12]
yadi na varṣec chvo bhūte dhāmacchadādīni trīṇi havīṃṣi nirvapati kṛṣṇānāṃ vrīhīṇām | [ĀpŚS, 19, 26 13]
tāny āsādyotkare kṛṣṇājinam āsādayati | [ĀpŚS, 19, 26 14]
kṛṣṇoṣṇīṣāḥ kṛṣṇavasanā nivītā ṛtvijaḥ pracaranti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 26 15]
tvaṃ tyā cid acyuteti yājyānuvākyāḥ | [ĀpŚS, 19, 26 16]

juhotīty eke | [ĀpŚS, 19, 26 18]
athāsāṃ dhūmam anumantrayate | [ĀpŚS, 19, 26 19]
{ĀpŚS, 19, 27}
asitavarṇā harayaḥ suparṇā iti | [ĀpŚS, 19, 27 1.1]

yadi bhidyeta varṣiṣyatīti vidyāt | [ĀpŚS, 19, 27 3.1]
anasa upastambhane śaṅkau vā kṛṣṇāvir baddhā bhavati | [ĀpŚS, 19, 27 4.1]
abjā asīti tāṃ prokṣati | [ĀpŚS, 19, 27 5.1]

{ĀpŚS, 20, 18}

{ĀpŚS, 20, 20}

sarvaṃ vaiśvadevam | [ĀpŚS, 20, 25 9.2]
āśvamedhikaṃ madhyamaṃ pañcamam ahaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 20, 25 10.1]
tasminn aśvaṃ medhyam ālabhate | [ĀpŚS, 20, 25 10.2]
pauruṣamedhikaṃ madhyamaṃ ṣaṣṭham | [ĀpŚS, 20, 25 11.1]
tasmin puruṣān | [ĀpŚS, 20, 25 11.2]
aptoryāmaḥ saptamaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 20, 25 12.1]
tasmin sarvān medhyān ālabhate | [ĀpŚS, 20, 25 12.2]
vapā vapāvatāṃ juhoti | [ĀpŚS, 20, 25 13.1]
tvaca utkṛtyāvapānām | [ĀpŚS, 20, 25 13.2]
śuṣkān ārdrāṃś cauṣadhivanaspatīn saṃvṛścyāhavanīye 'nuprakiranti | [ĀpŚS, 20, 25 14.1]
prātaḥsavane sanneṣu nārāśaṃseṣv annamannaṃ juhoti | [ĀpŚS, 20, 25 15.1]
sarvasyāptyai sarvasyāvaruddhyā iti vijñāyate | [ĀpŚS, 20, 25 16.1]
evaṃ mādhyaṃdine tṛtīyasavane ca | [ĀpŚS, 20, 25 17.1]
aṣṭamaṃ triṇavam | [ĀpŚS, 20, 25 18.1]
navamaṃ trayastriṃśam | [ĀpŚS, 20, 25 19.1]
viśvajit sarvapṛṣṭho 'tirātro daśamam ahaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 20, 25 20.1]
dakṣiṇākāle yad abrāhmaṇānāṃ dikṣu vittaṃ tat sabhūmi sapuruṣaṃ dadāti yathāśvamedhe yathāśvamedhe | [ĀpŚS, 20, 25 21.1]
{ĀpŚS, 22, 25}
atha savānāṃ vyākhyāto bṛhaspatisavaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 22, 25 1]
vaiśyaḥ puṣṭikāmaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 22, 25 2]
āgneyādīni sapta havīṃṣi nirvapati | [ĀpŚS, 22, 25 3]
pṛśniḥ paṣṭhauhī māruty ālabhyate | [ĀpŚS, 22, 25 4]
tasyāḥ purastāt sviṣṭakṛto yajamānāyatana ṛṣabhacarma prācīnagrīvam uttaralomāstīrya tasminn āsīnaṃ yajamānaṃ dadhnābhiṣiñcati | [ĀpŚS, 22, 25 5]
brāhmaṇo brahmavarcasakāmaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 22, 25 6]
āgneyādīny aṣṭau havīṃṣi nirvapati | [ĀpŚS, 22, 25 7]
purastāt sviṣṭakṛto hiraṇyena ghṛtam utpūya tena kṛṣṇājina āsīnam abhiṣiñcati | [ĀpŚS, 22, 25 8]
atha somasavaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 22, 25 9]
yat kiṃca rājasūyam ṛte somaṃ tat sarvaṃ bhavati | [ĀpŚS, 22, 25 10]
maitrābārhaspatyaṃ saṃsthāpya saumīṃ sūtavaśām ālabhate | [ĀpŚS, 22, 25 11]
tasyāḥ purastāt sviṣṭakṛto 'ṣāḍhaṃ yutsu pṛtanāsu paprim iti saumyarcādbhir abhiṣiñcati | [ĀpŚS, 22, 25 12]
śeṣaṃ saṃsthāpya saṃsṛpāṃ havirbhir diśām aveṣṭyā dvipaśunā paśubandhena sātyadūtānāṃ havirbhiḥ prayujām iti yajate | [ĀpŚS, 22, 25 13]
pṛthisavena paśukāmaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 22, 25 14]
yat kiṃca rājasūyam anuttaravedikaṃ tat sarvaṃ bhavati | [ĀpŚS, 22, 25 15]
maitrābārhaspatyasya purastāt sviṣṭakṛto ye me pañcāśatam iti nārāśaṃsyarcādbhir abhiṣiñcati | [ĀpŚS, 22, 25 16]
samānam uttaraṃ pūrveṇa paśubandhavarjam | [ĀpŚS, 22, 25 17]
vyākhyāto gosavaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 22, 25 18]
odanasavenānnādyakāmaḥ | [ĀpŚS, 22, 25 19]
rohiṇyāṃ yajatopavyuṣaṃ śrapayati | [ĀpŚS, 22, 25 20]
darvihomo bhavati | [ĀpŚS, 22, 25 21]
udita āditye siṃhe vyāghra iti catasra āhutīr odanāddhutvā rāḍ asi virāḍ asīty etaiḥ pratimantram | [ĀpŚS, 22, 25 22]
